LEE-01 船讯 / A Message Delivered

当第一条告诫在贝壳上显现的时候，我们抵达了别处、岛和永恒的土地。
When the first proverb appears on the shell, we reach the shores of elsewhere—the island, the upturned palm of Mother Sea.

小船儿哟，停泊在沙儿上
The once drifting boat now beds itself in the golden sand.

当第二条告诫在贝壳上显现的时候，我们生起熊熊篝火。
When the second proverb appears on the shell, we kindle the fire—the crackling warmth, the spark of hope.

欢乐的人们哟，日日年年
The joyful people are long blessed as one.

当第三条告诫在贝壳上显现的时候，我们习得海的慷慨。
When the third proverb appears on the shell, we accept the sea's gift—the rolling waves, the plentiful fish.

纯洁的海风哟，映照我身
The cool sea breeze cradles us.

当第四条告诫在贝壳上显现的时候，我们承受煎熬、绳索与思念的盐。
When the fourth proverb appears on the shell, we face the test—the salty tears, the longing gaze.

海的那边哟，不是家园
Beyond the sea, I find no home.

图图石子、卡穆塔：不是家园

卡穆塔：我们的祷告结束了。做得很好，图图石子。
Kamuta: You did well today, Tutu.

图图石子：为了庆祝几个月前顺利结束的船商贸易节，大家都准备了许多，我也只是在做我的工作～
Fatutu: Thank you, Kamuta! I was just playing my part in celebrating the success of the trade season. Nothing special, really.

图图石子：只是……
有什么事情比我们的篝火晚会更加重要呢？
Fatutu: But what are we doing here? What could be more important than the celebration?

图图石子：哥哥，你可从来没在这个时候偷偷溜出来过呀～
Fatutu: I've never seen you sneak off on a bonfire night before.

卡穆塔：……
Kamuta: ...

卡穆塔：我希望你能带领朋友们一起修好那艘废弃的船。
Kamuta: Tutu, do you think you and your friends could fix up that old ship?

卡穆塔：托阿、塞洛尼，还有其他的朋友们，你总能得到他们编好的第一串花环……大家一定都很乐意为你搭把手。
Kamuta: I know you're close with Toa, Selone, and the rest. They always make sure their first fous go to you. I'm sure they'd be happy to lend you a hand.

卡穆塔：老人们也不止一次地夸赞你，希望在自己死后将他们的“象形贝壳”传承给你。你能说服他们的，对不对？
Kamuta: And the elders like you, too. I've heard many of them say they'll leave their Spirit Shells to you. So you can win their support, too, right?

图图石子：等一等，哥哥。你说的是……修理“丰收满满号”？
Fatutu: Woah! Slow down, big chief! Are you saying you want to fix up the Quick Spear?

卡穆塔：……是的。
Kamuta: Hm! Yeah.

图图石子：可它明明已经损坏很久了。我不明白，哥哥……我们为什么突然就得修好它呢？
Fatutu: But why? We've kept it docked for years.

卡穆塔：总有一天我们得出海捕鱼，或是去某个别的小岛待上一阵子……
Kamuta: Maybe one day we'll need to set sail again—to fish or spend some time on another island.

图图石子：可是，我们有几个月一次的船商贸易节，有露兜树果和红鲷鱼……我们怎么会离开这儿呢？
Fatutu: But, the merchants already come by every few months to bring us hala fruits and red snappers. Why would we need to sail?

卡穆塔在图图石子的眼前来回踱步，堵在嘴边的话几乎重逾千斤。
Kamuta paces back and forth in front of Fatutu, the words stuck in his throat.

卡穆塔：万一这儿很快就会遭到一场风浪的侵袭呢？万一我们的房屋被冲垮了呢？万一……
Kamuta: Yeah, but what if a storm hits? Are we just going to sit around and let the waves wash away our homes?

图图石子：我们可不是第一次遇上这样糟糕的事了，努库泰澳人能面对这些威胁。
Fatutu: We've been through much worse than a few storms.

图图石子骄傲地昂起头来。
She raises her head proudly.

图图石子：海水一次次地漫上来，它们“轰隆——”吃掉了马拉尼亚环礁，小希拉尼最喜欢的地方，上面还有我们一起搭起的石子塔……
Fatutu: Remember when the waves came and took away Malaga? Heilani cried for days over that little pebble castle.

图图石子：接着是以提提，我们举办独木舟环岛比赛的地方。那儿的水道最平，水流也最缓……可不知从哪儿来的黑黢黢的油污把整座岛都给染成了黑色。
Fatutu: And then that strange oil polluted the water all around Itiiti—the only place where the water's calm enough to hold the Paopao race. We haven't held a race since.

图图石子：再后来是米缇、维布那……
Fatutu: Then Miti and Vaipuna ...

图图石子：可我们还是坚持过来了，大家也生活得更加亲近紧密。我们还有脚下的麦黎，不是吗？
Fatutu: But we've made it through, because that's what we do in the face of difficulties, right? We stick together. Besides, we're doing just fine on Meli.

卡穆塔：万一连麦黎也遇上了那样大的风浪呢？
Kamuta: But what if we lose Meli to the waves as well?

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

卡穆塔：如果真到了那个时候……图图石子，我希望你能带领大家暂时离开这里，你能照顾好大家的，对吧？
Kamuta: If it comes to that, Tutu, I need you to take everyone and leave—find somewhere to stay for a while. Can I ask that of you?

图图石子的眉头皱成了一条蜿蜒的河。
Fatutu's brow furrows.

图图石子：我不明白，哥哥。你一直在说一些很奇怪的话……难道你打算偷偷离开我们吗？
Fatutu: You've been acting strange, brother. Are you thinking of sneaking off and leaving us?

卡穆塔：我哪儿也不打算去。
Kamuta: I'm not going anywhere. I promise.

我向你保证，图图石子。

图图石子：所有人都是这样想的，哥哥。
Fatutu: Neither are the rest of us, brother.

卡穆塔：不，你们必须得做好准备——最好从现在就开始！
Kamuta: No! You must get ready. Start preparing now!

哥哥的反常令图图石子做出一个大胆的猜想。
Kamuta's unusual behavior leads Fatutu to make a bold guess.

图图石子：自从上一次的船商贸易节之后，你就总是心神不宁的，你以前可没有这么多在沙滩上散步、眺望海面的时候……
Fatutu: Something's been bothering you since last trade season. You've been spending a lot of time on the beach, looking out to the sea.

图图石子：难道你被外头的女巫下了可怕的巫术吗？
Fatutu: Did a witch put a spell on you?

图图石子：噢！你一定忘了在脖子上挂上几颗摩鲁卡，也没有把针织骨草和红藻流流叶揣在口袋里。
Fatutu: You better wear some molukka around your neck and carry knitbones and dulse leaves.

卡穆塔：不，不是那些船商，是格蕾丝女士。
Kamuta: No, no, there's no witch. It's just something Ms. Grace told me. It's been bugging me.

图图石子：那位……自称船长的女士？
Fatutu: Ms. Grace? That outsider who calls herself a captain?

船商节在努库泰澳的歌声中缓缓落幕。
With the singing of the Nukutai, the trade festival slowly comes to an end.

沙滩上，客人们与努库泰澳的主人们三三两两地告别，享受着难得的闲暇时光。
On the beach, the Nukutai bid farewell to their guests in twos and threes, enjoying this rare moment of leisure.

淑女格蕾丝：我并没有危言耸听，卡穆塔先生。
Ms. Grace: I don't mean to alarm you, Mr. Kamuta.

淑女格蕾丝：三个月后，麦黎将在一场海啸后彻底沉没。
Ms. Grace: But three months from now, Meli will be devoured by a tsunami.

黑衣女士款款而立，像是在谈论一件无足轻重的小事。
She stands nonchalantly, as if discussing something insignificant.

卡穆塔：格蕾丝女士，请不要再胡说八道了！
Kamuta: Ms. Grace, don't say such nonsense!

卡穆塔：我们欢迎到努库泰澳来的客人，但我们绝不接受任何外乡人对我们的无端恐吓。
Kamuta: You're welcome as a guest, but that doesn't give you the right to spread fear among my people.

淑女格蕾丝：如果我告诉您，关于马拉尼亚环礁与维布那的沉没……并非只是一场天灾呢？
Ms. Grace: What if I told you that the sinking of Malaga and Vaipuna wasn't entirely caused by the tsunami, but there were other factors at play?

卡穆塔：——！
Kamuta: ...!

淑女格蕾丝：海啸淹没了那儿。
Ms. Grace: It is true that the tsunami sent them into the sea. But long before it struck, foreign military forces had been eyeing the islands for their strategic value.

可在洪水退去之前，外界的军队便发现了这片颇有价值的无人区。

卡穆塔：那些轰隆的震响，难道它们不是普通的雷声——？！
Kamuta: Those rumbling sounds ... They weren't thunder?!

淑女格蕾丝：那是人类的鱼雷。
Ms. Grace: They were torpedoes launched by humans.

客人晃了晃手中一份颇有厚度的文件。
She presents a thick document in her hand.

淑女格蕾丝：真不巧，我恰好听说了关于它们的消息。
Ms. Grace: And I have some unfortunate news regarding them.

卡穆塔抢过了那份同样冷冰冰的白皮书。
Kamuta grabs the cold, impersonal stack of white paper.

卡穆塔：“我方宣布对该区域戒严，拟知会相关部门避开涉及相关海域的规划。”
Kamuta: "The area is now under martial law. Any development plans for the region should be revised accordingly."

卡穆塔：这上面的坐标……是我们的努库泰澳……
Kamuta: These coordinates ... they cover Nukutaeao.

淑女格蕾丝：军方对你们的家园进行了勘探，他们笃定自己找到了一片可供军事实验的无人区。
Ms. Grace: After a brief investigation, they concluded that your home is an unoccupied area suitable for their weapon testing.

淑女格蕾丝：不久之后，他们便会公开这份了不起的政绩。
Ms. Grace: It won't be long before they publish a report on this new test site and receive their rewards for discovering it.

卡穆塔：这是因为岛上的“无影无踪雾”……先辈们为了不被外界打扰，特意凝出了这片遮庇生灵的雾气。
Kamuta: The Veil of Nothingness was cast by our ancestors to protect us from the outside world.

卡穆塔：可现在它们却……
Kamuta: I never thought it would put us at risk.

卡穆塔：我得尽快和族人们商量这件事，或许我们早就应该消除这片“无影无踪雾”了。但这很可能引来更多的注意……
Kamuta: As Chief, I must bring this to the attention of my people. Perhaps it's time we removed the mist. But without it, we'll draw all kinds of attention.

卡穆塔捏紧了这份报告。
Kamuta clenches the report tightly in his fist.

卡穆塔：格蕾丝女士，您能将这份资料交给我吗？我需要用它来说服我的族人们。
Kamuta: Ms. Grace, may I borrow this document? My people need to see this.

淑女格蕾丝：当然，但您得抓紧时间了。
Ms. Grace: Be my guest. But you'd better persuade them quickly.

卡穆塔：我不明白您的意思。
Kamuta: Why's that?

淑女格蕾丝：扩大鱼雷试验场的计划早已被列入了军方的日程。
Ms. Grace: As far as I know, they're looking to expand the test site. It's on their agenda now.

卡穆塔：我们可以派出人员与他们谈判。
Kamuta: Right. We'll have to set up a meeting with them to negotiate.

淑女格蕾丝：当然，我衷心地希望您能说服那些杀气腾腾的老爷们，也祝愿你们能够顺利渡过接下来的海啸。
Ms. Grace: Certainly. I wish you the best of luck persuading those warmongers, and for your safety in the coming tsunami.

漫不经心的脚步中，一条条惊世骇俗的发言砸向卡穆塔的脑袋。
Every nonchalant word that leaves her mouth strikes Kamuta with the shocking gravity of the situation.

卡穆塔：我理解您的说法，可……
Kamuta: With all due respect, Ms. Grace ...

卡穆塔：哪怕是以海为生的努库泰澳人，也不敢断言几个月后的海上风浪。格蕾丝小姐，您究竟是如何做出如此大胆的预言？
Kamuta: Not even the Nukutai can predict the movements of the ocean that far in advance. On what basis are you making this forecast?

淑女格蕾丝：这并不是预言，卡穆塔先生……
Ms. Grace: It's not a forecast, Mr. Kamuta.

淑女格蕾丝：这是一次对“过去”的回望。
Ms. Grace: Call it the wisdom of hindsight.

淑女格蕾丝：或者说，您听说过“暴雨”吗？
Ms. Grace: Or perhaps, I should put it more clearly. Have you heard of the "Storm"?

图图石子：哥哥！哥哥！……卡穆塔！
Fatutu: Kamuta! Kamuta! Brother!

卡穆塔：——！
Kamuta: ...!

图图石子：雨越来越大了！别发愣了，我们得赶紧去躲雨！
Fatutu: The rain's getting heavier! We must go inside!

雨水模糊了卡穆塔的视线。
Rain blurs Kamuta's vision.

他眺望远方，倾洒着白沫的海浪呼啸着袭向海岸，似乎连海平面也升了起来。
He stares into the distance, his eyes widening as the frothing waves roar toward the coast. The sea level is rising.

卡穆塔：海啸……真的来了……
Kamuta: It's the tsunami. It's happening.

翻涌而上的海浪将哥哥的低语声拍得粉碎，与土壤一同淹没在愈发上涨的水平线中。
Like the soil beneath the ever-rising waterline, Kamuta's murmured words are quickly buried.

几乎要将整片环礁吞没。
The sea has almost swallowed the whole atoll.

托阿：这是怎么了，图图石子……卡穆塔？
Toa: What's going on, Tutu? Kamuta?

焦急的身影匆匆跑到了这里。
A worried figure hurries over.

图图石子：还不知道，但咱们得先尽力救下这些箱子。
Fatutu: No time for questions, Toa! We must bring these baskets to safety!

图图石子将沙滩上的草编箱子推上了一处高坡。四散的浆果和捆扎的麻布挤在一起，绷紧的草绳把她的手指勒得通红。
Fatutu is already pushing as many woven baskets filled with berries and bundled material as she can up to higher ground. Her hands are a sore red, her face stamped with desperate determination.

托阿：噢，这些是咱们的物资！
Toa: Ah, there's food and clothes in there!

塞洛尼：图图石子，我来帮你——
Selone: Here, I'll give you a hand!

匆匆赶来的高大身影抢过了孩子们手中的箱子，将它们扔到一边。
A tall figure rushes over, grabbing the baskets from the children's hands and tossing them aside.

塞洛尼：卡穆塔，你为什么要扔下它们……？！
Selone: Chief, what are you doing?!

卡穆塔：除了木板，什么都别管了，我们得马上修好那艘船！
Kamuta: Leave them! There's no time! We must get to the ship! Now!

图图石子：等水退了，我们还得想办法活下去呢！
Fatutu: Our people still have to live after the flood's over!

图图石子：但浆果可不会马上从树上掉下来，纱线和针脚也不会乖乖地抱在一起……
Fatutu: If we don't bring something, what are we going to eat or wear? These things won't fall into our laps, you know.

卡穆塔：情况不一样了，图图石子。现在最要紧的是——
Kamuta: Listen! It's different this time. You—

卡穆塔还想再说些什么，林间却突然蹿出了几团黑影。
Before Kamuta can finish speaking, a few dark shadows dart out from the forest.

？？？：吼呜——吼——
???: *roar*

卡穆塔：图图石子，小心！
Kamuta: Tutu! Watch out!

图图石子：——！
Fatutu: ...!

锋利的爪子与卡穆塔的背脊擦身而过。
A row of sharp claws grazes Kamuta's back.

托阿：该死，这儿怎么出现了这么多风暴猫？！
Toa: What are all these Splintercats doing here?!

？？？：&！*/% ……
???: &!*/% ...

塞洛尼：源源不断蹿出的魔精几乎令所有人都慌了神。
Selone: The near-endless surge of critters starts to create an even greater panic.

塞洛尼：不只是风暴猫，还有提克蜗和……长着“鬼脸”的螃蟹？
Selone: These aren't just Splintercats! Are those Sarmatian Sea Snails? And crabs with ghost faces?!

托阿：……以前再大的暴风雨都见不着它们，怎么这次全跑出来了！
Toa: I've never seen them all come out together before. What kind of storm is this?!

疑惑与担忧萦绕在惊雷映照下的每一张脸。
In the flashes of lightning, doubt and worry flicker across the Nukutai's faces.

卡穆塔：它们正处于海啸的应激状态——喊上族人们，我们得先驱逐它们！
Kamuta: They can sense the coming tsunami! Come, we need more hands to drive them off!

托阿：明白——！
Toa: Understood!

逃窜的魔精们如同汹涌的潮水，冲散了互相倚靠的努库泰澳人。
The fleeing critters surge like the tide, scattering the Nukutai.

不少人的身上都挂了彩。
Many are left wounded.

卡穆塔：走，快走——！
Kamuta: Go! All of you! Now!

卡穆塔：所有人——都到“丰收满满号”去！
Kamuta: Everyone, get to the Quick Spear!

“鬼脸螃蟹”：&@#/(#——！
Ghost-Face Crab: &@#/(#—!

图图石子：怎么会、这一次的海啸……看上去比任何一次都更严重！
Fatutu: This tsunami ... It's the worst I've ever seen.

图图石子：难道麦黎真的会被淹没吗？
Fatutu: Is it true? Is this the end of Meli?

卡穆塔：小心，图图石子——！别傻站在那儿！
Kamuta: Tutu! Don't just stand there! Get over here!

阴影中，一只布满棘刺的螯足朝着图图石子的位置挥舞着。
From the shadows, a spiny claw swipes at Fatutu.

？？？：*Slæstu í djúpan dvala.
???: *Slæstu í djúpan dvala.

淑女格蕾丝：漆黑如墨的术法轨迹一闪而逝。
Ms. Grace: An inky-black incantation flashes past her.

淑女格蕾丝：一张熟悉的面庞又一次出现在礁石的最高处。
Ms. Grace: A familiar face appears at the highest point of the reef.

图图石子：——！
Fatutu: ...!

卡穆塔：格蕾丝女士……
Kamuta: Ms. Grace!

格蕾丝环顾四周，朝着慌乱的众人露出一个亲切的笑容。
Grace surveys the scene, a gentle smile on her face.

淑女格蕾丝：看来我并没有来迟。
Ms. Grace: Seems I'm right on time.

图图石子：你就是……格蕾丝。
Fatutu: You're Ms. Grace.

淑女格蕾丝：你该更当心些的，好姑娘。
Ms. Grace: You should be more careful out here, dear.

淑女格蕾丝：我亲爱的努库泰澳朋友们，你们准备好启航了么？
Ms. Grace: People of Nukutaeao, are you ready to set sail?

苍白的影子施施然落在了图图石子的身边。
The pale shadow gracefully lands beside Fatutu.

图图石子：启航……？
Fatutu: Set sail?

图图石子：不，不，你误会了，女士。
Fatutu: No, no, you've got this all wrong, outsider!

图图石子：我们哪儿也不去，努库泰澳人永远不会离开自己的家园。
Fatutu: We are not going anywhere. We Nukutai will not abandon our home.

胸前的一串串贝壳随着图图石子的胸膛一同执拗地起伏着。
The string of shells around Fatutu's neck heaves along with the defiant breaths in her chest.

卡穆塔：冷静点，图图石子。也许格蕾丝女士能有更合适的办法呢……
Kamuta: Tutu, wait. Maybe Ms. Grace knows a better way.

图图石子坚决地挣脱开卡穆塔的手。
She pulls away from Kamuta's hand.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

淑女格蕾丝：可是，你们的家园很快就会被彻底淹没呀。
Ms. Grace: Refuse all you like, Miss, but your homeland will be completely submerged before long.

轻飘飘的话语随意地摆弄着眼前几乎坚不可摧的顽石。
Her words are light, almost careless, as they toy with this unmoving rock before her.

图图石子：努库泰澳人感谢您的援助。
Fatutu: We appreciate your help, Ms. Grace, and we'll make sure to return the favor as best we can.

在海啸过去后，我们会以最高的礼节向您表示最诚挚的谢意。

图图石子：但请原谅，我们无法接受您这样夸大其词的说法。
Fatutu: But we don't find your view on the situation all that convincing.

淑女格蕾丝：……是吗？
Ms. Grace: You don't, do you?

那枚被术法禁锢的偷袭者又一次被递到了图图石子的面前。
The critter, now bound by Grace's incantation, is pulled before Fatutu.

淑女格蕾丝：好好欣赏吧，这可是多么难得一见的珍宝啊。
Ms. Grace: Take a look at this little creature—one of nature's many remarkable creations.

“鬼脸螃蟹”：……
Ghost-Face Crab: ...

淑女格蕾丝：它有一个有趣的名字，月相招潮蟹。
Ms. Grace: It has a fitting name too: the Moon-Eyed Fiddler.

淑女格蕾丝：它们藏在水中，随着潮水的周期与月相藏匿行迹，躲在谁也找不到的地方。
Ms. Grace: They hide themselves in the water, covering their traces with the ebb and flow of the tide.

淑女格蕾丝：直到潮水袭来，它们才不得不途经海岸，迁徙到更安全的水域。
Ms. Grace: They only come ashore when the tide is high, and from there, they migrate to quieter waters.

淑女格蕾丝：无数占卜者和神秘商人们趋之若鹜，视它们为行走的海中黄金。
Ms. Grace: To diviners and arcane dealers, they are the living gold of the ocean.

淑女格蕾丝：可对于那些月相招潮蟹出没地的人们而言，就没那么幸运了……
Ms. Grace: But to the people who live near their regular habitats, they are an ill omen.

淑女格蕾丝：无尽的潮水、海浪，甚至是一场毁灭的洪灾。
Ms. Grace: Wherever they appear, floods are sure to follow.

格蕾丝不着痕迹地朝图图石子靠了靠。
Grace takes a few subtle steps toward Fatutu.

淑女格蕾丝：这只是个开始。
Ms. Grace: This tsunami is only the beginning.

淑女格蕾丝：动物们在应对危机上远比我们清醒，它们会毫不犹豫地抛弃自己的居所……哪怕在其中生活了数十年。
Ms. Grace: Animals migrate and leave their homes behind when conditions become unfavorable. You should do the same.

淑女格蕾丝：你该多为同伴们着想的。
Ms. Grace: Look around you. Think about your people.

魔精的潮水似乎暂时地消退了，努库泰澳人身上的伤痕却仍在汩汩冒血。
The tide of critters seems to have subsided, but the Nukutai still bleed.

四周粗重的叹息与吸气声无比清晰地落入图图石子的耳中。
Fatutu can clearly hear their labored sighs and gasps.

卡穆塔：妹妹，你没有做错任何事……
Kamuta: Tutu, it's okay. We know you have your reasons.

图图石子站在原地，任海水裹起的砂砾冲刷微微颤抖的脚踝。
Fatutu stands frozen, the sand and gravel carried by the seawater washing over her trembling feet.

泪水盈满眼眶，天空斑驳的暴雨灰似乎与地上流淌的血红凝成了一团。
Tears well up in her eyes as the mottled gray of the sky above seems to merge with the crimson ground below.

图图石子：我们一定要离开这儿么？
Fatutu: Do we really have to leave?

格蕾丝的手轻柔地整理图图石子的衣襟，拭去了图图石子脸上的雨珠。
Grace gently adjusts Fatutu's collar, wiping the rain from her face.

淑女格蕾丝：外面的事并不像你想的那样轻松，当然也并没有那样可怕。
Ms. Grace: The outside world is indeed full of dangers, but there is less to fear than you think.

淑女格蕾丝：无论如何，我会帮你的。
Ms. Grace: I'll help you through it.

海潮越发汹涌，拍打着礁石、沙滩，木质的房梁与基座摇摇欲坠。
The tide grows more turbulent, crashing against rocks and shaking the foundations of the Nukutai's homes.

而后是一阵阵轰响，椰子树倒塌，土坡接连不断地塌陷，仿佛山呼海啸。
There's a series of crashes as coconut trees fall, and earth crumbles and falls into the sea.

逐渐黑屏+船只鸣笛的声音，即将出发

淑女格蕾丝：我们的船来了。
Ms. Grace: There it is. Our ship.

长黑屏+鸣笛声由远及近，转接到无线电小姐的广播声

《地球上最后的夜晚》

A hand precisely presses the little green button.

紧接着是更清晰的沉痛哀嚎声。

星锑：无线电小姐——！
Regulus: Ah, Ms. Radio!!

星锑：这可是宝贵的休假时间！你怎么能忘记关闭那可恶的闹钟——！
Regulus: How could you do this to me—today of all days? Your bloody alarm ruined my precious holiday lie-in!

无线电小姐：很抱歉，但这并不是闹钟，而是例行播报的今日资讯。
Ms. Radio: My apologies, Ms. Regulus. But it wasn't an alarm. It was the daily news broadcast.

被拍到一边的无线电小姐信号似乎更好了。
The swatted-aside Ms. Radio seems to have a clear signal.

无线电小姐：如果您对新闻不感兴趣的话，我还可以为您提供今日美文考评、音乐鉴赏、澳大利亚风味美食等相关内容。
Ms. Radio: If the morning news isn't quite to your taste, I can offer a variety of alternatives, including programs on literature and music critique, Australian food, and so on.

星锑：你……！
Regulus: Ugh. No!

船长悲愤的呼喊远远地传了出去。
Her cry echoes through the room.

爱兹拉：抱歉，我似乎不该在这时候出现。
Ezra: Sorry, it seems I've caught you at a bad time.

从门外探头进来的爱兹拉缩了缩脑袋。
Ezra, having just peeked his head through the door, immediately ducks back.

一场单方面的暴行似乎无可辩驳。
A one-sided conflict seems inevitable.

爱兹拉：……但我必须提醒您，星锑小姐，拉普拉斯科算中心鼓励对机器的全方位研究，但不鼓励暴力拆解等行为。
Ezra: Um. But please be careful, Ms. Regulus. I know the LSCC encourages us to examine machines like Ms. Radio, but I don't think a violent disassembly would go down so well.

负隅顽抗的海盗终于站起身来。
Regulus gets to her feet.

星锑：这完全是污蔑，我才是受害者！我要上诉——！

爱兹拉：好的，但您的申请很可能要被搁置一段时间。目前拉普拉斯澳大利亚分部正在进行分组改制的试验。
Ezra: Well, I'm afraid justice might be slow to come. The Australian branch is going through restructuring at the moment. Things will be put on hold for a while.

爱兹拉：您被纳入了一个新的组别，“暴雨”专项研究小组。
Ezra: In the meantime, you've been assigned to a new team—the "Storm" Research Group.

星锑：我……我吗？
Regulus: What? Me?

爱兹拉：当然，“暴雨”专项研究小组的负责人乌尔里希先生亲自将您列入了名单，它很期待与您的首次会面。
Ezra: Yes. Mr. Ulrich's leading it. He made a special request for you to be on the team. He's looking forward to meeting you in person.

星锑：这也太草率了吧——它完全没有征询过我的任何意见啊！
Regulus: What, just like that? Didn't anyone care to ask me what I wanted to do?!

摇滚海盗的疑惑并未持续太久，她猛然想起了什么。
Regulus's puzzled expression soon gives way to a sudden realization.

星锑：等等，你为什么会在今天告诉我这个消息——？！
Regulus: Wait. Why are you telling me this now?

爱兹拉：呃……“暴雨”专项研究小组的成员名单已经在拉普拉斯内部论坛的首页公示一周了，其中写明了所有相关人员的突出贡献。
Ezra: Um. The list of group members and the reasons for their selection have been up on Laplace's website for a week now.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

爱兹拉：而且，今天是“暴雨”专项研究小组正式成立的日子。作为拉普拉斯的正式员工，尤其是“暴雨”专项研究小组的重要成员……您应该到场观礼。
Ezra: And today is its official founding day. You should be there, as a Laplace staff member and an important part of the new team.

星锑：…………？
Regulus: ...?

星锑：不——绝不可能！
Regulus: Hold on a minute! As far as I'm concerned, I'm still on Team Timekeeper!

按照划分，我现在应该归属司辰小队！

星锑：更更更更重要的是，现在仍是我的休假时间！
Regulus: And more importantly, I'm still on my time off!

维尔汀：很高兴你这么有时间观念，星锑。
Vertin: Good to see that you actually paid attention in our last group meeting, Regulus.

箱子的主人，星锑的救星，伟大的司辰小姐及时地降临在门口。
The owner of the suitcase, Regulus's savior, the great Timekeeper, arrives at the door.

星锑：没错，维尔汀——！
Regulus: Vertin! Thank God you're here!

星锑：快，告诉所有人，我们的假期还远远没有结束！
Regulus: Go on! Tell them I'm still on holiday!

为权利奋战的海盗期待着一艘救生艇。
The fast-drowning pirate is hoping for a life preserver.

维尔汀：很遗憾，星锑。今天是短期休假的最后一天。
Vertin: Sorry to break it to you like this, Regulus, but today's our last day off.

星锑：嗯——？！
Regulus: You can't be serious!

维尔汀：当然，我们也接到了拉普拉斯的邀请，乌尔里希组长表现得相当热切。
Vertin: Of course, I am. Also, Mr. Ulrich has invited us to attend the ceremony in Laplace.

维尔汀：需要为你留出一些整理着装的时间吗？
Vertin: Shall I give you a moment to get ready?

星锑：不————！
Regulus: Noooooo!

画面逐渐黑屏

澳大利亚街道

APPLe: Captain, we seem to have deviated from our route to Laplace.

前往科算中心的路途总是遍布坎坷。
The road to the LSCC is ever fraught with obstacles.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

星锑：伟大的海盗依靠的从来都不是罗盘，而是一颗勇往直前的心！

APPLe：原来如此，我还以为你借机支开维尔汀小姐，只是为了行使度过最后一天假期的权利。
APPLe: Ah. This APPLe thought you were trying to slip away to make the most of your final day off.

星锑：咳咳。这当然也很重要！
Regulus: Ahem. Well, that too.

如同特洛伊战争后凯旋的奥德修斯，船长身手矫健地闯入眼前的一个个漩涡。
Like Odysseus returning victorious from the Trojan War, Regulus nimbly dives into one vortex after another.

街头商人：来自巴西的苏卡拉特兽触须，炼制“凉飕飕药剂”的绝佳材料！
Street Vendor: Come get your Succarath whiskers all the way from Brazil, perfect for brewing a Chillwind Elixir! Only 185 Sharpodonties!

Street Vendor: See anything you like? You won't find a better price anywhere!

这样的好东西你还藏着多少？统统拿出来——

星锑：噢，好吧～
Regulus: Oh, yeah. You're right.

星锑：嘿、嘿嘿！老兄，颜料可不是这么使的，我非常建议你尝试波普艺术，再邋遢的艺术家碰上它也能摇身一变，吸引街上所有人的注意～
Regulus: Alright, mate? Whoa, love the colors! How about bringing in some pop art? Trust me, it'll take it to a whole new level.

Regulus: I beg your pardon?!

Cruise Ticket Seller: Ladies and gentlemen, the party starts now! Put your hands together for the enchanting Ms. Barcarola and her captivating melodies!

星锑：喔～～～
Regulus: Woo-hoo!

溢美之辞从宣传员的口中井喷而出，舞台中央的明星悄悄侧过脸去。
Compliments gush from the ticket seller's mouth as the star at the center of the stage subtly turns her face away.

芭卡洛儿侧头低语。

芭卡洛儿：这样的宣传词也太夸张了……汉米西先生……
Barcarola: You're much too kind, Mr. Hamish, saying all these wonderful things about me, but I'm only a cruise musician.

芭卡洛儿：我很乐意为“自由海风号”尽一份力，但它的成功属于每一位船员，过、过高的评价不……
Barcarola: It's thanks to the collective efforts of the whole crew that the "Free Breeze" has been so successful. I just feel privileged to be a part of it.

宣传船员：“过高的评价不利于培养出一位伟大的音乐大师”，我完全理解，芭卡洛儿小姐——
Cruise Ticket Seller: I know you want to stay humble, Ms. Barcarola, but there's no reason to be so modest!

宣传船员：可事实上，我们的客人大多都是冲着您和您的独门乐器来的，我相信，您的名气一定会为“自由海风号”招徕更多的客人～
Cruise Ticket Seller: Many of our guests come aboard just to hear you play, and I'm sure there will only be more in the future! So, what's the harm with hyping the crowd up with a little round of applause?

芭卡洛儿：好吧……这不是为了我自己，而是为了我们的“自由海风号”。
Barcarola: Well, if it's for the ship, I suppose I can handle a little publicity.

宣传船员：当然，芭卡洛儿小姐～
Cruise Ticket Seller: Of course you can! And you deserve it, too! By the way, do you know the guest over there? She's very, uh, enthusiastic.

另外……您认识那位过于热情的客人么？

芭卡洛儿：嗯？
Barcarola: Hm?

她朝着船员手指的方向望去，那儿有派对中格外热情的一角。
She follows the direction he's pointing to find a particularly lively duo among the crowd.

一位红白相间的女士与一颗飘浮的苹果。
A girl dressed in red and blue, and a floating apple.

LEE-03 密码学入门 / Cryptography for Beginners

像是在窥视某种隐秘的信息。

Ulrich: You've been working in Laplace for 11 months now, and you still haven't submitted your performance appraisal or published a single valid project result!

乌尔里希：换而言之，你还没有通过拉普拉斯科算中心的试用期考核，自然也无法享有拉普拉斯正式员工的福利。

乌尔里希：计算机在你的左侧，第二个柜子里还有几本你可能会用到的参考资料，其中涉及了一部分计算机的基本原理及使用教程。

特殊玩法-做数独题（已和系统确认）
The mathematical onslaught seems endless.

单方面的数字霸凌似乎远远没有尽头。

Ulrich: The ninth "Storm" has passed, Researcher Regulus. You've had plenty of time to brush up on your math.

组长从纷纷扬扬落下的纸质雨幕中穿行而过，随手接下了其中一张凌乱的稿纸。
Ulrich strides over, picking up a paper from the desk on his way.

乌尔里希：在这里，我们只需要将这些信息编码进行最基本的解码，再代入拉普拉斯的密钥进行重编译……注意它们尾部第四位数字的变化，星锑研究员。
Ulrich: Alright, let me explain. All you have to do is a basic decode and transcription of the result using the Laplace encryption key. See how the fourth from last digits have changed?

乌尔里希：第十七区间的数字，没有任何一个数字大于24，而第十八区间的数字限度则是59……因此，我们便能做出一个大胆的假设——
Ulrich: There are no numbers greater than 24 within the 17th interval, and those in the 18th interval don't exceed 59. So, if we make a bold assumption here—

乌尔里希：这些代码很可能隶属于拉普拉斯命名法，这一规则要求将第十二区至第十八区用作可转译的时间编码。
Ulrich: These numbers have probably been coded using Laplace's nomenclature, where the codes of time are always placed between the 12th and 18th intervals.

乌尔里希：它们被广泛运用于科算中心相关的船只编号、天文事业、人员批次等资料收录中。
Ulrich: You'll see this a lot here. We use them for ships, satellites, manpower arrangements, and such.

乌尔里希：将这些转译后的编码输入到拉普拉斯的天文数据库后，我得到了它们。
Ulrich: Finally, we input the result into the Laplace astronomy database to see if we find any matches and ... there.

乌尔里希：一组天文照片。
Ulrich: A set of photos taken from space.

星锑视角：画面中心是排列成一排的照片【需要标明年份】

星锑：……！
Regulus: Huh?

星锑：你的意思是，困扰我这么久的，只是几张普通的照片——？！
Regulus: Are you telling me I spent the whole day doing this just to find a few photos?

乌尔里希：星锑研究员，它们也许比你意识到的更重要一些。
Ulrich: These aren't just any photos, Researcher Regulus. Take a closer look.

乌尔里希：第一张拍摄于1995年12月2日，内容为太阳与日球层探测器的发射升空。
Ulrich: The first picture was taken on December 2nd, 1995, the day the Solar and Heliospheric Observatory was launched.

像是打开了灵感的缺口，源源不断的信息激烈而迅速地涌入了星锑的大脑。
Ulrich continues to deliver a flurry of information.

乌尔里希：根据上面的数据显示，第二张照片拍摄于1997年6月25日，具体内容为太阳黑子的活动记录。
Ulrich: The second picture was taken on June 25th, 1997, during a period of sunspot activity.

乌尔里希：而第三张照片拍摄于1998年11月21日，内容为太空拍摄，空间站的第一个舱体，一颗人造卫星。
Ulrich: The third one is from November 21st, 1998. It's an image of the first satellite ever deployed from a space station.

星锑：第四张是在1999年12月28日，拍下来的是一场……橄榄球赛？
Regulus: And the fourth is from December 28th, 1999. Is that a rugby game?

乌尔里希：那是在墨尔本举办的最后一场球赛，自那之后，那个体育场就被推平了，现在大概被归入了某类千篇一律的商业区划中。
Ulrich: Yes. Looks like it was the last one held in that stadium in Melbourne. The place is just a commercial district now.

她的视线继续向后，却又突兀地卡在了下一张照片。
Her eyes wander over the next photos. Then, she freezes.

星锑：不、不，这不对——！
Regulus: But, wait. This isn't right!

星锑：如果按照你的说法，那么后面的照片根本无法解释……
Regulus: If you're suggesting what I think you are, then these next photos are ...

她的声线有些颤抖。
Her eyes widen.

乌尔里希：是的，从第五张照片开始，我们已经无法确认具体的拍摄内容，它们可能涉及哈雷彗星、柯伊伯带阋神星、乌卢鲁运动会、摇滚音乐节等一系列内容。
Ulrich: That's right. From the fifth photo onward, we can't pinpoint their exact time or location, but it seems they involve Halley's Comet, 136199 Eris and the Kuiper Belt, the Uluru Games, and a rock festival.

乌尔里希：更可怕的是，它们的时间仍在向前。
Ulrich: And there are more. Take a look at these time stamps.

乌尔里希：2001年2月9日，2003年10月21日，2005年11月……
Ulrich: February 9th, 2001 ... October 21st, 2003 ... November, 2005 ...

星锑：最后一张是……2007年4月16日。
Regulus: And the last one's from ... April 16th, 2007.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

组长抬起头来，窗外万里无云，巨大的信息流在其中悄无声息地奔涌。
Ulrich looks out to the endless blue of the sky outside.

乌尔里希：这证明了一件事。在我们，在基金会，在所有人未曾理解即将面临的浩劫，在第一次“暴雨”到来之时——
Ulrich: This proves one thing: Before all our struggles to study and control the effects of the "Storm" ...

乌尔里希：有一位先驱，他穿越了“暴雨”，为我们留下了这些宝贵的信息。
Ulrich: This pioneer crossed the "Storm" unscathed and sent us these images.

“暴雨”，一个沉重的话题。
The "Storm." That heavy topic.

它又一次突兀地在人们的眼前显现，漫不经心地作弄着每一个试图理解这个荒唐世界的人。
Once again, it rears its ugly head, mocking anyone who dares to make sense of its absurdity.

星锑：可……
Regulus: But ...

好在永远有人不会接受它的摆布。
Thankfully, there will always be someone who doesn't bend to its desires.

星锑：你为什么要告诉我这些？难道其他拉普拉斯员工的考核，都涉及这么重要的机密内容吗？
Regulus: Why are you telling me all this? Did everyone else's assessments turn into some kind of top-secret briefing?

星锑：……我只是希望预支一部分工资而已啊！
Regulus: All I wanted was an advance on my salary!

组长极力压抑住隐隐作痛的磁流体。
The ferrofluid gives a stifled pang.

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：星锑，你明白么，一项伟大的事业正在我们面前展开——
Ulrich: Just for once, could you see the bigger picture here? We've been presented with an amazing opportunity.

乌尔里希：——难道你只能想到这个？！
Ulrich: And all you can think about is your salary?!

LEE-04 时代之声 / Music of the Era

星锑：阿嚏——！这儿的灰尘未免也太多了！
Regulus: Achoo! Ugh, the dust in here! What, are we inside some kind of vacuum cleaner?

星锑：乌尔里希组长，难道这就是你随身携带玻璃脑袋的原因吗？
Regulus: Is that why you always wear that fish tank on your head?

Familiar with Regulus's quirks, Ulrich opts for the most efficient form of communication: none.

摸清了身旁组员的习性后，快步前进的组长早已明了最妥善的交流方式。

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

星锑：你在践行某种绝不附和他人的摇滚精神吗？
Regulus: What's got you so quiet? Pulling the "strong and silent" act now?

乌尔里希：我们到了。
Ulrich: Here we are.

陌生的环境久疏打理，灰尘与杂物肆无忌惮地徜徉在观测台所有目所能及的角落。
The site has been utterly neglected. Dust and debris litter every corner of it.

星锑：这里是……？
Regulus: Here, as in ...?

乌尔里希：拉普拉斯克罗纳拉发射场，拉普拉斯、基金会、美国航空航天局曾在这展开过许多合作项目。
Ulrich: The Laplace launch site in Sydney. We've collaborated with the Foundation and the space agency for various projects here.

星锑：多亏了你的提醒，组长。我差点以为这儿是某个摇滚歌手的家了。
Regulus: Thanks for the heads-up. I almost thought we'd just barged into some rock star's house.

乌尔里希：事实上，在两年之后，这儿才被正式列为航空航天的发射场之一。
Ulrich: It will actually take another two years before this place becomes an official launch site.

星锑：噢！我差点儿忘了，我们现在正处于“过去”。
Regulus: Oh! Yeah, right, we're basically living in the past.

乌尔里希：为了验证那颗卫星的资料，我先后辗转了数个卫星发射基地，圭亚那航天中心、普列谢茨克航天发射场……最后才来到了这里。
Ulrich: I visited various launch sites to verify the photos—Guiana Space Centre, Plesetsk Cosmodrome—then, I found this place.

乌尔里希：尽管大部分的资料早就被“暴雨”摧毁了，但好在这儿还保留了不少前期的调研资料。
Ulrich: Most of its archives were lost in the "Storm," but a small portion of the early records survived.

乌尔里希：我把它们和我整理的资料都放在这里……
Ulrich: I left them here with the rest of the files I compiled.

文件与纸张们随着组长越发急迫的翻找动作一同飞扬起来。
Papers scatter into the air as he rummages through the files.

乌尔里希：该死的，它们被扔哪儿去了——？！！！
Ulrich: Damn it! Where did they go?!

磁流体的波动震耳欲聋。

星锑：哈……？
Regulus: Huh?!

星锑：那我们是不是可以各回各家……
Regulus: So, does this mean we can all go home now?

乌尔里希：没门儿！
Ulrich: Absolutely not!

乌尔里希：星锑，你得到了一项新任务：呆在原地别动，什么也别做，等着我找回那些资料！
Ulrich: Alright, new task: Stay put and don't touch anything. I need to find those files.

星锑：好吧。
Regulus: Ugh, fine.

组长的身影匆匆离去，星锑举起的手臂仅仅维持了一瞬。
As Ulrich makes his exit, Regulus scans the room, a glint growing behind her eyes.

星锑：——才怪～

星锑：尘封的军事基地，隐秘的传闻……喔，这里面一定藏着某种重大的秘密！
Regulus: An old military base, mysterious photos ... Oh, this is going to be juicy!

星锑：乌尔里希组长决不能阻止一位躁动的摇滚海盗放弃对宝藏、咳……对重要资料的追逐！
Regulus: No chance Ulrich is stopping this rockin' pirate from going after treasure, I mean, very, very important files.
Regulus: The hunt is on!

星锑：本船长宣布，发射场大冒险正式启航——！
Regulus: Haha! Let's start with what's on this table!

星锑：嗯哼～就从这张幸运的桌子开始吧～
The clinking and clattering of rummaging fills the air, like a string of cheerful musical notes.

叮叮当当的翻找声此起彼伏，像是一簇簇欢快的音符。

星锑：♪～♫～～♬～～～～
Regulus: ♪ ... ♫ ... ♬

星锑：噢，差点忘了最重要的事——对未知之地的探索怎么能缺少一首同样激情的摇滚乐伴奏呢？！
Regulus: Oh, I almost forgot! Can't go treasure hunting without some music to rock out to!

拨动旋钮，打开功率扩大器。
Turning the knob, she powers up the amplifier.

世界属于摇滚！
The world belongs to rock!

远远传来的强有力的震动令它脑子里的磁流体几乎要蹦出玻璃缸来。
The vibrations reach Ulrich, causing the ferrofluid to ripple.

连桌面也在轻微地晃荡。
Even the desk is trembling.

乌尔里希：该死的，我忘了禁止她制造噪音！
Ulrich: Damn it! I forgot to tell her to keep quiet!

？？？：咕吱——！
???: Squawk!

更刺耳的鸟鸣声盖过了远处的哼唱。
The screech of a bird pierces through the pumping music.

乌尔里希：怎么了？这里地震了吗？
Ulrich: What's happening? Is this an earthquake?

几团灵巧的黑影蹦到了观测台的高处。
A few agile black shadows leap around the upper parts of the observation deck.

在一阵剧烈的震颤中，一张贴在墙板上的便签轻飘飘地滑落下来。
The tremors free a note pinned to the wall, and it flutters down to the ground.

上面的字体相当眼熟。
The handwriting is all too familiar:

“调查员报告，附近发生过数起特里波德罗袭击人类事件。”
"Investigator's Report: Multiple Tripodero attacks on humans have occurred in the area."

“它们似乎把这儿的废弃工程视为自己的领地，会对任何入侵领地的外来生物发起攻击。”
"They seem to regard this abandoned facility as their territory, attacking any intruders."

“记得动作放轻些！！！”
"Remember: Keep your movements quiet!!!"

记录人：乌尔里希
Ulrich

乌尔里希：噢，该死——这是我之前留下来的！
Ulrich: Ah, crap! This is the note I wrote last time I was here!

磁流体迅速扩散出一圈涟漪。
The ferrofluid ripples violently.

乌尔里希：星锑，把你的音响关了！——立刻！马上！
Ulrich: Regulus! Turn off that speaker! Now!

星锑：♪～♫～～
Regulus: ♪ ... ♫ ...

快乐的寻宝海盗依然沉浸在自己的世界里。
Regulus is too immersed in her treasure-seeking to hear him.

特里波德罗：吱吱——吱吱——！
Tripodero: Squawk!

一团墨绿色的黏液从高处射了下来，乌尔里希打了个滚儿，堪堪躲了过去。
A glob of dark green sludge shoots down from above. Ulrich darts aside, narrowly avoiding the attack.

乌尔里希：干**的[拉普拉斯脏话]！
Ulrich: I knew I should have upgraded my memo module!

乌尔里希：我早晚有一天得给这套装置搭载最新的备忘录系统！
He looks to the observation deck. There is Regulus, gleefully twisting to the music.

它瞥了眼身后星锑所在的观测台，仿佛看到后者正欢快地跳着扭扭舞。
He looks to the observation deck. There is Regulus, gleefully twisting to the music.

乌尔里希：……乌尔里希，你得老老实实给每一位不靠谱的组员擦屁股，这是你的职责。
Ulrich: Calm down, Ulrich. You're a leader. It's part of your job to clean up after your team.

组长环视四周难以估算价值的装置与器械，叹了口气，转头便闪进了紧急出口的通道。
He looks over the priceless equipment around him and sighs before ducking through the emergency exit.

捍卫领地的特里波德罗们紧随其后。
The Tripoderos follow in hot pursuit.

磁流体的“思想电流”在一个个电子元件中迸出激烈的火花，嘈杂的噪音接连不断地涌出，三脚架鸟儿们四散奔逃。
Ulrich sends a current through the electronic components around him, creating a cacophony of sounds that sends the Tripoderos scattering.

特里波德罗：吱！#&%——
Tripodero: Squawk!

乌尔里希：**的[拉普拉斯脏话]——终于结束了！
Ulrich: Flux! FLUX! Finally, it's over!

组长毫不留情地谩骂着，终于将最后一件毁坏的器械塞进了回收箱。
Ulrich stuffs the last piece of damaged equipment into the recovery bin.

它气喘吁吁地翻回了窗户。
Then, he climbs back through the window. He is visibly drained.

乌尔里希：冷静，乌尔里希，冷静……想成为一个成熟的组长，你不得不接受这滑稽的现实。
Ulrich: Relax. Don't overheat. You'll have to get used to this if you wanna be a good leader.

一无所知的步伐蹦蹦跳跳地回到了这里。
Regulus bounces lightly into the room.

星锑：嘿，组长——
Regulus: Ulrich!

星锑：瞧我发现了什么——！
Regulus: Look what I found!

她晃了晃手中的战利品——一份写有乌尔里希亲笔签名的厚重档案。
She waves her treasure—a hefty stack of documents, signed in bold by Ulrich himself.

星锑：为我欢呼吧！
Regulus: Ahem. Where's my round of applause?

星锑：如果是一位合格的组长，它一定会为星锑研究员的卓越表现争取一个令人满意的薪水评级！
Regulus: If you're even half a leader, you'll fight your hardest to get a decent salary for such an outstanding employee as myself!

摇滚海盗得意地朝着组长挤眉弄眼。
She shoots him a triumphant wink.

乌尔里希：……好。
Ulrich: Sure.

星锑：但身为一位合格的研究员，我必须本着科研精神说出一个事实……
Regulus: Just one more thing, scientist to scientist—

星锑的眉头紧皱，朝着乌尔里希身旁仍在滋滋作响的老旧机器们努了努嘴。
Regulus gestures toward the still-sparking machines beside Ulrich.

星锑：乌尔里希组长，我不知道你竟然有着这么前卫而特别的音乐喜好～
Regulus: You made some pretty cool "electronic music" in that battle. Didn't know you had it in you!

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

组长深深地叹了口气，决定不再与这位跳脱的组员进行任何辩驳。
Ulrich lets out a deep sigh, deciding to avoid any further arguments with his team member.

乌尔里希：这些就是我们能找到的关于这座天文望远镜卫星项目的全部资料。
Ulrich: Here are all the files related to the satellite.

乌尔里希：打开看看吧，星锑。
Ulrich: Look them over, Regulus.

星锑：乌尔里希组长……我们非得现在就和文字战斗吗？
Regulus: Do we have to go through all this right now?

星锑：难道这些资料里还有比那些天文照片更劲爆的内容？
Regulus: Why? Is there some even more juicy stuff in them?

乌尔里希：对你而言，是的。
Ulrich: For you, it might be.

乌尔里希：这一卫星项目的载荷舱搭载了许多神秘学材料制品，包括太空种子、龙血树脂罗盘、黑曜石晶体、广域照相机、天体摄谱仪等等……
Ulrich: The satellite carries a variety of arcane items. Space seeds, dragon tree resin compasses, obsidian crystals, WFPCs, astronomical spectrometers ...

乌尔里希：甚至连它的动力源也是一台神秘学唱片机。
Ulrich: Even its power source is an arcane record player.

乌尔里希：我们已经将所有相关的材料列入了“人工暴雨”项目的实验清单，那正是我们之后要探索的方向。
Ulrich: We've made a list of everything that was on it so we can test them against the "Artificial Storm."

乌尔里希：它们象征着人类对于最尖端神秘学与科研技术的探索。我们的望远镜同事携带着这些人类智慧的结晶，孤独地躲过一次又一次“暴雨”。
Ulrich: The satellite is an archive of the wisdom of the entire human race. It's somehow survived multiple "Storms."

星锑：……你们不打算接它回家吗？
Regulus: What are you going to do with it?

乌尔里希：很遗憾，因为缺少维修，它最终因为零件故障而坠毁了。
Ulrich: Sadly, a lack of maintenance caused it to plummet to the Earth.

乌尔里希：坠毁的时间正是你所经历的时代，1966年。
Ulrich: It crashed in your time, 1966.

星锑：……！
Regulus: ...!

星锑的墨镜在震惊中掉到了地上，但她无暇顾及。
Regulus's sunglasses slide off her face, but she doesn't even notice.

她抢过那沓厚重的空间望远镜资料，翻到了最后一页。
She grabs the stack of documents and flips to the last page.

“至此，该空间望远镜于2007年坠毁于伦敦奥尔德堡，携带仪器一并损毁，遗失……回收失败。”
"The telescope officially crashed in 2007 in Aldeburgh, England. All onboard instruments were destroyed ... Recovery failed."

“‘星锑空间望远镜’项目，报告如上。”
"'Regulus Space Telescope' project report: as above."

乌尔里希：这个空间望远镜项目的命名，那台搭载其中的神秘学唱片机的唱片，还有你的名字……
Ulrich: The telescope project was named after a record that was on the satellite, which also happens to share your name.

星锑：都是……星锑？！
Regulus: Regulus!

星锑将背包抱在胸前，装满珍藏的口袋微微敞开。
Regulus holds her backpack tightly to her chest, its pockets full of treasures.

颤抖的手指抚过一张张唱片，她清楚地意识到自己在寻找什么。
She flips through a series of records, her hands trembling.

她终于找到了那张“正确”的珍藏——一张与资料图案一模一样的唱片。
Finally, she finds the treasure she is looking for—a record identical to the one depicted in the documents.

来自1966年的奥尔德堡“陨石坑”音乐节上的一次意外。
It's from the 1966 Aldeburgh "Crater" Music Festival, an accident from the past.

伟大的摇滚海盗最爱的那一张。
And her all-time favorite.

星锑：是它……我最宝贝的“小东西”？
Regulus: My "little thing"—it was the record on the satellite?

乌尔里希：——！
Ulrich: ...!

乌尔里希：真没想到，它竟然如此完好地保存在你手里！
Ulrich: Yes, that's the one! Wow, you've kept it in great shape!

星锑：在它身上，也许就藏着能让我们越过“暴雨”的秘密……？
Regulus: So, this is the key to braving the "Storm"?

乌尔里希：我唯一能够确认的是，它是“免疫回溯”的可能性之一。
Ulrich: It might be. Among several other options.

星锑：这也是你将我列入“暴雨”专项研究小组成员名单的原因。
Regulus: I get it. That's why you wanted me on the "Storm" research team.

乌尔里希：不止如此。
Ulrich: Not just that.

乌尔里希：我了解过那座数字岛的事件报告，你在谷神星解码中展现了出色的解密天赋……更重要的是，你亲历了数次“暴雨”。
Ulrich: I've read the Apeiron Island reports. You demonstrated some serious talent with the Ceres puzzle in that cave, and you've faced more "Storms" than the majority of the Laplace staff.

乌尔里希：这不是为了某个人的研究成果，而是为了全人类的希望……
Ulrich: We're not working together for a couple of research papers. This is about the survival of everything on Earth.

乌尔里希：你理应成为其中的一份子。
Ulrich: We need all the help we can get, including yours.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

跳脱的组员罕见地沉默了许久。
Regulus falls into an uncharacteristic silence.

乌尔里希：咳、事实上，关于如何借用你的唱片，基金会和拉普拉斯甚至开展了一次专门的研讨会。
Ulrich: Ahem. In fact, Laplace even held a meeting with the Foundation to discuss borrowing your record.

乌尔里希：基金会方建议，我们应该以“人工暴雨”项目的名义，向基金会总部申请物品调令，由他们与司辰进行后续对接工作。
Ulrich: The Foundation suggested we apply for an item transfer order under the "Artificial Storm" project and let the Timekeeper take over the matter.

乌尔里希：科算中心的一些同事告诉我，对内部职员的资产调用，可以直接援引《拉普拉斯科算中心人员处理条例》，这是每一位科算中心人的义务。
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：……
The frequency of the ferrofluid's vibrations is chaotic, like some kind of unsolvable cipher.

磁流体的震动频率杂乱无序，形如某种没有答案的密文。
Ulrich: But ... alright.

乌尔里希：好吧好吧——
Ulrich: Let me be honest with you. I'm not comfortable with taking your record by force. It's yours, after all. It's your choice what you do with it.

乌尔里希：我承认，我一点儿也不想援引那些该死的条例，它们完全违背了个人意志——无论如何，这是你的唱片！
Ulrich: Let me be honest with you. I'm not comfortable with taking your record by force. It's yours, after all. It's your choice what you do with it.

乌尔里希：因此，我只想在这儿，以乌尔里希的个人名义和你谈一谈。
Ulrich: So, here I am, not as your leader, but as myself, hoping we can find a solution that works for both of us.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

星锑：乌尔里希组长，有人告诉过你……你真的很不适合做演讲吗？
Regulus: Has anyone ever told you that you're terrible at negotiations?

乌尔里希：——该死的，我就知道没那么容易！
Ulrich: Ah, damn it. I knew it wouldn't be easy.

组长恼怒地挥了挥拳头，那张令它魂牵梦萦的唱片却直楞楞地停留在它的眼前。
He angrily knocks his tank with his fist. He is so close to the record he's been searching for.

玻璃缸的磁流体显著地炸开了一个微妙的弧度。
The ferrofluid ripples into a subtle arc.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

星锑：拿去搞你的“人工暴雨”研究吧，乌尔里希组长～
Regulus: Go ahead, Mr. Ulrich. Take it.

星锑：在我改变主意之前。
Regulus: Before I change my mind.

星锑的表情从未如此郑重。
Regulus's expression has never been so serious.

乌尔里希：你愿意将它捐赠给“人工暴雨”项目——？！
Ulrich: Y-You're willingly giving it over to the "Artificial Storm" project?

准备好的数套说辞扑了个空。
His carefully prepared arguments vanish in a moment.

星锑：毕竟你们也是为了解决“暴雨”问题，这也称得上是与摇滚乐同样伟大的事业了！
Regulus: For a cause even greater than rock music? Absolutely!

星锑：但事先声明——这只是暂时的捐赠，实验结束后，你必须马上归还它！
Regulus: But just to be clear: I'm only lending it to Laplace. You have to give it back when you're done!

星锑：这可是全球仅此一张的限量款！是将要流传在星锑博物馆的镇馆之宝！！！
Regulus: It's the only copy in the world and the future centerpiece of the Regulus Museum!

乌尔里希：感谢你的奉献，星锑研究员。
Ulrich: Thank you, Researcher Regulus. Thank you so much!

乌尔里希：我原以为这会是场相当复杂的谈判。为了应付这一风险，我甚至提前向拉普拉斯申请了一大笔专项经费，以及一个月的自由假期……
Ulrich: I was gearing up for a much tougher talk. I even applied for additional funding and a month's leave to offer you as leverage. Well, I suppose I won't have to use it after all.

玻璃镜面映出的自豪的扭扭舞步僵在了原地。
Regulus freezes.
Regulus: AH! WHAT?!

星锑：什么——？！
The suitcase is in its usual harmony.

箱中的气氛显然要比外界安静得多。
Its occupants go about their business, each busying themselves in their own little worlds.

人们各行其是，在房间里忙碌着各自的小世界。

？？？：司辰——？
???: Timekeeper?

维尔汀：十四行诗，你看起来很忙碌。
Vertin: Sonetto? What's the rush?

十四行诗：……我来提醒您，我们在澳大利亚的假期已经结束了。
Sonetto: I just wanted to remind you that our vacation in Australia is over.

十四行诗：如果您有什么需要收拾的行李，请告诉我。
Sonetto: If you need any help packing, please let me know.

她擦了擦额头上渗出的细汗，又突然想起了什么。
She wipes the sweat from her forehead. Then, she remembers something.

十四行诗：对了，这是留给您的。
Sonetto: Oh, and I have something for you.

一张花花绿绿的纸张被递到了维尔汀的面前。
She hands her a colorful piece of paper.

维尔汀：……？
Vertin: Huh?

十四行诗：星锑委托我将它分发给大家，她在游轮宣传比赛中赢得了这一批战利品。
Sonetto: Regulus asked me to pass these out. She won them at a sailaway party.

十四行诗：“非常有纪念价值！值得所有人瞻仰！”她是这么说的。
Sonetto: She said they're "highly valuable, the finest choice for any collection," if I recall correctly.

维尔汀：可这似乎只是一张普通的广告宣传单……难道其中藏着某种深意吗？
Vertin: Looks like an ordinary flyer to me.

十四行诗：我已经检查过了。
Sonetto: I've already inspected them.
Sonetto: They're just advertisements with a handwritten signature in the corner and some completely over-the-top promises.

十四行诗：里面只是些寻常的宣传口号，一个漂亮的手写签名……噢，还有几句让人看不懂的句子。
Sonetto: Regulus told me it's a trick that advertisers use. They use fancy words to catch people's eyes and make it seem more grand.

十四行诗：星锑告诉我，这是广告商惯用的手段，用一些让人看不懂的话语来凸显商品的文化与底蕴。
Sonetto: Phrases like "an opulent odyssey upon the boundless sea," "tour the illustrious Pacific coast," "a veritable feast of harmonic reverie," "rare and fortuitous seasonal discount," and "facilities unimaginable in their splendor" ...

十四行诗：“豪华海上假期”、“环太平洋巡游”、“音乐盛宴”、“季节折扣”、“豪华设施”……
Sonetto: Hmm. What's this on the back?

十四行诗：嗯……那些句子是……
Sonetto: Nor happiness, nor harmony, nor fame,

十四行诗：欢欣，平安，或是声名，康健
Sonetto: Nor happiness, nor harmony, nor fame,

十四行诗：又及敬佩与尊严，技巧同孔武
Sonetto: Nor pride, nor strength, nor skill in arms or arts.

维尔汀：——！
Vertin: ...!

熟悉的词句如同激荡的电流在耳边炸响。
Those familiar words hit like a tidal wave.

维尔汀：那牧鞭与其谦卑羔羊算得什么？
Vertin: Before a cruel whip ...

众：人，要想成为人
Man who man would be,

众：须主宰自身上建立的王廷，以自我所克制的意识
Must rule the empire of himself; in it must be supreme, establishing his throne ...

众：平定他的渴求与惧怕蛊惑
On vanquished will; quelling the challenges of hopes and fears ...

完全地成为他自己本人
Being himself alone.

她触电般地缩回了手。
She recoils in shock.

传单飘落在地。
The flyer falls to the ground.

十四行诗：……！
Sonetto: ...!

十四行诗：您怎么了——司辰？
Sonetto: Is everything alright, Timekeeper?

那是一首她曾无比熟悉的诗。
This is a poem she once knew intimately.

它曾由许多双稚嫩的手托举而起，在许多同样稚嫩的声带间缓缓流淌。
One that had been held by countless young hands and flowed gently through equally young voices.

在树洞，在广场，在门外。
In the tree hollow, in the square, in the outdoors.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀：十四行诗，计划有变。
Vertin: Sonetto, change of plan.

维尔汀：我需要立刻联系基金会。
Vertin: We need to contact the Foundation. Now.

LEE-05 离港日 / The Day We Set Sail

康斯坦丁：会长，向您致意。
Constantine: Good afternoon, Mr. President.

康斯坦丁：愿和平与我们同在。
Constantine: May the peace be with us.

会长：愿和平与我们同在，我的朋友。
President: May the peace be with us, my friend.

康斯坦丁微微颔首，目光落在更深的阴影里。
Constantine gives a slight nod as she peers into the shadows.

康斯坦丁：芝诺军备学院的内部整顿行动已经结束了，如预期一样，除了一部分伊戈尔的极端拥护者，大部分的人员对此次叛逃事件并不知情。
Constantine: Zeno has been restored to its usual state. Aside from Igor's ardent supporters, the rest of the Zeno soldiers and officers were unaware of his betrayal—just as we expected.

康斯坦丁：我们按原定计划为“上将伊戈尔”举办了隆重的葬礼，按照芝诺葬礼的规定，所有芝诺军备学院的相关人员都留在了南美。
Constantine: "Admiral Igor's funeral" has been held as planned—one that befits his rank and status. All relevant personnel remained in South America for the ceremony, as per Zeno's funeral regulations.

康斯坦丁：目前新的上将人选仍在遴选中，稍后我会将他们的名单呈递给您。
Constantine: We're in the process of selecting a new admiral. I'll provide you with the candidate list shortly.

康斯坦丁：另外，我们派出了一支特殊调查小队前往火地岛，持续追查伊戈尔的动向。
Constantine: Additionally, we've dispatched an investigative team to Tierra del Fuego to search for Igor.

会长：很好。
President: Very well.

会长：那个女孩呢？
President: What about the girl?

温顺的领结迟滞了片刻。
She pauses.

康斯坦丁：女孩……洛佩拉？
Constantine: The girl? Are you referring to Lopera?

康斯坦丁：她的情绪已经稳定下来了，我们暂时将她留在南美分部。
Constantine: Her emotions have stabilized, so we've decided to leave her in South America for the moment. Of course, she'll be put through the necessary investigations as circumstances dictate.

当然，必要的调查质询无法避免。

会长：抓牢她。
President: Keep a close eye on her.

会长：噢，还有那只爱唱歌的小鸟。
President: Oh, and that little singing bird?

康斯坦丁：……
Constantine: ...

康斯坦丁不着痕迹地走近了几步，压低了声音。
Constantine takes a step closer, lowering her voice.

康斯坦丁：芝诺方对金伯利女郎的处理决定相当不满，他们坚持要求对她进行更全面的调查……
Constantine: Zeno is quite upset about our decision regarding Ms. Kimberly. They're insisting she undergoes a more thorough investigation.

康斯坦丁：我担心过度的干涉会引起芝诺的不满。
Constantine: I feared that if we gave too much pushback, they would take a more extreme stance in response. So I agreed.

会长：军人的执拗啊……
President: *sigh* Those soldiers never budge.

康斯坦丁：当然，芝诺承诺，他们对金伯利女郎的审查会在基金会的监督下进行。
Constantine: Of course, Zeno agreed that the investigation would be done under the supervision of the Foundation.

康斯坦丁：在调查结束后，她才能被正式编入司辰小队，享有相应的权利，并由司辰直接指挥。
Constantine: If nothing else comes up, she will be put into the Timekeeper's team and granted the same rights as the other members.

会长：别让维尔汀等太久。
President: Good. Don't keep Vertin waiting too long.

芝诺的棋子安全落地，康斯坦丁悄无声息地松了口气。
The Zeno piece has landed safely. Constantine gives an internal sigh of relief.

康斯坦丁：另外，接Z女士报告，司辰小队传回了新的情报。
Constantine: There's more. Madam Z has received word from the Timekeeper.

康斯坦丁：司辰在悉尼港发现了重塑之手的踪迹，他们极有可能藏身在一艘名为“自由海风号”的游轮上。
Constantine: The Timekeeper suspects Manus Vindictae is active again in Sydney Harbor. They're likely onboard a cruise ship named "Free Breeze."

康斯坦丁：这也解释了外派调查小组们调查受阻的原因，重塑伪装得很好。
Constantine: This would explain why our field investigators have been having difficulties with their tasks. Manus has covered their tracks carefully this time.

会长：船的目的地呢？
President: Where's the cruise bound for?

康斯坦丁：目前尚未查明。但从飞蛾的线报来看，“自由海风号”刚刚经过了大洋洲沿岛。
Constantine: That's still unclear, sir. However, Moth just reported in, confirming that the ship has passed the Oceania islands.

会长：嗯，漂亮的出子。
President: Hmm. An interesting development.

康斯坦丁：是。
Constantine: Indeed.

康斯坦丁的语气中藏着微不可察的骄傲。
Constantine's tone carries an imperceptible trace of pride.

会长：我们在正确的道路上快步前行，这很好。
President: We're making excellent progress. That's good.

会长：给维尔汀下达新的任务。
President: Assign a new mission to Vertin.

康斯坦丁：您的意思是派遣司辰小队登船？
Constantine: You mean, to send them on that cruise?

会长：孩子总得走出安稳的家乡啊。
President: We can't keep her under our wing forever.

康斯坦丁：……是。
Constantine: Understood.

会议室又重新安静了下来。
The conference room falls silent once more.

层叠的大理石廊柱间，有一抹雪白从窗外扑腾着飞过。
Amid the layered marble pillars, a flash of white flits past the window.

白鸽落在会长的手上，轻啄其中的掌纹。
A white dove lands on the President's hand and gently pecks at his palm.

会长：老朋友，有什么事儿需要你亲自跑一趟呢？
President: What brings you all the way over here, old friend?

他低下头去，任由对方亲昵地蹭着他的指尖。
He lowers his head, allowing the bird to nuzzle his fingertips.

会长：哦……哦……嗯……
President: Oh ... Mm ... Mm.

会长：……
President: ...

那抹雪白又轻飘飘地飞走了。
The white dove takes wing, flitting away once more.

会长：科算中心提交了关于“人工暴雨”的援助申请？
President: So, Laplace has requested the Foundation's assistance with the "Artificial Storm" project?

康斯坦丁：是的，负责这一项目的是乌尔里希。它请求基金会向科算中心澳洲分部提供一批非对称核素R，越多越好。
Constantine: Yes. Ulrich is overseeing the project and has requested as much asymmetrical nuclide R as we can spare.

康斯坦丁：另外，它希望我们的调查员能配合寻找符合实验环境的对应坐标。
Constantine: He's also requested our help in determining the most suitable location for the experiment.

康斯坦丁：我拿到过一些符合科算中心需要的资料……
Constantine: I have several in mind that should meet his needs.

康斯坦丁不由自主地停顿了片刻。
Constantine involuntarily pauses for a moment.

康斯坦丁：距离澳洲分部最近的实验坐标，正是那艘“自由海风号”。
Constantine: The location closest to Laplace's Australian branch is on the sea, right where the "Free Breeze" cruise ship happens to be.

会长：倒是很合理。
President: I see where you're going.

康斯坦丁：我担心这会牵涉到我们在重塑之手的布局。
Constantine: However, I do have concerns about how this might disrupt our current plans against Manus Vindictae.

会长：全力支持科算中心的“人工暴雨”。
President: Regardless, Laplace will have our full support for the "Artificial Storm" project.

意料之外的坚决。
Unexpected determination.

康斯坦丁：可飞蛾的状况尚不明朗。如果太过冒进……
Constantine: But Moth's status still remains unclear. If we proceed too hastily ...

康斯坦丁：它很难全身而退。
Constantine: We might jeopardize the situation.

一闪而过的犹豫落入会长的眼中。
Her fleeting hesitation catches the President's attention.

会长：我以为你早就做好了准备，我的朋友。
President: I thought you'd have foreseen something like this.

会长：命令几颗弃子不择手段地前进，接着，我们赢下整场棋局。
President: A few pieces must be sacrificed if you're to win the game.

会长：你比谁都擅长这个，对吧？
President: You know that better than anyone, don't you?

康斯坦丁：……
Constantine: ...

康斯坦丁：这是鸽子屋的意思吗？
Constantine: Is this also the Pax House's decision?

会长：是的。
President: You have my word on it.

康斯坦丁：我明白了。
Constantine: I see.

康斯坦丁：至于更多的任务细节，我会尽快知会司辰和乌尔里希。
Constantine: I'll inform the Timekeeper and Ulrich of their missions.

会长：那很好，他们的会面一定会很有趣的。
President: Thank you. I look forward to their meeting.

乌尔里希：我们又见面了，司辰。
Ulrich: We meet again, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：很高兴再见到你，乌尔里希先生。听说你和星锑的交流相当顺利？
Vertin: Pleasure's mine, Mr. Ulrich. I've heard good things about your work with Regulus.

乌尔里希：坦白说，星锑对科学进步的热情和奉献精神远超我的预料。毫不夸张地说，她是一位不求回报的伟大研究者。
Ulrich: Frankly, I was surprised by how selfless, passionate, and forward-looking she is. I'm truly grateful to have someone like her on my team.

玻璃缸里的磁流体相当稳定。
The ferrofluid is remarkably stable.

显而易见，这是一句真心话。
Clearly, this is a sincere statement.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀：“自由海风号”的情况相当复杂，我们还不清楚上面潜伏着多少重塑之手的人员。
Vertin: The situation on the "Free Breeze" is still unclear. We don't know how many Manus Vindictae followers might be on board.

维尔汀：按照计划，我们会以游客的方式登船。
Vertin: Our plan is to board the cruise as ordinary passengers.

维尔汀：星锑在“自由海风号”上有相熟的船员。她打包票，在那位朋友的帮助下，我们的登船资料已经得到了妥善的修饰，绝不会引起任何人的注意。
Vertin: Regulus said she's made acquaintance with a crew member and has made sure to alter our profiles so we don't attract any unwanted attention.

乌尔里希：了不起！原来星锑研究员申请的那一大笔经费并不只是为了个人的娱乐。
Ulrich: That's good to hear. So Regulus didn't use her money for her own amusement after all.

自言自语之余，乌尔里希终于又想起了眼下的正事。
After muttering to himself, Ulrich returns to the task at hand.

乌尔里希：我会错开你们的登船时间。
Ulrich: We should stagger our boarding times.

乌尔里希：如果发现了重塑之手的行踪，我会联络你们的。
Ulrich: I'll reach out if I spot any signs of Manus Vindictae.

乌尔里希：互通有无，朋友——！
Ulrich: Let's stay in touch. See you on board!

临行前信誓旦旦拍下的胸膛令人安心。
Ulrich gives her a reassuring pat on the shoulder.

维尔汀：我们也很乐意为你的任务提供协助……
Vertin: Mr. Ulrich, we're more than happy to assist with your mission.

乌尔里希：不、不，绝不需要！
Ulrich: Oh, no, no, no! Please, don't trouble yourself.

乌尔里希：噢，别误会，我没有轻视任何人的意思。
Ulrich: Sorry, don't get me wrong. I'd appreciate your help were the circumstances different.

乌尔里希：事实上，实验进度目前尚未对外公开。基于对“人工暴雨”项目的外部预期及风险控制，我希望你能对我们的研究进度暂时保密。
Ulrich: But the experiment is still confidential. Please don't mention it to anyone. I'd like to avoid any unnecessary risks or interference.

乌尔里希：在“自由海风号”上，我们互不相识。
Ulrich: On the cruise ship, we are but strangers.

维尔汀：……好的。
Vertin: I see.

乌尔里希：别担心，我会做好伪装工作的。
Ulrich: Don't you worry. I have a little disguise for myself, too.

LEE-06 群岛已远 / As Home Fades

大厅内吵吵嚷嚷，酒杯里晃荡的液体与叫不上名字的耳熟旋律交织在一起，显出粼粼的光彩。
The main hall is packed with passengers. Their wine sways slightly, emitting an enchanting luster in the beautiful, familiar melody.

亮眼的姑娘小心翼翼地避过兴奋的人群，像是逡巡在海中的游鱼。
Girls weave their way carefully through the excited crowd, like a school of nimble fish.

不断有绅士与淑女们向走在最前的女孩点头致意。
The passengers nod politely to the girl at the front.

客人Ⅰ：噢！芭卡洛儿小姐——您果然出现了！
Guest I: Ms. Barcarola! At last you've graced us with your presence!

客人Ⅰ：亨利先生与我打赌，我们的游轮明星决不会出现在聚光灯以外的地方，看来他要输给我一整杯威士忌了。
Guest I: Henry and I were just having a little wager on whether we'd see our musical star outside the spotlight. Looks like he'll be buying me the next round of whiskey, eh? Haha.

芭卡洛儿：当然，弗兰克先生。令每一位“自由海风号”的客人都能获得宾至如归的体验是我的责任，需要我为您的威士忌加点冰吗？
Barcarola: Ah, well bet, sir! Allow me to pour you the first glass. How do you like your whiskey? On the rocks, perhaps?

客人Ⅰ：哈哈～那可真叫人荣幸。
Guest I: Indeed, thank you, my dear.

客人Ⅱ：天呐——妈妈，您必须来看看，我发现了芭卡洛儿小姐！
Guest II: *gasp* Over here, Mum! It's Ms. Barcarola!

客人Ⅱ：上一次在港口里，芭卡洛儿小姐一个人就完成了一整支乐队的演出，我从没见过这样精彩的表演——我可没有骗您！
Guest II: Last time I saw her, she performed an entire symphony all by herself. She was the whole orchestra! I've never seen anything like it!

芭卡洛儿：你好呀，热情的小客人——我们又见面了～
Barcarola: It's good to see you again, my little friend.

一旁的妇人转过身来，怜爱地抚摸着孩子的脑袋。
The woman beside her turns around and lovingly pats the boy on the head.

客人Ⅲ：我们总算见到您了，芭卡洛儿女士。
Guest III: Ms. Barcarola, what a pleasure. I've heard so much about you.

客人Ⅲ：自从我的孩子在悉尼港和您聊天之后，他便无时无刻不在谈论着您对迪吉里杜的见解与热情……
Guest III: My child hasn't stopped talking about you since you spoke to him about the didgeridoo at Sydney Harbor.

客人Ⅲ：甚至吵着让我们买一支新的迪吉里杜带上船来～
Guest III: He was so excited by it that he begged us to bring one onboard.

芭卡洛儿：迪吉里杜确实是一件很有意思的乐器！
Barcarola: How lovely! The didgeridoo truly is an enchanting instrument.

芭卡洛儿：尽管音域不广，但胜在音色浑厚、野性而高昂……我正在尝试将它融合到啪唧匣子里，我相信它一定能和爱尔兰哨笛、卡林巴琴还有别的朋友配合得很好！
Barcarola: It's so resonant, don't you think? It almost feels like it's echoing from the depths of the earth itself. I've actually been experimenting with playing it alongside my Crackling Box. It's a wonderful match with the tin whistle and kalimba, and I'm sure a number of other instruments too!

谈及乐器上的编排，少女眼中的光芒明显热切了起来。
As she speaks, Barcarola's eyes sparkle with enthusiasm.

身旁的欢呼与喝彩声将她紧紧包裹在其中，绚丽的光芒几乎晃晕了一旁戴着墨镜的无辜游客。
The admiration surrounding her is so bright that it almost blinds the tourist standing nearby. Luckily, she's wearing sunglasses.

星锑：啧啧，看来她也是个大明星啊～
Regulus: Looks like she's pretty popular, too!

十四行诗：也……？
Sonetto: Too?

星锑：难道你忘了吗，十四行诗？我也曾在伦敦接受过万人围堵……咳、万人追捧的待遇。
Regulus: Have you forgotten, Sonetto? You're also looking at a popular public figure yourself! One that had half of London hunting, ah, oh, I mean, cheering for her.

星锑：这令我苦恼了许久～
Regulus: Ah, the bittersweet burden of fame!

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

不再关注眼前的插科打诨，维尔汀的目光转向了另一个更安静的角落。
Their attention is quickly turned to a quiet corner of the ship.

头戴树冠、服装鲜艳而充满海岛风情的人们围成一圈，暗铜色的肌肤在灯光下泛起光泽。
There's a group of people dressed in brightly colored clothes. Crowns made of leaves and flowers adorn their heads, and their bronze skin is glowing under the warm lights.

他们围成一圈，不时向四周张望，胸前的贝壳发出叮叮当当的碰响。
They stand in a circle, occasionally glancing around, the shells on their chests clinking together melodiously.

维尔汀：他们看起来很紧张……旅行中的游客会这样吗？
Vertin: That group over there seems unusually uptight.

环绕掌声与恭维的明星姑娘终于款款莅临了这一处角落。
Having absorbed all the adoration of the people around her, Barcarola makes her way over.

她当然不会忽视来自任何一位客人的疑惑。
She certainly wouldn't overlook the curiosity of any of her guests.

芭卡洛儿：他们是船长亲自邀请登船的贵宾，来自一个隐秘的小岛，努库泰澳。
Barcarola: Oh, those are the captain's special guests. They're from one of the Oceania archipelagos. Nukutaeao, I believe.

芭卡洛儿：请别多虑，努库泰澳的客人们或许只是不常与外人交流罢了。
Barcarola: They're probably just a bit nervous. I imagine they don't often find themselves among so many foreigners.

刚交代完眼前的小事，备受欢迎的乐手又被远处客人们的呼声匆匆唤走。
After handling the small matter at hand, Barcarola is hurriedly called away by the distant voices of other guests.

十四行诗：努库泰澳……
Sonetto: Nukutaeao ...

十四行诗：我曾在第一防线学校图书馆的《神秘学族群史》里听说过这个名字，他们以贝壳为信仰，生活在几座不知名的小岛上，几乎不会与外界有所交流……
Sonetto: I read about it in A History of Arcane Ethnicity back in the SPDM. It's a remote place, and its people hold a special kind of shell at the center of their beliefs. They've rarely made contact with the outside world.

十四行诗：那儿民风淳朴，与世无争，是无数诗人笔下歌颂的理想乡。
Sonetto: It's often been described as a peaceful paradise.

十四行诗：可我明明听说过……努库泰澳人从来都不会离开他们的岛……
Sonetto: I also read that the Nukutai almost never leave their homeland. Why are they here?

努库泰澳人显然听见了这儿的嘀嘀咕咕。
Their hushed conversation clearly meets the ears of the nearby Nukutai.

一个年轻的身影从人群中蹿了出来，气鼓鼓地站在十四行诗的面前。
One young boy strides forward, his chest puffed up in indignation.

托阿：努库泰澳人绝对不会抛弃自己的家园！
Toa: The Nukutai will never abandon our homeland!

托阿：等、等到了新时代，那些被淹没的海岛都会回来的！
Toa: J-Just wait. We'll find our way back when the new era comes!

维尔汀：新的时代……
Vertin: The new era ...

浸泡在陌生口音中的词汇令人耳熟。
Though in a foreign accent, these words sound all too familiar.

塞洛尼：托阿，别再解释了——图图石子告诫过我们，不要与陌生人有过多的交流。
Selone: Toa, that's enough. Tutu told us not to talk with outsiders.

另一个同样稚嫩的身影挡在了托阿的面前。
An equally young girl stands protectively in front of the boy.

托阿：可……我、我什么也没说错！
Toa: But, someone had to tell them the truth!

十四行诗：抱歉，我并不是想指责你们。我只是……
Sonetto: I apologize. I didn't mean to accuse you of anything. I was just curious.

托阿：别再假惺惺了——来自外面的家伙！
Toa: Well, next time keep your mouth shut. What could you possibly know about the Nukutai?

无端的冲突似乎一触即发。
The boy looks about ready to explode.

尚在远处寒暄的忙碌乐手匆匆赶来。
Noticing the outburst, Barcarola breaks away from the other guests and hurries over.

芭卡洛儿：客人们，请冷静下来。
Barcarola: Please, everyone, no fighting.

芭卡洛儿：我是“自由海风号”的乐队负责人，如果你们有任何感到不适的地方，请及时与我交流。
Barcarola: I'm Barcarola, the musical director. Is there anything I can help you with? I'll do all I can to ensure everyone has a pleasant experience.

在抵达目的地前，一阵清脆的贝壳碰撞声便挡住了芭卡洛儿的脚步。
Before she can reach them, a crisp collision of shells stops Barcarola in her tracks.

芭卡洛儿：……！
Barcarola: ...!

图图石子：你们想做什么——！
Fatutu: What's going on? What do you want?

稚嫩的话语毫不遮掩自己的敌意。
Her voice holds no restraint in its hostility.

塞洛尼：……图图石子！
Selone: Tutu!

图图石子：塞洛尼、托阿，小心些，外面的人比我们想象得还要可怕的多呢！
Fatutu: Selone, Toa, stay back. These outsiders could be dangerous.

芭卡洛儿：什……么？难道你不认识我吗？
Barcarola: Dangerous? Have you never heard of me before?

图图石子仔细打量着眼前一脸难以置信的少女，审视着对方身侧的古怪木匣。
Fatutu looks Barcarola over, eyeing the peculiar wooden contraption by her side.

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

她努力压抑住对眼前古怪乐器的好奇心，目光又重新坚定起来。
Suppressing her curiosity about this unique object, she steadies her gaze once more.

图图石子：不管你们是什么奇怪的家伙，请不要再靠近我们了。
Fatutu: Whoever you are, I ask that you leave us in peace.

芭卡洛儿：我……你……
Barcarola: I ... You ...

从未享受过如此待遇的芭卡洛儿一时语塞，对方的发言显然远远偏离了自己的预想。
Barcarola is lost for words. Clearly, her status as a musical star has made her unaccustomed to such remarks.

毫不顾及眼前几乎面红耳赤的少女，努库泰澳人又把自己藏进了角落里。
Ignoring the now flushed girl before her, Fatutu and the other Nukutai retreat back to their corner.

塞洛尼：还好你及时回来了，图图石子，要不然，我都不知道该怎么办才好了……
Selone: Tutu, thank the tides you came! I wasn't sure what to do.

托阿：哼！为了重建家园，我们不正是要加入格蕾丝女士的组织吗？大不了——
Toa: Hmph. So are we going to take Ms. Grace's offer or not? She promised it would bring our islands back.

少年露出一个恶狠狠的眼神。
Toa casts a fierce glare at Fatutu.

图图石子：托阿，别总是把这些事儿挂在嘴边，这样只会让外面的家伙对我们更加警惕……
Fatutu: Enough, Toa! These outsiders don't need to know why we're here. And stop mentioning Ms. Grace. Could draw unwanted attention.

托阿：难道你不想回到努库泰澳吗——？
Toa: But what's there to hide? There's no shame in wanting our home back.

托阿：如果我们不加入格蕾丝女士的复仇大业，我们可就永远没法回归家园了！
Toa: If we don't stand with Ms. Grace, we'll lose Nukutaeao forever!

图图石子：我比任何人都更希望回到那儿……我想念麦黎，我想念岛上的红珊瑚，想念那儿的独木舟赛……
Fatutu: I want to go home too, probably more than anyone! I already miss Meli's red coral reefs, blue sea, and canoe races.

图图石子：相信我，一切都会好起来的，托阿。等回到努库泰澳，咱们还可以继续当邻居，采摘面包果和椰树花，除了复仇，我们眼下还有很多的事儿可以做。
Fatutu: We'll get through this, Toa. I promise we'll be neighbors again, picking breadfruit and coconut flowers together. But before we accept Ms. Grace's offer, there's a few things that need to be made clear.

图图石子：更重要的是，这些事都与船上的其他人无关，不是么？
Fatutu: And remember, none of these passengers are to blame for what happened to our home, okay?

塞洛尼：可……格蕾丝女士不是这么说的。
Selone: But Ms. Grace has offered us a way home.

塞洛尼：那美好的时代有永恒的时间，无损的昔日家园……是努库泰澳人真正的应许之地……
Selone: We'll have our islands back, just as they were. Our promised land.

图图石子：我们一定会回家的，塞洛尼，我向你们保证。
Fatutu: We will go home, Selone. Trust me.

图图石子：只是、只是……在这之前，我们得先弄明白更多的事。
Fatutu: I just need to figure out a few things first.

图图石子：关于格蕾丝女士所说的一切。
Fatutu: Starting with this "wonderful new era" she keeps talking about.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

淑女格蕾丝：您看上去很焦急，卡穆塔先生。
Ms. Grace: You seem a little on edge, Chief Kamuta.

一个壮硕的身影在不大的房间里来回踱步。
Kamuta is pacing back and forth in the cabin.

卡穆塔：格蕾丝女士，我们什么时候才能抵达您承诺的新时代？
Kamuta: Ms. Grace, how much longer do we have to wait for this new era to come?

卡穆塔：您知道的，我们的许多族人几乎从未离开过努库泰澳，他们的身体状况很差，已经有不少人出现晕船、高烧等问题了……像这样海上漂流的日子显然让人难以承受。
Kamuta: Many of our people have never left Nukutaeao before. We're struggling to adjust. Some have even fallen sick. We can't stay adrift on the sea like this much longer.

卡穆塔：不少人都郁郁寡欢，我甚至已经能从他们的“象形贝壳”看到那些阴郁扭曲的裂纹了……
Kamuta: Our spirits are low. The shells of some of my people have begun to crack.

他埋下头去，一串串纹理细腻的规整贝壳散发着微光，在手中微微发烫。
He lowers his head to the faintly glowing shells in his palm. They radiate warmth.

卡穆塔：并非所有人都身强力壮，能挺过船上这段难熬的日子……请帮帮我们，格蕾丝女士。
Kamuta: Not everyone is strong enough to endure this journey. Please, Ms. Grace. You have to help us.

淑女格蕾丝：我很遗憾得知这一切。
Ms. Grace: While it pains me to hear this ...

淑女格蕾丝：“自由海风号”上仍有不少尚未使用的区域，我们可以提供遗体收殓场地。当然，也包括遗物保管等服务……
Ms. Grace: The journey must go on. You have nowhere to return to, after all. We still have some space below deck. You can use it to store your people's bodies should they die.

她的目光始终停留在那些晶莹的贝壳上。
Her gaze remains fixed on the crystalline shells in Kamuta's hand.

卡穆塔：不……这些并不是我们真正需要的……
Kamuta: That's not exactly what we're asking for.

卡穆塔：我恳求您，愿您能给予我们新的指引……正如您预言麦黎的沉没那般。
Kamuta: Please, show us another way. Help us like you did when you foresaw the destruction of Meli. I beg of you.

格蕾丝侧过头来，饶有兴趣地打量着眼前这副痛苦的面容。
Grace tilts her head, a glimmer of intrigue on her face as she observes the pained expression on Kamuta's face.

淑女格蕾丝：我早已给过你们方向了，不是么？
Ms. Grace: I've already shown you a way, haven't I?

卡穆塔：——！
Kamuta: ...!

胸膛传来一阵突兀的压迫感，某种黏稠的液体悄然攀上了他的肌肤。
A sudden pressure swells in his chest as a sticky black liquid silently drips onto his skin.

卡穆塔：您说的是……加入重塑？
Kamuta: You mean joining the Manus?

卡穆塔：……
Kamuta: ...

卡穆塔：努库泰澳人向来厌恶纷争，我们藏身于无人知晓的岛屿，几乎不在外界露面……
Kamuta: But the Nukutai haven't had a conflict with anyone for centuries. That's why we hid ourselves away from the world.

卡穆塔：……我很难说服其他族人们。
Kamuta: Difficult to persuade my people to do this.

卡穆塔：我们只是希望族人的魂灵与躯体回到我们熟悉的故土，希望能有一处不被打扰的家园……
Kamuta: All we want is for our people to return to familiar soil, to feel our spirits at home. Nothing more.

淑女格蕾丝：麦黎已经被淹没了。
Ms. Grace: But Meli is already gone.

卡穆塔：那是一场天灾……我们无法责怪任何人……
Kamuta: Yes, but that doesn't mean we should take revenge on the outside world. It was an act of the sea itself. It would be unjust to blame anyone for it.

淑女格蕾丝：被划为鱼雷试验场的马拉尼亚环礁和维布那也是么？
Ms. Grace: What about the torpedo test sites designated over Malaga and Vaipuna? Aren't there people who should answer for that?

卡穆塔：他们……只是无意的……
Kamuta: It was probably just a mistake.

卡穆塔：那片海域是努库泰澳的外围区域，几乎没人到那儿捕鱼……外面的人根本没有意识到努库泰澳人的存在。
Kamuta: The area they chose was far from the main islands of Nukutaeao, and hardly anyone fishes there. They may not have realized that my people lived there.

淑女格蕾丝：倾倒的污水、泄露的油船……那些因此死去的可怜鱼群，它们也就该如此么？
Ms. Grace: And the oil spill? The wastewater discharge? Were all those fish killed by pollution also just an "act of the sea"?

卡穆塔：我们……不想与任何人为敌。
Kamuta: I ... Please ... We're not looking for conflict.

淑女格蕾丝：当然，他们在无声无息间摧毁了你们赖以生存的一切——
Ms. Grace: Of course you're not. After all, they've only stolen everything you've ever held dear ...

她的声突兀地放低了，却像是一片挠人心肝的羽毛。
Her voice drops abruptly, her next words delivered with the lightness of a feather.

淑女格蕾丝：尽管他们对努库泰澳一无所知。
Ms. Grace: ... and arrogantly assumed every inch of this planet is theirs to exploit.

卡穆塔：……
Kamuta: ...

淑女格蕾丝：战争从来不会停下，不论你们身处何地……努库泰澳人。
Ms. Grace: War is inevitable, whether you want it or not, Nukutai.

那副面具被轻轻推上前来，连上面泛着的冷光都清晰可见了。
She gently pushes the mask forward. Its dark presence is unavoidable.

淑女格蕾丝：时间站在我们这边，卡穆塔先生。
Ms. Grace: But if you join us, you will have an invaluable ally: time.

格蕾丝瞥了瞥手中的怀表，又轻飘飘将它放进了口袋。
Grace glances at her pocket watch before slipping it lightly into her pocket.

淑女格蕾丝：但它的慷慨可不会持续太久。
Ms. Grace: The window is closing.

淑女格蕾丝：“大筛选”快要开始了。
Ms. Grace: The sifting is about to begin.

胸前的“象形贝壳”滚烫如火，那些扭曲而狰狞的象形文字热切地攀附上来。

像是在催促，又像是在预言。
Both a prompt and a prophecy.

卡穆塔：…………
Kamuta: ...

胸前的“象形贝壳”滚烫如火，那些扭曲而狰狞的象形文字热切地攀附上来。
The Spirit Shells around Kamuta's neck burn. They cling to his chest as they twist with ferocity.

卡穆塔：……这是复仇么？
Kamuta: Has it really come to this? To revenge?

他猛然抬起头来，正对上桌上那副张牙舞爪的冰冷面具。
His eyes flash up to the jagged mask on the table.

狰狞的触须向四周无规则地延伸着，像是一种无言的引诱。
Dark tendrils extend from it, groping at the air in a silent invitation.

几乎要灼伤他胸口的“象形贝壳”。
His Spirit Shells are almost scorching.

淑女格蕾丝：不，这是一场拯救。
Ms. Grace: Oh no, it's quite the opposite. It's salvation.

LEE-07 音乐或亮光 / Music or Light

大厅里挤满了人，却罕见地没有演奏任何音乐。
The main hall is packed with people, yet there is no music to be heard. A peculiar scene indeed.

好在客人们并不因此感到无聊，别的舞台上可找不到这样一场精彩的情景剧。
Fortunately, the guests don't seem to mind. There is no stage in the world that offers a performance like this one.

芭卡洛儿：星锑小姐，你应该明白，一首完美的协奏曲需要多么精妙的排布、天才的想法和精湛的演奏技巧——
Barcarola: Ms. Regulus, as I'm sure you understand, there's a great deal of effort involved in creating a concerto, from the initial spark of inspiration to the careful arrangement of the music to the skill required to play it.

芭卡洛儿：这些音乐能够诞生，本身已经是最伟大的奇迹了！
Barcarola: The fact that any concerto has ever been performed at all is nothing short of a miracle!

芭卡洛儿的语气相当郑重，像是一曲渐强的行进乐。
Barcarola's tone is solemn, like a steadily intensifying march.

芭卡洛儿：身为乐队负责人，我必须选择合适的曲目，并将它演绎给每一位听众。
Barcarola: As musical director, it is my duty to select the perfect repertoire to bring delight to every listener.

芭卡洛儿：而“自由海风号”尊贵的客人，需要做的应该是端坐在座位上，享用热腾腾的苹果派，安静地欣赏音乐。
Barcarola: Then, the esteemed passengers of the "Free Breeze" can enjoy their dessert and wine with the finest musical accompaniment.

星锑：噢不——坐在座位上听曲子是最无聊透顶的事儿了！
Regulus: Oh, you can't be serious. Where's the fun in just sitting there and listening?

星锑：我向你保证，这儿的客人们一定听腻了那些懒洋洋的爵士、黏糊糊的钢琴曲，或者滋滋冒烟的电子乐！
Regulus: I promise you, this lot have had more than enough lazy jazz and swooning piano to last a lifetime!

星锑：为了让这趟旅程成为20世纪末最伟大的一次航行，我们必须要做出改变！
Regulus: We need to shake things up—make this voyage the greatest of the century!

星锑：比如，一场来自60年代的摇滚运动！
Regulus: How about some '60s rock?

星锑：而最最最具先见之明的前船长星锑恰巧准备了一台最棒的唱片机～
Regulus: And wouldn't you know it? This visionary former captain has a record player right here with her!

一沓唱片被高高扬起。
She holds a stack of records high in the air.

星锑：朋友们，欢呼起来！
Regulus: Alright, people! Let me hear you cheer!

星锑：音乐不需要条条框框，它能在任何时候、任何地方感染每一个人！
Regulus: Music is freedom! It should stir the soul, anytime, anywhere!

芭卡洛儿：嘿——放下它，星锑，我才是这儿的乐手！
Barcarola: Stop, Regulus! I'm the musician here, not you!

难得一见的通红映在芭卡洛儿的脸上。
Barcarola's cheeks flush red.

客人们饶有兴趣地为台上的闹剧鼓掌，一顶小巧的珊瑚花编帽不着痕迹地藏在当中。
The audience claps, amused by the antics on stage. A small flower-adorned girl sits discreetly among them.

图图石子：外面的世界很闹腾，可……
Fatutu: These outsiders seem so full of life.

图图石子：她们一点儿也不像格蕾丝女士说的那样“充斥着仇恨与战火”呀……
Fatutu: They're nothing like what Ms. Grace described, "full of hatred and hostility."

图图石子仍然警惕地望着台上，目光始终不曾挪开分毫。
Fatutu remains alert, her eyes fixed on the stage.

芭卡洛儿：这儿是我的舞台……如、如果你实在想要播放摇滚乐，你也可以向船长申请，成为一名优秀的游轮乐手！
Barcarola: This is my performance! If you really must share your music with us, then, perhaps you should go to the captain and apply to be a cruise musician like me!

星锑：向你致敬，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Regulus: With all due respect, Ms. Barcarola.

星锑：但——
Regulus: The point I'm trying to make ...

星锑：电台骑师知道客人们真正想听到的是什么～
Regulus: ... is that only a DJ knows what the crowd really wants!

罔顾惊声冲上前来的白天鹅，狡猾的小狮子早已按下了唱片机的播放键。
Before Barcarola can protest anymore, the cunning little lion presses the play button on the record player.

“啪嗒——”

四周的灯光突兀地暗了下去，不着调的电台骑师从未意识到自己的唱片机还有如此功效。
In a moment, all the lights on the ship have gone out. Regulus had no idea her record player could produce such effects.

星锑：……？
Regulus: Huh?

星锑：难道我真是神秘学天才？
Regulus: Did I just shoot lightning bolts from my fingertips?

芭卡洛儿：当然不是！
Barcarola: Of course not!

芭卡洛儿终于夺回了麦克风的掌控权，但此刻客人们显然面临着更严重的问题。
Barcarola finally manages to wrest the microphone from Regulus's hand, but a far more pressing issue than the content of the concert now faces them.

漆黑一片的船舱中，呼喊与抱怨声此起彼伏。
Amid the darkness, discontent quickly arises.

客人Ⅰ：该死的，谁踩了我的高档皮鞋？！
Guest I: Goddamn! Who's stepping on my brand-new leather shoes?!

客人Ⅰ：你们就不能小心点儿么？
Guest I: Will you please watch yourself?!

客人Ⅱ：这正是我要说的话——你这个慌慌张张的笨家伙，你扯着我的夹克衫扣带了！
Guest II: I was just about to say the same thing! Let go of my jacket, you moron!

客人Ⅲ：闭嘴，伙计们！别在这儿吵吵嚷嚷的，我什么也听不清了！
Guest III: Could you all keep it down? I'm going deaf here!

客人Ⅲ：噢，天呐——我的白葡萄酒和帕玛尔干酪！
Guest III: Oh, no! My wine! And the cheese platter!

争吵声几乎塞满了耳膜。
The clamor of irritated voices quickly fills the space.

芭卡洛儿：这样下去很可能会发生更大的事故……不行，有我在的航程决不能有如此灾难！
Barcarola: This could turn to total chaos before long. No, I can't let that happen!

芭卡洛儿：我得赶紧去电闸那儿看看。
Barcarola: I must go check on the master switch.

芭卡洛儿摸黑挤进人群，努力寻找去往电力供应室的通路。
Barcarola pushes through the crowd as she carves a path to the power room.

星锑：嘿，芭卡洛儿小姐！
Regulus: Hey! Ms. Barcarola!

芭卡洛儿：唔——别再挤过来了，伊丽莎白女士。
Barcarola: Uh. Please let me through, Ms. Elisabeth.

遗憾的是，在如此漆黑的环境中，人们很难分辨出一颗海上明珠。
Unfortunately, the guests can't tell a musician from a mechanic through the darkness.

星锑：芭卡洛儿，你打算去哪儿——！
Regulus: Barcarola! Where are you going?!

星锑：本海盗很乐意为你提供帮助。
Regulus: Let me give you a hand!

星锑：往这儿来——芭卡洛儿～我找到一个空隙！
Regulus: Come on! There aren't as many of them this way!

芭卡洛儿：真不可思议……难道你真有什么从混乱中逃脱的天赋吗？
Barcarola: Unbelievable. It's like you're an escape artist or something!

星锑：咳、我拒绝回答这一问题。
Regulus: Uh. I'll take that as a compliment.

芭卡洛儿：总而言之……感谢你的帮忙，星锑小姐！
Barcarola: It is a compliment! Thank you so much, Ms. Regulus.

一条勉强可以通行的前路显露了出来，不顾礼仪的乐手奋力地向前挤去。
A narrow path appears, and Barcarola unceremoniously pushes forward with all her might.

但意外总是源源不断。
But it seems the surprises for today are far from coming to an end.

芭卡洛儿：啊——
Barcarola: Ah!

？？？：——！
???: ...!

一阵微弱的亮光闪过芭卡洛儿的视野，随后迅速砸到了地上。
A faint light flickers across Barcarola's vision, then quickly falls to the ground.

芭卡洛儿：……这是？
Barcarola: What was that?

半截粗糙的树皮被扭成了灯罩的造型，一朵形如罗盘的草根在当中燃烧着，火光微弱却慷慨地照亮了四周的角落。
A piece of rough bark twisted into the shape of a lampshade, with a compass-like root burning warmly inside, shines through the darkness.

塞洛尼：图图石子……你没事吧？
Selone: Tutu. Are you okay?

图图石子：没关系——我们的“罗盘灼灼”没摔坏吧？
Fatutu: I'm fine. How's the Sea Mother's Eye?

塞洛尼：当然，这可是努库泰澳人最骄傲的手艺之一！
Selone: Solid as ever, of course. It takes more than a few knocks to damage Nukutai craftsmanship!

托阿：哼，我早就说过，我们不应该靠近这些粗鲁的家伙……
Toa: *sneer* I knew getting too close to those oafs would bring trouble.

芭卡洛儿：粗鲁……家伙……
Barcarola: Oafs?

芭卡洛儿：——等等，你说的该不会是我吧！
Barcarola: Are you calling me stupid?!

在气氛朝着更难以预料的局面演变前，那盏造型古怪的灯具被拾了起来。
Before the situation can escalate any further, Barcarola picks up the oddly shaped lamp.

一团微弱的火光照亮了芭卡洛儿的视野。
She is quickly basked in its glow.

芭卡洛儿：这是……？
Barcarola: What's this?

托阿：粗鲁的笨家伙，你当然没见过这个！
Toa: Hah! What did I say? Of course you have no idea what this is.

图图石子：我们收集棕榈树的树皮，将它们打磨成一个个椰子壳大小的灯罩。接着，我们会将油脂浸泡过的罗盘草系在灯罩里……
Fatutu: We form palm bark into lampshades about the size of a coconut, then tie fat-soaked compass grass inside.

图图石子：每一位努库泰澳人都擅长制作“罗盘灼灼”。
Fatutu: We call it Sea Mother's Eye. Every Nukutai knows how to make one.

托阿：哼，它可比外面这些滋滋作响的玻璃泡可靠多了！
Toa: They're way better than those noisy, buzzing lightbulbs!

托阿：等等，图图石子！我们干嘛要告诉她这些……
Toa: Wait, why are we even telling her this?

图图石子：嘘——
Fatutu: Shh.

更急切的话语尚未从口中蹦出，图图石子赶忙把托阿扯到一边。
Before he can say another word, Fatutu hastily pulls Toa aside.

图图石子：这当然是为了让外面的家伙放松警惕。
Fatutu: We need to lower their guard.

托阿：……嗯？
Toa: Huh?

几簇狐疑的目光盯住了图图石子。
Toa eyes Fatutu suspiciously.

图图石子：这是为了骗取她们的信任。
Fatutu: So that we can earn their trust.

图图石子：如果对可能的敌人一无所知，我们又怎么能帮助格蕾丝船长，怎么能完成重建家园的使命呢？
Fatutu: If we don't understand our enemies, how can we help Ms. Grace with her mission and rebuild our home?

托阿：噢……
Toa: Oh ...

图图石子：更何况，那些笨家伙们叽里呱啦的动静会影响到族人们的休息！
Fatutu: Besides, we can't just leave them to shout and run around! It'll disturb our people's rest!

狐疑目光的源头终于松了口气。
Toa finally breathes a sigh of relief.

图图石子：相信我——过不了多久，那个单纯的家伙就会跑来找我们道谢。
Fatutu: Trust me. That girl will thank us for this later.

图图石子：到时候，她就会把自己知道的一切都统统告诉我们啦～
Fatutu: And then, we can get all the information we need from her!

托阿：所以我们应该制作更多的“罗盘灼灼”，将它们分发给更多的笨家伙们！
Toa: Then, we should make more Sea Mother's Eyes and hand them out to the outsiders!

图图石子：……没错。
Fatutu: Now you've got it.

塞洛尼：天呐，图图石子，你真聪明……怪不得长老们都愿意听你的主意呢～
Selone: By the waves, Tutu, you really are clever! No wonder the elders always listen to you.

备受褒奖的图图石子转过身去，悄悄捏紧了衣角。
Despite this praise, Fatutu turns away, a quiet look of doubt on her face.

图图石子：我……
Fatutu: I ...

图图石子：这样是对的吗？
Fatutu: Is this really the right thing to do?

无论如何，窸窣的、摩擦树皮的声响总算是传递开来了。
Regardless, the sound of bark scraping grows as her people get to work.

一盏盏“罗盘灼灼”亮了起来。
One by one, the Sea Mother's Eyes light up.

它经由一双双或粗糙或柔嫩的手，映出红褐色的肌肤、亚麻色的瞳仁与棕黄色的头发。
They are passed through rough and soft hands alike, illuminating bronze skin, flax-colored irises, and chestnut hair.

微弱的光芒顺着人流向四周飘散，它掩去吵嚷的人声，盖过张皇失措的呼喊，将素不相识的人们牵引在一起。
As the warm lights make their way through the crowd, the clamor subsides. No more panicked shouts, no more arguments, only a unique harmony.

船员Ⅰ：这个小家伙的样子可真别致，让我想起了还在渔船上的日子……那会儿我总期待着返航时那座同样怪模怪样的灯塔。
Crew Member I: What peculiar little things. Reminds me of my days on the fishing boat. I always loved spotting the lighthouse on our way back. These look just like it.

客人Ⅰ：瞧瞧这手艺，工厂里那些笨头笨脑的铁疙瘩可压不出这样的弧线～
Guest I: The craftsmanship is remarkable. You'd be hard-pressed to find something of this standard in a factory these days.

船员Ⅱ：它像极了我祖母的手笔，她总在我小时候和我一起编织各种有趣的小玩意儿！
Crew Member II: They remind me of the things my grandma and I used to make when I was little.

船员Ⅱ：哈哈～你们绝对想不到防风草做成的口哨——！
Crew Member II: Haha, she could even carve a whistle out of a parsnip!

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

图图石子：传递食物与火光，分享有意思的事儿……这和我们的篝火大会有什么不同呢？
Fatutu: They're sharing food and stories, just like we do on bonfire nights.

图图石子偷偷瞥了眼身边的努库泰澳同胞，回忆与向往写满了许多人的脸庞。
Fatutu glances at her fellow Nukutai. Relived memories and longing are etched into their faces.

图图石子：格蕾丝女士，我越来越不明白了……
Fatutu: I'm getting more and more confused by Ms. Grace's words.

狼狈的客人们三三两两地倚靠在一起，点亮了四周的微光。
The guests lean on one another, chatting happily under the warm glow of the lamps.

客人Ⅱ：芭卡洛儿小姐……
Guest II: Ms. Barcarola.

怯生生的童稚话语在游轮乐手的耳畔响起。
The timid voice of a child reaches Barcarola's ears.

客人Ⅱ：我……我想家了……
Guest II: I ... I wanna go home.

芭卡洛儿：……
Barcarola: ...

眼前的景象一片狼藉，这儿当然不是一个合适的交响乐演奏场合。
The scene before her is a mess. This is certainly no time for a symphony performance.

身穿红蓝色波点裙的摇滚少女在人群中摇晃着脑袋。
Among the crowd, she sees Regulus shaking her head.

芭卡洛儿：这也是成为音乐大师的必经之路吗？
Barcarola: Is this one of the changes I must make to truly embrace music?

芭卡洛儿：♪——
Barcarola: ♪ ...

一个略显颤抖的音符从巨大的匣子里飘荡而出。
A single note drifts from her Crackling Box.

紧接着，是更加欢乐、热闹的迥异音色。
Then, a harmonious melody of joyful, lively, and contrasting sounds.

星锑：哇噢噢噢——！
Regulus: Woah!!

在扑闪扑闪的火光中，人们不约而同地打起了拍子。
Their joy illuminated by the lamps, the guests start to clap along.

通讯员：以下是来自格蕾丝船长的紧急通报——
Broadcast: Attention, passengers!

通讯员：我们已经确认“自由海风号”当前的停电状况。经排查，该问题是由于底部货舱漏液导致的保险丝熔断，现已解决。
Broadcast: The "Free Breeze" is currently experiencing a power outage due to a fuse blown by a cargo leak in the lower deck. We ask that everyone remain calm.

通讯员：为表歉意，我们将向全船乘客发放不限量的免费冰淇淋。
Broadcast: We sincerely apologize for the inconvenience. To make your wait more comfortable, we'll be offering unlimited ice cream shortly.

通讯员：另外，我们即将驶入巨齿飞鳐的聚集区，路程中很有可能会出现颠簸情况，并产生不可避免的驱逐噪音。
Broadcast: Additionally, since we're approaching the habitat of the Serres, we're expecting an increase in turbulence and noise as we work to ward them off.

通讯员：烦请各位谅解。
Broadcast: We appreciate your understanding.

通讯员：……
Broadcast: ...

船舱又明亮了起来，客人们互相告别，那些小巧的提灯仍被紧握在一双双手中。
The hall brightens again, and the guests bid one another farewell, the lamps still tightly held in their hands.

芭卡洛儿长舒了口气，海盗得意洋洋地凑近了她。
Barcarola exhales deeply as Regulus approaches her, a smug look on her face.

星锑：嘿，朋友，我说的没错吧～
Regulus: See? What did I tell you?

星锑：在任何时候，我们都应该来点儿音乐！
Regulus: Music works wonders, anytime, anywhere!

芭卡洛儿：你是对的，星锑小姐。
Barcarola: You were right, Ms. Regulus.

星锑：那作为报酬，你是不是应该……
Regulus: You owe me one now. So, how about a little reciprocity?

狡诈的海盗搓了搓手指。
She rubs her fingers together mischievously.

星锑：比如说，一场盛大的海上摇滚革命——！
Regulus: Say, letting me have a rock session on the ship?

芭卡洛儿：你只是打算宣传你的摇滚乐，而不会搞出什么新的乱子？
Barcarola: Do you promise you won't cause any trouble?

星锑：当然～
Regulus: Cross my heart!

芭卡洛儿：好吧，我可以答应你，但是——
Barcarola: Alright, you can do it. But—

兴奋的海盗根本不在乎多余的要求，远远抛下一句热情的提醒便欢呼而去。
Permission granted, Regulus doesn't wait to hear her extra condition. She's already dashed off, speaking as she goes.

星锑：别忘了那位提灯小姐的帮助～
Regulus: Don't forget to thank the girl who made the lamp!

芭卡洛儿：……
Barcarola: ...

芭卡洛儿：哼……一位成熟的乐手才不需要这种简单的提醒，那是我的下一个目的地！
Barcarola: As if I need you to remind me! I'll have you know I was just about to head over to her.

芭卡洛儿步伐轻快地迈向阴影中的一角，努库泰澳的朋友们熟悉的隐秘角落。
Barcarola gently paces over to the darkened corner that has become the gathering place of the Nukutai.

托阿：——！
Toa: ...!

托阿：图图石子说的一点儿也没错，这位单纯的女士果然过来了！
Toa: Tutu was right! The stupid girl's back!

塞洛尼：嘘……！
Selone: Shh!

芭卡洛儿：……？
Barcarola: ...?

芭卡洛儿：事先声明，我绝不接受你们给我贴上“粗鲁”、“笨家伙”的标签。
Barcarola: I must say I don't appreciate being called an "oaf" or "stupid."

芭卡洛儿：但我发自内心地为你们的勇敢援助表示真诚的感谢。
Barcarola: But I would like to thank you for your help back there.

托阿：——什么？
Toa: What?

芭卡洛儿：我代表全体船员向你们致敬。
Barcarola: On behalf of the whole crew, you have our respect.

托阿：等等……我们该怎么办？！
Toa: Oh. Uh, what do we do now?

托阿：图图石子可没说过外面的人会这么热情呀……
Toa: Tutu never said they'd be so friendly.

手足无措的人们面面相觑。
The bewildered islanders exchange glances.

塞洛尼：图图石子……
Selone: Tutu?

塞洛尼：嗯……图图石子去哪儿了？
Selone: Where did she go?

LEE-08 老调子 / An Old Song at Sea

图图石子：我了解了更多关于外面的事，可为什么……
Fatutu: I've learned so much about the outside world since I boarded this ship, so ...

图图石子：脑袋里的问题一点儿都没有减少呢？
Fatutu: Why do I feel even more confused?

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

图图石子：努库泰澳的大家当然是好人。
Fatutu: I trust my people. They're good and kind, and they've never lied to me.

图图石子：我们有最了不起的“象形贝壳”——麦黎的舞蹈与合唱将滋养它们的外壳，纯粹而高涨的情感能够为它们晕染出最优美的纹理。
Fatutu: You just have to look at their Spirit Shells to see it. The songs and dances of Meli nourish the Shells, and the purity of my people's souls color their surface in the most beautiful patterns.

图图石子：格蕾丝女士呢？
Fatutu: And Ms. Grace, she's been good to us, too.

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

图图石子：她预言了麦黎的淹没，从洪水与风暴中拯救了我们，她向我们揭露世界的真相……
Fatutu: She warned us about the destruction of Meli, saving us from the flood. And she showed us the world as it really is.

图图石子：她，希望我们加入重塑之手的复仇计划。
Fatutu: She even wants us to be part of her plan.

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

图图石子：祖辈们留下的贝壳告诉我们，努库泰澳外面的世界有多么可怕，有信奉黑暗的邪恶女巫，有盘踞在海上的纳卡鲁瓦蛇，有轰隆隆的怪物与巨鸟。
Fatutu: Our ancestral shells have also told us how terrible the world outside is—that it's a place with sanguma witches, Nakarua serpents, and all kinds of other beasts.

图图石子：可……
Fatutu: But ...

舷窗里的一幕幕倒映在她的眼中。
Those scenes replay again and again in her mind.

寻常的寒暄，温暖的笑容，一盏盏昏黄的灯，向她伸出的手。
The casual conversations, the warm smiles, and the glowing lamps in their hands.

图图石子：外面的人们……与努库泰澳的大家，真的有什么不可逾越的差别么？
