Fatutu: But now I'm here, on this ship full of outsiders, and I feel that they're just like us.

过往与当下在恍惚中重叠在一起，令人耳晕目眩。
Past and present blur together as Fatutu searches her memories, leaving her dizzy and overwhelmed.

女孩在不知名的角落里愣神，一声嗓音浑厚的呼唤惊醒了她。
In her daze, she has wandered into another part of the ship. It isn't until a voice snaps her out of her thoughts that she realizes where she is.

舵手伊萨姆：嘿！小姑娘，你在做什么呢？
Helmsman Esam: Hello, young lady! What are you doing out here all by yourself?

舵手伊萨姆：别在外头站着啦，到这儿来～
Helmsman Esam: Don't just stand there. Come on in!

图图石子：——！
Fatutu: Hmm?

图图石子：我……抱歉，我有点走神了。
Fatutu: Sorry, I didn't even realize where I was going.

在眼前不断打着晃的蓝色水手帽惊醒了她。
One helmsman gives her a hearty pat on the shoulder.

舵手老查理：没什么好抱歉的，小客人。
Helmsman Charlie: No need to apologize, my dear.

舵手老查理：要不是你，咱们可就得一直在这儿孤零零地呆到下一个港口了。
Helmsman Charlie: You're more than welcome. You've saved us old folks from sitting here in silence till we reach shore.

舵手乔瓦尼：哈哈～别见怪，老查理总算逮住了一个吹嘘自己的好机会。
Helmsman Giovanni: Haha! Charlie's just happy to have someone new to tell his stories to!

舵手老查理：伊萨姆，难道你不想让客人看看你是如何驱赶那些热情过剩的巨齿飞鳐吗？
Helmsman Charlie: I bet Esam will jump at the chance to show off how he drives off those Serres, too.

图图石子：巨齿飞鳐，是那些热衷与海船搏击，给水手们捣乱的坏家伙——？！
Fatutu: Serres? I've heard they're a real headache for passing ships.

图图石子：我还从来没见过任何一只真正的巨齿飞鳐呢……
Fatutu: But I've never seen one with my own eyes.

图图石子好奇地望向窗外。
Fatutu curiously peers out the window.

某种古怪而熟悉的低吟呜呜作响。
A strange yet familiar hum fills the air.

巨齿飞鳐：#&呜@/——！
Serres: *roar*

舵手老查理：瞧瞧，咱们可是碰上了一位见多识广的小姑娘啦～
Helmsman Charlie: Well, well, it seems this young lady knows a thing or two about the sea!

舵手伊萨姆：那这位幸运的客人，小海怪专家——你愿意帮我们搭把手吗？
Helmsman Esam: How about you give us a hand, eh?

图图石子：我……
Fatutu: I ...

一双粗糙的手伸到了她的面前。
He extends a rough hand to her.

图图石子慌忙退了两步，可那双手却毫不动摇，仍然热情地停在她的眼前。
Fatutu takes a hasty step back, but the hand remains warmly held out before her.

那是一双令人眼熟而亲切的手，图图石子见过无数类似的老茧，在佩纽奶奶、塔雷克叔叔、纳塔诺爷爷以及更多努库泰澳人的手上。
She has seen many hands like his before. Callused, working hands, like those of Grandma Penu, Uncle Tarek, Grandpa Natano, and many of the other Nukutai. There's something comforting in its familiarity.

图图石子：……我可以么？
Fatutu: Me? I'm not sure I know how to ...

舵手老查理：放心吧，这一点儿也不难～
Helmsman Charlie: Don't worry. It's almost too easy!

舵手乔瓦尼：巨齿飞鳐畏惧噪音，而咱们的“自由海风号”，最不缺的就是扩音喇叭！
Helmsman Giovanni: These Serres are afraid of loud noises, and the "Free Breeze" has plenty of speakers on board!

舵手乔瓦尼：更何况，我们的大海母亲会保佑我们的。
Helmsman Giovanni: The sea is with us today.

舵手伊萨姆：当然，还有比咱们更虔诚的子民吗？
Helmsman Esam: Of course it is! For how long we've sailed its waves, why wouldn't it be?

水手们互相挤眉弄眼，一种无言的亲切感从勾肩搭背的呼喊中传递了出来。
The helmsmen exchange a few winks and shoulder pats. There is a clear camaraderie between them.

他们摩拳擦掌，像是在筹备一场即将到来的演出。
They roll up their sleeves as they prepare for their performance.

舵手伊萨姆：准备好，伙计们！
Helmsman Esam: Get ready, folks! Port the helm!

满舵——！

舵手伊萨姆：改变航向至二七零度，右满舵。
Helmsman Esam: Course 270, hard starboard!

舵手伊萨姆：将航速减至五节，注意艏向波！
Helmsman Esam: Slow down to five knots. Watch the bow wave!

舵手伊萨姆：打开扩音器，准备驱逐海怪。
Helmsman Esam: Turn on the speakers! Time to chase off some sea monsters.

一条条指令在老练的引航员口中有条不紊地发出。
The seasoned navigator issues a steady flow of instructions.

游轮缓缓转向，巧妙地避开了莫阿纳海怪“触手”可及的范围。
The cruise ship slowly turns, skillfully avoiding the reach of the sea monster's "tentacles."

舵手乔瓦尼：会吹这个么，小姑娘？
Helmsman Giovanni: Little girl!

一枚口琴被递到了她的面前。
He gives Fatutu a harmonica and asks if she can play it.

图图石子：我不擅长……
Fatutu: Uh ... No ...

舵手老查理：别担心，小客人。不论吹得怎么样，我想都不会比伊萨姆制造的噪音更可怕了～
Helmsman Charlie: Don't worry. Anything you play will do. Can't be worse than what Esam has to offer.

舵手伊萨姆：咳咳——！
Helmsman Esam: I can hear you, you know!

海员们相互打趣，争先恐后地挤在了麦克风前面。
The sailors joke and jostle as they clamor for their respective instruments.

舵手众：当远离故乡 我多么悲伤
Helmsmen: I grieve to leave my native home.

舵手众：当告别亲朋 我多么悲伤
Helmsmen: I grieve to leave my comrades all.

突然响起的合唱声几乎震破了图图石子的耳膜。
They burst into song.

舵手伊萨姆：小姑娘，快来～
Helmsman Esam: Come on, join in!

不知不觉间，那枚口琴附在了她的嘴边。
The harmonica finds its way to her lips.

悠扬的口风笛声，跑调却热忱的歌声，随着风遥遥吹向海面。
Melodious music, off-key yet heartfelt, drifts out toward the sea.

麦黎常有如此的篝火盛会。
This is just like those nights by the bonfire in Meli.

舵手众：我们这般可怜的舵手呀
Helmsmen: But a poor simple sailor just like me,

舵手众：只好在无边洋流中颠簸
Helmsmen: Must be tossed and turned in the deep dark sea.

舵手众：向那海岸告别 告别新斯科舍
Helmsmen: Farewell to Nova Scotia, the sea-bound coast.

舵手众：让黯淡和荒凉将群山淹没
Helmsmen: Let your mountains dark and dreary be.

舵手众：当我随水流飘荡 在远洋之中
Helmsmen: For when I'm far away on the briny ocean tossed,

舵手众：你是否仍会叹息 仍将祝福我
Helmsmen: Will you ever heave a sigh or a wish for me?

……
...

巨齿飞鳐：呜——！
Serres: *roar*

一首又一首说不上名字的船歌撕开了海雾，亮光在海面上闪烁，像晚会后荧荧的篝火。
One nameless sea shanty after another tears through the fog, with lights shimmering on the sea's surface like embers after a festival bonfire.

图图石子：我……我……
Fatutu: I ...

后知后觉的小姑娘终于意识到自己参与了什么。
Realization strikes her. She finally understands her role.

图图石子：格蕾丝女士……
Fatutu: Ms. Grace!

淑女格蕾丝：外面的事并不像你想的那样轻松，当然也并没有那样可怕。
Ms. Grace: The outside world is indeed full of dangers, but there is less to fear than you think.

淑女格蕾丝：无论如何，我会帮你的。
Ms. Grace: I'll help you through it.

叮嘱与劝诫仿佛言犹在耳，她的身子一阵发虚。
Advice and reassurances echo in her mind. She suddenly feels weak.

图图石子：——我都做了些什么啊！
Fatutu: What am I doing?!

图图石子：抱歉，我想……我得先离开了。
Fatutu: Sorry, I have to go.

舵手伊萨姆：嗯？
Helmsman Esam: Hm?

仓促的脚步声蹬蹬地逃开了。
She scurries off.

图图石子：格蕾丝女士……我不明白……
Fatutu: I don't understand.

图图石子：……外面的人，都是这么吵闹而热情吗？
Fatutu: Why are they so nice? This is nothing like the stories.

敲门的手与无数真切的困惑一同悬在空中。
Her questions hang in the air, and so too does a knuckle at a door.

？？？：请进。
???: Come in.

十四行诗：司辰——刚才的事故对您有什么影响吗？
Sonetto: Timekeeper, I hope you didn't have too much difficulty during the power outage.

维尔汀：没什么，我借此测试了X的新发明，“蹦蹦跳弹力灯泡”。
Vertin: Not at all, Sonetto. It actually gave me the opportunity to try out X's latest invention—the Bouncing Bulb.

维尔汀：这是个有趣的发明……美中不足的是，它对体力的要求颇高。
Vertin: It's very interesting, a little draining though.

十四行诗：……您也可以试试这个。
Sonetto: Would you like to try out one of these, then?

维尔汀：十四行诗，这是你做的吗？
Vertin: Did you make this, Sonetto?

十四行诗：嗯，那位来自努库泰澳的塞洛尼小姐将“罗盘灼灼”灯具的做法教给了我。
Sonetto: I did. Ms. Selone from Nukutaeao taught me how to make it. It's called a Sea Mother's Eye.

十四行诗：她告诉我，当暴风雨来临时，麦黎的每家每户都会点起相似的灯。它们能为不得不出海的同伴们指引返航的方向……
Sonetto: She told me every household in Meli lights them during storms to help guide those at sea safely home.

十四行诗：“我们永远不会迷失自己的家乡。”
Sonetto: She said, "With this, no one will ever be lost in the dark."

维尔汀：这是一句很美好的祝福。谢谢你，十四行诗。
Vertin: Thank you, Sonetto. And what a lovely saying.

十四行诗松了口气，目光却仍然停留在那盏“罗盘灼灼”上。
Sonetto breathes a sigh of relief, but her eyes remain fixed on the Sea Mother's Eye.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀：在这次任务结束后，我们应该能向基金会申请一次去往意大利的短期考察。
Vertin: After this mission, we should be able to apply for a field investigation in Italy.

十四行诗：意大利……考察……
Sonetto: Italy?

十四行诗：谢谢您，司辰。
Sonetto: Thank you, Timekeeper.

橘发姑娘难掩眼中的欣喜。
Sonetto is unable to hide her delight.

维尔汀：但现在，我们得先着眼当下的任务。
Vertin: But let's focus on this mission first.

维尔汀：十四行诗，能将你的通讯器借给我么？
Vertin: May I borrow your communicator?

维尔汀：我需要验证一个猜想。
Vertin: There's something I need to verify.

十四行诗：好的。
Sonetto: Of course.

通讯器：“哔哔——”
Communicator: *beep*

通讯器：正在为您接通圣洛夫基金会，Z女士。
Communicator: Connecting to Madam Z of the St. Pavlov Foundation.

通讯器：“——”
Communicator: *static*

通讯器：“滋——滋滋——”
Communicator: *buzz*

通讯器：通讯受到严重干扰，暂时无法接通。请在“哔——”的一声后留言，当通讯恢复后，我们将尽快为您送达。
Communicator: The person you're trying to reach is currently unavailable due to communication interference. Please leave a message after the beep.

十四行诗：……？
Sonetto: Huh?

通讯器：“哔——————”
Communicator: *buzz*

维尔汀：果然，我们的通讯器都无法与外界联络了。
Vertin: Just as I suspected. Communications are blocked.

维尔汀：有人在干扰船上的信号……
Vertin: Someone's jamming the signal.

十四行诗：……是重塑之手？
Sonetto: Do you think it's Manus Vindictae?

维尔汀：很有可能。“自由海风号”的传单证明，他们与重塑之手有着千丝万缕的联系，我们得更加小心了。
Vertin: It's possible. The flyer proved that this ship has some kind of association with them. We need to stay vigilant.

十四行诗：我得赶紧去把这个消息告诉星锑。
Sonetto: Regulus should know about this. I'll go find her.

话音未落，一阵撕心裂肺的呼喊便沿着钢铁墙壁在各个房间中久久回响。
A heart-wrenching scream echoes from afar, reverberating through the halls of the ship.

？？？：不——！
???: NOOOO!

维尔汀：……是星锑的声音！
Vertin: Regulus!

急促的脚步声终于赶上了惊呼的源头。
They hurry over to the source of the scream.

十四行诗：星锑，你没事——
Sonetto: Regulus! Are you alright?!

关切的话语戛然而止。
Sonetto stops in her tracks.

眼前的画面相当熟悉，它曾无数次于科算中心的任何角落上演。
The scene before her is all too familiar, for it has played out countless times at the LSCC.

乌尔里希：咳、今天天气不错。
Ulrich: Ahem, beautiful day, isn't it?

没有对一旁星锑跌落的墨镜发表任何见解，乌尔里希冷静地将手中的咖啡灌入能源口中。
Ignoring the fact that Regulus just dropped her sunglasses, Ulrich calmly pours coffee into his energy intake.

十四行诗：乌尔里希先生……你怎么会出现在这儿？
Sonetto: Mr. Ulrich? What are you doing here?

玻璃缸内的磁流体以一个扭曲的弧度尴尬地旋转着。
The ferrofluid swirls in a distorted arc.

乌尔里希：咳咳，你们好，星锑研究员，十四行诗女士，还有……司辰小姐。
Ulrich: Ahem. Good day, Timekeeper, Researcher Regulus, Ms. Sonetto.

维尔汀：乌尔里希……这就是你说的伪装吗？
Vertin: Is this really the disguise you went with?

星锑：等、等等——！
Regulus: Wait a minute!

星锑：维尔汀，为什么你一点儿也不惊讶？！
Regulus: Vertin, did you know he'd be here?

星锑：我严正声明，我绝对不会负担半张额外的船票支出——！
Regulus: Listen, there's no way I'm paying for even half an extra ticket. In fact, he should be paying for me!

乌尔里希：咳，此事说来话长。
Ulrich: Well, this might take a while to explain.

LEE-09 战争与和平 / Science Salon

“人工暴雨”项目非正式会议，于“自由海风号”启航前
An unofficial meeting on the "Artificial Storm" project was held before the "Free Breeze" set sail from Australia.

与会人员Ⅰ：你疯了吗，乌尔里希？
Attendee I: Did you wake up with a glitch this morning, Ulrich?

与会人员Ⅰ：“暴雨”已经害死了那么多人，你居然还打算搞出一场“人工暴雨”？！
Attendee I: The "Storm" has already taken so many lives, and now you're planning to intentionally bring another one upon us?!

乌尔里希：别那么紧张，乔纳森！我会严格控制实验区域与参与人员，你的名字不在上面。
Ulrich: Quit your worrying, Jonathan. The "Artificial Storm" will be under strict control, and you're not even on the research team.

乌尔里希：更何况，目前的技术处于瓶颈阶段，我们尚有不少实验难题需要解决。
Ulrich: Besides, there are some issues we still need to fix, so we've come to a bit of a standstill for now.

乌尔里希：至少现在，我可以向你保证，这座大楼绝对安全！
Ulrich: I promise, you won't wake up to find the building engulfed by the "Storm."

与会人员Ⅰ：什么——你已经在开展实验了？！
Attendee I: Sorry, are you saying that you've already started?!

与会人员Ⅱ：乌尔里希，我必须警告你。
Attendee II: Ulrich, I have to warn you.

与会人员Ⅱ：自从解开“星锑望远镜”的谜题之后，你就把拉普拉斯的规章制度远远甩在了脑后！
Attendee II: Ever since you found that satellite, you've been pushing past the limits of Laplace's regulations.

与会人员Ⅱ：调用其他分部资料，征用珍贵素材，私自实验——
Attendee II: You've accessed materials from other branches, used valuable resources for your own purposes, and run experiments without proper clearance.

乌尔里希：停止你的污蔑，佩内洛普！我关于“人工暴雨”的每一次行动，都按照现行的规定向总部的中心负责人提交了审批。
Ulrich: What baseless claims, Penelope! I'll have you know that everything I've done has been approved by the HQ director.

与会人员Ⅰ：该死的，你明知道那个鸟位置现在还空着！
Attendee I: Director? We don't have a damn director!

乌尔里希：你瞧，我这不是还专程请来了代理负责人吗？
Ulrich: But we do have a "substitute director." So there.

它朝着一个阴沉的方位点头致意。
He gives a pointed nod in Enigma's direction.

哑谜：我再重申一次，我不是代理负责人！除了露西女士，现在没人能坐那个位置。
Enigma: For the last time, I'm not the "substitute director." No one can substitute for Madam Lucy.

熟悉的敲桌声又一次重重响起。
That familiar heavy knock on the table resounds once more.

哑谜：收起这些不着边际的话术吧，各位同僚。我们要在这儿讨论的是关于“星锑望远镜”的处理方案，而不是针对乌尔里希个人的投诉大会。
Enigma: But let's set that aside. We're here to figure out what to do with the satellite, not to stage an intervention for Ulrich.

与会人员Ⅲ：嘿嘿，这并不难，朋友们～
Attendee III: The solution's as clear as day, my friends!

与会人员Ⅲ：我们完全可以学普列谢茨克那群家伙，就在第三次暴雨的时候来着——找上几个勇敢的同事，“砰”地送到近地轨道上去！
Attendee III: We'll do exactly what they did in Plesetsk during the third "Storm." Find someone brave and send them into space!

与会人员Ⅳ：没错，既然我们能造一次天文望远镜，为什么就不能造第二次呢？
Attendee IV: He's right. Why don't we just build another satellite and see how it handles the "Storm"?

另一侧突兀地响起了掌声。
A sarcastic applause suddenly erupts.

兔毛手袋：哇哦，多么天才的想法啊～这也是为了对照组试验对不对？
Medicine Pocket: Wow, what an amazing idea! Truly a stroke of genius! So, we're talking about a controlled experiment, right?

兔毛手袋：我猜你打算送的不止一颗卫星，而是搭载不同材料的几十颗卫星！
Medicine Pocket: That means we'll send not just one, but dozens of satellites, all carrying different items!

与会人员Ⅳ：……这有什么问题吗？
Attendee IV: What's the problem with that?

兔毛手袋：我倒是有个更省事的提议——或许我们可以再等一段时间，让“暴雨”把我们带回1995年。
Medicine Pocket: Oh, nothing. The budget team will be thrilled at the idea. Here's a better one: We sit tight and wait till the "Storm" sends us back to 1995.

兔毛手袋：“啪——”！我们的卫星就能直接出现在天上，甚至还能为我们节省一大笔经费。
Medicine Pocket: And bingo! Surprise!! There's our satellite, orbiting around the Earth once again.

哑谜：兔毛手袋研究员，请遵循学术交流的基本礼节。
Enigma: Medicine Pocket, please mind your tone in the meeting room.

兔毛手袋：如果他们不打算把拉普拉斯的经费消耗个干净的话，我倒是很愿意这么做。
Medicine Pocket: Oh sure, just as soon as they stop trying to waste all our research funds.

乌尔里希：我赞成兔毛手袋研究员的异议。
Ulrich: I'm with Researcher Medicine Pocket here.

乌尔里希：重新发射卫星毫无必要，我们应该把注意力放到“人工暴雨”项目上来——
Ulrich: There's no need to launch more satellites. We should be focusing on the "Artificial Storm" project.

组长一拍桌子，将所有人的注意力拢回了一处。
Ulrich knocks the table, drawing everyone's attention.

乌尔里希：“人工暴雨”项目已经取得了相当的成果！
Ulrich: The project has made substantial progress!

众人：……
Crowd: ...

乌尔里希：我收集了“星锑望远镜”搭载清单上的全部材料，甚至包括普列谢茨克航天基地的太空种子——你们应该知道它们有多难搞到，甚至超过了星锑的唱片！
Ulrich: I have collected every item that was once on the "Regulus Satellite," including the space seeds from Plesetsk. You have no idea how difficult that was; let me tell you! It was easier to get Regulus's record!

哑谜：不要试图粉饰自己的偷窃行为，乌尔里希！
Enigma: Still, you probably didn't need to steal it, Ulrich!

与会人员Ⅴ：我早就听说了你的实验进展，它根本没有你吹嘘的那么顺利！
Attendee V: You say that, but I've heard that it isn't going all that smoothly!

与会人员Ⅴ：通过声波发生器按照固定频率促进非对称核素R发生反应，以模拟“暴雨”环境。你的实验方向看似美好——
Attendee V: Accelerating the reaction of asymmetrical nuclide R with fixed-frequency sound waves so as to simulate the "Storm." It sounds impressive, but ...

与会人员Ⅴ：可结果呢？
Attendee V: What's the payoff? Have you found the key material that provides immunity from the "Storm"?

乌尔里希，你找到那种能够免疫回溯的材料了么？

乌尔里希：你是对的，卢卡斯。目前的“人工暴雨”实验流程存在严重缺陷。
Ulrich: Good point, Lukas. I never claimed the experiment was perfect. In fact, I'll be the first to admit that it has some serious procedural flaws.

与会人员Ⅴ：……？
Attendee V: Huh?

乌尔里希：经过26次在实验室环境下的“人工暴雨”反应，我确认了包括7种太空种子、天体摄谱仪、高速光度计、黑曜石晶体、泽兰护符的材料效果。
Ulrich: Through 26 microscale "Artificial Storms," I tested seven different space seeds, an astronomical spectrometer, a high-speed photometer, some obsidian crystals, and a Lycopus lucidus talisman.

乌尔里希：它们确实不具备免疫回溯的功能。
Ulrich: None of them endured the trials.

与会人员Ⅴ：那你是打算放弃了？
Attendee V: So, what do we do now? Just give up?

乌尔里希：当然不!
Ulrich: No!

组长尴尬地轻咳两声。
Ulrich awkwardly clears his throat.

乌尔里希：……只是非对称核素R的储备严重不足了。
Ulrich: But I have used all the asymmetrical nuclide R that we had in the warehouse.

兔毛手袋：什么——？！
Medicine Pocket: What?!

愤怒的研究员像是触电般蹦到了桌上。
Medicine Pocket springs to their feet like a shocked animal.

哑谜：冷静点，兔毛手袋！——乔纳森研究员，去调用最新材质的解压弹力球！
Enigma: Sit down, Medicine Pocket! Jonathan, go get them a stress ball!

兔毛手袋：拍桌子可不只是你的特权，代理负责人。
Medicine Pocket: No! I can shout all I want, okay, "substitute director"?!

乌尔里希面前的桌子几乎快要震飞出去。
Medicine Pocket slams the table, sending papers flying.

兔毛手袋：见鬼，你把那些非对称核素R都用了？！
Medicine Pocket: Ulrich! All the asymmetrical nuclide R? It's all gone?!

乌尔里希：这是必要的实验耗材。
Ulrich: I had to use it. It's just standard consumption, like in any other experiment! And I got results!

兔毛手袋：当然，毕竟你有源源不断的耗材可以填进去，再愚蠢的学生把答题卡填满内容也总会有蒙中的时候。
Medicine Pocket: With that amount of resources, of course you'd find something, dumbass! Even a broken clock's right twice a day!

兔毛手袋：再跑快几步，你就能在错误的道路上蹿得更远了。
Medicine Pocket: Keep at it if you want. You're gonna smash that dead end head-on!

乌尔里希：你负责的是生物技术组，我不需要向你汇报我的工作。
Ulrich: I don't see why you're commenting on my work. We're not even in the same department.

乌尔里希按住桌子，以减轻脑袋里磁流体与桌子的共振。
Ulrich presses down on the table to ease the vibrations shaking the ferrofluid in his tank.

兔毛手袋：那可不是一星半点！你几乎把拉普拉斯和基金会所有分部的非对称核素R库存掏了个干净——
Medicine Pocket: Because you used my materials! That was most of the nuclide R from both Laplace and the Foundation!

兔毛手袋：就连我那聒噪的同事九个人都用不了这么多非对称核素R，而我填上几十张那该死的申请表才能被批准用上堪堪几滴——！
Medicine Pocket: You have to be kidding me! You get all you want while I'm here, like some chump, filling out endless forms just to get a few drops!

兔毛手袋的工牌在某种强劲而琐碎的咬合声中吱呀作响。
The badge on Medicine Pocket's chest creaks under the stress of their shouts.

兔毛手袋：要我说，如果你们一开始就把浪费的经费和非对称核素R让给我的项目，我很乐意在下一次“暴雨”时带着那些需要验证的材料去外头跑上几圈！
Medicine Pocket: Next time, just give me the funds and nuclide, and I'll be more than happy to run a few laps in the "Storm" with that crap from the satellite and see what happens!

乌尔里希：我们不会漠视任何一个实验人员的生命安全。
Ulrich: We would never endanger the life of a researcher like that.

与会人员Ⅲ：最安全的项目当然是重新发射一颗新的卫星。更何况，科算中心还能找到不少致力于太空研究的前辈。
Attendee III: That's why we should launch another satellite! No need to risk anyone's life, especially since we've got plenty of colleagues with aeronautics experience.

哑谜：我否决这一提案，目前最了解太空的研究员还躺在拉普拉斯的病房里。
Enigma: Can't do that. Our best space expert is still in the Laplace care unit.

众人：……
Crowd: ...

眼下的硝烟短暂地消散了，终于有人想起会议的正题。
The smoke temporarily clears, and finally, one member returns the meeting to its main agenda.

与会人员Ⅱ：你打算如何推进下一步实验，乌尔里希？
Attendee II: So, Ulrich, what's the next step with your experiment?

乌尔里希：当然是到外面去。
Ulrich: I'm taking it outside, of course.

乌尔里希：非对称核素R储备最丰富的地方绝不是我们的实验室或是基金会的储物间，而是整个世界！
Ulrich: The richest deposits of asymmetrical nuclide R aren't in the lab or the Foundation's warehouse. They're out there in the real world!

哑谜：……？
Enigma: ...?

乌尔里希：更重要的是，过往的“人工暴雨”研究忽略了纯粹环境的影响。
Ulrich: We've been overlooking how the density of nuclide R has affected our experiment results.

与会人员Ⅴ：你只是在为你的失败找借口，乌尔里希！其他地方的研究所怎么可能比我们的实验室更加纯净呢？
Attendee V: Come on, Ulrich, that's just an excuse. Where would you find a higher nuclide R density than in a Laplace lab?

乌尔里希：“暴雨”的象征从来都不是纯粹，而是混沌。
Ulrich: That might be the exact problem. The environment here is too controlled, too clean. The "Storm" has never been the manifestation of order, but of chaos.

与会人员Ⅴ：……
Attendee V: ...

哑谜：可你要怎么满世界地找到你声称的混沌环境，这是在大海捞针！
Enigma: And how exactly do you plan on finding chaos?

会议室的天才们各不相让，为自己的项目与研究预算而战。
The scientists are fighting tooth and nail to secure the budgets for their individual projects.

乌尔里希：够了——！
Ulrich: Everyone, please!

乌尔里希：再这样争执下去，连那个鬼鬼祟祟的洛伦兹研究所的进度都要超过我们了！
Ulrich: If we just sit here arguing instead of getting out there and doing something, those sneaky researchers at Institutum Lorentz are going to get ahead of us!

它重重地将一封蝴蝶纹样的信封拍在桌上，为这团热闹的火又添了一把薪柴。
He slams a butterfly-patterned envelope heavily onto the table, adding yet more fuel to the fiery chaos.

哑谜：洛伦兹……那个古怪的神秘学至上的秘密结社？
Enigma: Lorentz. That strange secret society?

兔毛手袋：让我瞧瞧，它们又寄了什么挑衅信过来？！
Medicine Pocket: Let's see what kind of bull they're spouting this time!

与会人员Ⅱ：住嘴，兔毛手袋——我们有专业的碎纸机！
Attendee II: No, Medicine Pocket! Just toss the letter into the shredder!

急促的脚步踏入了这片纷乱的废墟。
Hurried footsteps echo, and a clear voice cuts through the chaos.

希曼：女士们，先生们，很抱歉打扰你们的头脑风暴，圣洛夫基金会方通过了最新的决议。
Simone: Ladies and gentlemen, my apologies for interrupting your debate. The St. Pavlov Foundation has passed a new resolution.

LEE-10 一面又一面 / Piracy—Not the Fun Kind

希曼的发言显然是颗更重磅的炸弹。
Simone's statement is definitely a much more damaging bomb.

与会人员Ⅰ：希曼女士，我没听错吧……您刚才提到了基金会？
Attendee I: Ms. Simone, did you just say something about the Foundation?

与会人员Ⅰ：据我所知，这次会议需要解决的是如何确认能够越过“暴雨”的稳定性材料，这跟基金会有什么关系？
Attendee I: Are we not moving off-topic? We were discussing our efforts to identify substances immune to the "Storm." What is all this about the Foundation?

兔毛手袋：——天大的好消息！
Medicine Pocket: No idea, but it's sure to be the most cheerful, positive, wonderful news.

兔毛手袋：你们赶走了铁壳子，现在这儿得轮到基金会的呆脑瓜们拍板了。
Medicine Pocket: That'll teach you to run Madam Bucket Head out of town. Now it's going to be those Foundation dimwits calling the shots, ha.

哑谜：首先，我完全不接受基金会对于拉普拉斯科算中心的一丁点儿管辖权，我会在之后解决这个问题的，我保证。
Enigma: I won't stand for the Foundation ordering Laplace around. I'll set things straight with them later, you have my word.

心怀愤懑的会议主持人高举手掌，片刻后又无奈放下，只能颓然坐倒在椅子上。
He raises his hands in exasperation before promptly dropping them and slumping back into his chair.

哑谜：其次，你可以开始宣布了，希曼女士。
Enigma: In fact, Ms. Simone, you may relay my message now.

希曼：我理解你的心情，哑谜先生。但就眼下的状况而言，这不见得是一件坏事。
Simone: I understand your concerns, Mr. Enigma. But given our present circumstances, the Foundation's involvement may have a bright side.

她展开了一份工整的文书。
She unfolds a neatly prepared document.

希曼：基金会的决议主要是关于“人工暴雨”项目的，乌尔里希先生。
Simone: The resolution the Foundation relayed to me was principally concerned with your "Artificial Storm" project, Mr. Ulrich.

乌尔里希：……？
Ulrich: ...?

与会人员Ⅱ：你背叛了组织，乌尔里希？
Attendee II: What? Did you switch gears on us, Ulrich?

乌尔里希：该死的，我没有——！我只是想要一份基金会仓库的通行证。
Ulrich: For flux's sake! All I did was ask for a little support.

希曼：基金会答应了你的援助申请。
Simone: Speaking of, the Foundation also sent through their approval for your other requests.

希曼：实验清单里提及的大部分材料、非对称核素R的储量补充、协助实验的外派调查员，一切都将分批运送到拉普拉斯的各分部。
Simone: Mostly, anyway. They agreed to supply the majority of your requested materials, including replenishing a portion of our asymmetrical nuclide R, and they've dispatched field investigators to assist us.

希曼：另外，关于你提到的符合实验条件的坐标，基金会同样做了初步筛选与确认。
Simone: Additionally, they've done preliminary screenings on the locations you mentioned and confirmed they meet the specifications of our experiments.

与会人员Ⅰ：……基金会之前可从没对我们这么大方过。
Attendee I: The Foundation has never been this generous with us before.

乌尔里希：——！
Ulrich: ...!

幸福来得太过突然，连久经战场的组长也恍惚了许久。
Joy rushes through Ulrich. He feels almost in a daze.

兔毛手袋：别高兴得太早了，乌尔里希！
Medicine Pocket: Don't go popping the champagne just yet, Ulrich!

兔毛手袋：这还远远不够填上你浪费的非对称核素R的缺口——！
Medicine Pocket: Our new bosses aren't going to come anywhere close to replacing all the asymmetrical nuclide R you've wasted!

它对兔毛手袋的发言置若罔闻，目光炽烈地盯着希曼手中的信件。
Ulrich ignores them, his gaze fixated on the letter in Simone's hands.

乌尔里希：基金会的条件是什么？
Ulrich: Still, it's all too easy. What's the catch?

希曼：他们必须得到第一手的实验结论。
Simone: They want to witness our results—firsthand.

可怜的桌子发出了今天的倒数第二声哀嚎。
The table is smacked once again.

乌尔里希：成交！
Ulrich: Deal!

乌尔里希：随便谁——别忘了做会议记录！
Ulrich: Someone—anyone—take down the minutes!

乌尔里希重重挥拳，玻璃缸中的磁流体翻起一阵波浪。
Ulrich pounds the table once more, sending waves through the ferrofluid.

希曼：另外，信件上提到了一个特殊的坐标，他们无法确认该坐标的具体情况……
Simone: They also sent over another possible location that they haven't been able to confirm.

希曼：那是……一艘船。
Simone: A ship.

希曼：考虑到可能的风险，基金会方建议你亲自前往调查。
Simone: The Foundation has requested that you investigate it personally.

希曼：关于它的详细内容，你可以联系司辰。
Simone: The Timekeeper will brief you on the details.

……
...

星锑：好吧，乌尔里希组长，我接受你的解释了。
Regulus: Fine, Fish Tank, you're off the hook for now.

星锑瞧了瞧维尔汀，又望了望正在坦然脱下伪装的乌尔里希。
Regulus glances at them, then her eyes fix on Ulrich, who is calmly removing his disguise.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

星锑：所以你并不打算带着我的“小东西”偷渡出港，而是为了实验？
Regulus: Just so we're clear. You're not planning to smuggle out my "treasure," right?

乌尔里希：当然。
Ulrich: I wouldn't think of it.

星锑：也不打算榨干你可怜组员的钱包给自己补票？
Regulus: Fab, and you're not angling that I foot the bill for this excursion, right?

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希轻咳了两声，将话题掰回了正轨。
Ulrich clears his throat before steering the conversation back on track.

乌尔里希：基金会的情报相当准确，经过初步检测，这儿确实是个符合实验条件的地方。
Ulrich: The Foundation's intel appears accurate. After some preliminary checks, I am certain this will be an ideal locale to conduct our experiments.

乌尔里希：除了“暴雨”的时候，非对称核素R检测仪的读数可从来没有这么激烈过。
Ulrich: I've never seen such intense readings of asymmetrical nuclide R outside of the "Storm."

星锑：慢着，乌尔里希组长！
Regulus: Now hold on a minute, Ulrich!

星锑：你会抱着那些材料到海里去游泳吗？
Regulus: You're not about to take a swim, are you?

乌尔里希：如有必要的话。
Ulrich: Only if necessary.

星锑：……喂！我抗——
Regulus: With my record! You've got to be off your rocker, mate!

抢在星锑发出新的宣言之前，一张熟悉的唱片猝不及防地映在了墨镜的倒影中。
Ulrich quickly abates her protestations by presenting her with the record.

乌尔里希：它该物归原主了。
Ulrich: Not at all. It's time it was returned to its rightful owner.

星锑：——！
Regulus: ...!

一人一唱片亲昵地搂抱在一起。
She embraces the record like an old friend.

星锑：我的宝贝儿唱片，欢迎回家！——我保证我会在APPLe电台连续播放72小时，为你举办最最最盛大的回归派对！
Regulus: Oh, my darling, oh, my treasure, welcome home! I'll broadcast your tracks on Radio APPLe for 72 hours straight and hold the rockin'-est party ever just for you! Oh! You've got my word!

重逢的喜悦终于在接连不断的热泪与耳鬓厮磨中宣泄完毕，一个更严峻的可能性闪过星锑的脑海。
The joy of this reunion pours out of her, before a graver possibility flashes across her mind.

星锑：等等，你该不会打算现在收回对我的一切资助吧——！
Regulus: Hold on. You're not about to withhold my funds, are you?!

乌尔里希：你误会了，星锑研究员。
Ulrich: Fret not, Regulus.

乌尔里希：考虑到这张唱片本身对于你的特殊意义……我们将对它的“采样与成分分析”工作列入了第一优先级，目前这项工作已经完成了，它当然应该物归原主。
Ulrich: Given its special significance to you, we made its composition analysis our first priority. Now that the first step is done, I'm more than happy to return it to you.

星锑：可，你的实验还没有结束……
Regulus: But what about your experiments?

星锑抚摸着手中的“小东西”，咬了咬牙，又忍痛将它递给了乌尔里希。
Clutching her "little thing" in her hands, Regulus hesitates, then reluctantly hands it to Ulrich.

组长轻咳了两声，又故作正式地重新披上了“伪装”。
Ulrich clears his throat again, donning the feigned formality of his "disguise" once more.

乌尔里希：别担心，我早有准备。
Ulrich: Not to worry. I've already made arrangements.

它得意洋洋地扬起风衣，展示拉普拉斯最新的杰作。
He proudly raises his coat to unveil Laplace's latest masterpiece.

数十张一模一样的“小东西”唱片叠成了一摞。
Dozens of identical "little thing" records are stacked neatly together.

乌尔里希：为了实验结果的一致性，我们甚至以同样的书写材料与笔迹模拟了上面的乐队签名。
Ulrich: We went to great lengths to ensure these replicas were identical in every way. We even reproduced the ink used in the signature.

乌尔里希：这些材料是拉普拉斯工艺的结晶。音场的空间感与细节表现、唱片本身使用的乙烯基材料，甚至是中间的装饰水晶，我们都做到了结构与表现的完全一致。
Ulrich: Identical down to their heart and soul, courtesy of Laplace craftsmanship. We've achieved complete consistency in both composition and appearance.

组长自豪的语气与星锑惊讶的疾呼声交织在一起。
Ulrich's proud tone is cut off by Regulus's exclamation of surprise.

星锑：什么——！
Regulus: What?!

星锑：尽管我完全认可拉普拉斯科算中心的科研素质与实验态度——
Regulus: Well, I've got to hand it to you; they're dead-ringers for the real thing.

星锑：……但这并不代表我支持你的盗印行为啊！
Regulus: But this is piracy, and not the fun kind! Musical piracy!

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：看来你对科研使命的理解仍有不足……星锑研究员，你还有很长的路要走啊！
Ulrich: Drastic times call for drastic measures. I hope you'll find it in your heart to forgive us, Regulus.

LEE-11 我可恨的乡土啊 / The Hateful Hometown

积云在夜空中缓缓倒退，像是一阵接一阵涌起的海浪，无名的星星们林立着，遥远地拢成一个小小的斑点。
Cumulus clouds drift slowly across the night sky like the rolling waves of the sea, the countless stars glinting gently behind them.

湿润的海风挟着水汽裹在船栏上。观景舷窗前，年轻的船长看不出表情。
The damp sea breeze has laid a heavy layer of moisture on the surfaces of the ship. Standing at the observation window, the captain's face betrays no emotion.

某些微不可查的声音在门前踌躇着。
There is a faint, hesitant sound at her door.

淑女格蕾丝：——！
Ms. Grace: ...!

淑女格蕾丝：真没想到你会主动到这儿来，图图石子小姐。
Ms. Grace: Oh, Ms. Fatutu, I hadn't expected you to visit.

惊喜的表情写满了她整张脸。
Grace's face lights up, every inch radiating joy.

格蕾丝热切地推开门，将瑟缩不前的姑娘亲昵地牵到面前。
She eagerly opens the door, affectionately pulling Fatutu into the room.

淑女格蕾丝：我差点儿都以为会主动来拜访我的只有那些庸俗的、捏着几张薄纸片在唠叨着什么旅游规划、长期合作的官员和商人了……
Ms. Grace: I must say it's a welcome relief from the onslaught of greedy businessmen and boorish officials.

淑女格蕾丝：他们脑子的肿胀程度简直快赶上我从水里捞起的标本了……但是你明白的，作为收藏品而言，这些叽叽喳喳的家伙们还为时尚早。
Ms. Grace: All puff and no substance—bloated, lifeless, they remind me of a few specimens of decay from my collection.

图图石子：格蕾丝女士，难道您的收藏品是海上的浮、浮……
Fatutu: Decaying specimens? Ms. Grace, you mean bodi—

淑女格蕾丝：嘘——抱歉，我好像说的有些太多了。
Ms. Grace: Hush. Let's just leave things at that.

她眯了眯眼睛，打量着眼前姑娘微微凸起的血管，想象着血液在其中局促而张皇地奔流。
She squints as she studies the faintly protruding veins on the girl's hands, imagining the blood coursing anxiously through them.

淑女格蕾丝：忘了它吧，我猜你希望询问的问题与它们无关。
Ms. Grace: So then, you're here to talk about something else? Go ahead.

图图石子：……是的，格蕾丝女士。
Fatutu: Yes, Ms. Grace.

图图石子：我希望能从您这儿得到指引……
Fatutu: I just wanted some advice, if you don't mind.

淑女格蕾丝：当然可以，我们是朋友，对吧？
Ms. Grace: Not at all, my dear. We are friends, aren't we?

淑女格蕾丝：在海上，迷茫是我们最大的敌人，我们脚不着地，不知自己身在何处，也不知自己将去向何地……我很乐意为朋友解答类似的问题。
Ms. Grace: We are venturing into the unknown. So, it is little surprise that you feel lost, but disorientation is a dangerous enemy. I am more than happy to help.

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

淑女格蕾丝：放轻松，我们至少还有一个漫长的夜晚。
Ms. Grace: Relax and keep an open mind, dear. We have a long night ahead.

隐约的细碎响动从外面传来，但这显然无法影响姑娘们的促膝长谈。
A few soft, subtle noises come from outside, but they are not enough to disrupt the intimate conversation between the two.

格蕾丝放下手中的怀表，目光穿过半掩的舱门，勾出一抹似有若无的微笑。
Grace sets down her pocket watch, her gaze drifting past the slightly ajar door, a faint smile teasing her lips.

图图石子：我试图遵循您的建议，对外界的一切都置之不理……但我失败了。
Fatutu: The thing is, I tried to ignore the outside world, just like you said, but I failed.

图图石子不自觉地低下了头。
Fatutu instinctively lowers her head.

图图石子：我无法朝着完全不了解的人举起复仇的长矛，哪怕是为了我们自己的家园……
Fatutu: The idea of raising a spear against people I know so little about, even if it was to avenge my home.

图图石子：所以我尝试了解更多关于外面的事，我……我违背了您的告诫。
Fatutu: I thought I had to learn more about these outsiders, to understand them. I'm sorry I went against your advice.

图图石子：我想要变得更加坚定……
Fatutu: I thought that learning about them would harden my resolve.

图图石子：我以为这样就能让我憎恨他们，下定决心跟随您，参与重塑的复仇计划，能够带领努库泰澳人去往新世界……
Fatutu: I thought that I would hate them from the depths of my soul, that the hatred would be so strong that I'd feel no remorse, that I would see in them what you and Manus Vindictae do.

图图石子：可……
Fatutu: But ...

意志的动摇令图图石子羞愧地低下了头。
In the face of her wavering resolve, Fatutu bows her head in shame.

图图石子：可为什么我在“自由海风号”上了解的越多，我却越来越迷茫呢？
Fatutu: Instead, after interacting with the people here ...

喧嚷的音乐厅、闹腾的游客、热烈的灯火与船歌，船上的一幕幕犹在眼前。
The noisy music hall, the bustling tourists, the bright lights, the sea shanties—they all linger in her mind.

淑女格蕾丝：这一点儿也不可耻，图图石子小姐。
Ms. Grace: Fatutu, my dear. There's no shame in having second thoughts.

温和的答复令图图石子愣了愣神。
The gentleness of her response leaves Fatutu momentarily stunned.

淑女格蕾丝：在窥见世界的全貌之前，我们大都会有类似的误解。
Ms. Grace: How could you not? This was but your first glimpse of a world so much wider than you knew.

淑女格蕾丝：这个世界是一具刚刚死去的躯体，肺部甚至还残留着新鲜吸入的空气。
Ms. Grace: But you'll soon realize that it is nothing more than a dying corpse, its lungs still clinging on to its last breath.

淑女格蕾丝：最先腐败的是面庞。噢，那是一个糟糕的开始，迅速缩小而浑浊的眼球是令无数标本家们都相当苦恼的难题之一。
Ms. Grace: The face rots first, you know? It's a nasty scene, I assure you. Those shrinking, putrefying eyeballs are always a headache for taxidermists.

淑女格蕾丝：紧接着是胸腔与肺部，情况变得糟糕，难闻的气体争先恐后地涌入每一寸尚未被占领的角落。它们膨胀开来，像是即将迸散的礼花。
Ms. Grace: Next, the chest cavity. It rots out from the inside, bloating with noxious gases produced by its decomposing flesh until it's ready to pop like a party balloon.

淑女格蕾丝：但值得庆幸的是，倘若你在这时候观赏其中的手足，或是轻抚其中的骨骼，你仍然会惊叹于造物主的伟大，“噢！祂究竟是如何雕琢出如此完美的结构的？”
Ms. Grace: Even at this stage, if you were to hold your breath and look only to the limbs, you might marvel at the artisanship—such a perfect creation! Yet, it dies all the same. So it goes.

图图石子从未见过这样热情洋溢的船长。
Fatutu has never encountered such a warm and spirited captain before.

淑女格蕾丝：你可以再想想，好好地想一想……
Ms. Grace: Do you see the world any clearer now? Take your time. Think it through.

格蕾丝轻轻敲击着船板，像是在为门外的窸窣脚步声打着节拍。
Grace lightly taps her finger on the board beside her, as if keeping time with the faint footsteps outside.

沉思中的图图石子对这一切浑然未觉。
Lost in thought, Fatutu remains oblivious to it all.

图图石子：……
Fatutu: ...

图图石子：外面的人和我想的很不一样……他们真的那么邪恶吗？
Fatutu: The outsiders are different from what I expected. Ms. Grace, are you sure they're truly evil?

淑女格蕾丝：……呵呵。
Ms. Grace: Heh heh.

格蕾丝瞥了瞥窗外。
Grace glances out the window.

空无一人的舷窗里，古怪的震响声越发明显了。
Through the porthole, a strange vibrating sound grows louder and more distinct.

图图石子：……？
Fatutu: ...?

跟随船长的视线，图图石子终于注意到了那片巨大的“阴影”。
Following Grace's gaze, Fatutu notices an enormous "shadow" on the other side of the porthole.

遮阳伞与围栏，真的能组成如此巨大的阴影吗？
Can parasols and railings really create such an enormous silhouette?

淑女格蕾丝：她们无比狡猾、邪恶，甚至还会偷听他人的秘密。
Ms. Grace: They're cunning, menacing, and at times, have even been known to engage in eavesdropping.

“阴影”蹑手蹑脚地朝着她们的方向逼近了。
The "shadow" creeps closer toward them, stealthy and deliberate.

图图石子：格、格蕾丝……小姐，那个“怪物”在朝着我们探头探脑——！
Fatutu: M-Ms. Grace, watch out! It's ... it's some kind of monster!

毫无疑问，这样刻薄的形容词激怒了对方。
There is no doubt. This cutting description has angered the shadowy intruder.

？？？：哈……？
???: Huh?

图图石子：难道——是敌人？！
Fatutu: I-It's here!

图图石子手忙脚乱地抱起周围的杂物，信号灯、扫帚、抛绳……它们像雨点一样飞扬起来，接连不断地飞向门外。
Scrambling, Fatutu grabs whatever is nearby—signal lights, brooms, and heaving lines—and flings them out the door.

图图石子：我……我来保护你，格蕾丝小姐！
Fatutu: I'll protect you, Ms. Grace!

门外的动静似乎消失了。
The commotion seems to have come to an end.

图图石子：危、危机……解除了吗？
Fatutu: Is it dead?

大口喘气的图图石子勇敢地冲出了船舱。
Panting heavily, Fatutu musters the courage to rush out of the cabin.

甲板上出现的人影与预想中的可怕敌人相去甚远。
The figure on the deck is far removed from the terrifying enemy she envisioned.

图图石子：啊——竟然是你，芭卡洛儿小姐……
Fatutu: Oh! It's you, Barcarola.

芭卡洛儿：呜呜……
Barcarola: *sob*

一副泫然欲泣的脸庞从大战后的废墟中探了出来。
A familiar tear-streaked face emerges from the aftermath of the chaos.

船长显然对游轮员工的狼狈状况早有预料。
The captain, however, seems unfazed by the disheveled state of her cruise staff.

淑女格蕾丝：很高兴能在这儿见到你，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Ms. Grace: Ms. Barcarola, what a pleasure to see you.

芭卡洛儿：图图石子，你、你怎么能这样？！
Barcarola: Have you lost your mind, Fatutu?!

芭卡洛儿：我只是想为“罗盘灼灼”的事向你道谢，可我哪儿也找不到你——
Barcarola: I've been looking all over the ship for you to thank you for the lamps you made!

芭卡洛儿：就算你不愿意接受我的谢意，也不该做出乱扔东西这么粗鲁的举动呀！
Barcarola: This is a funny way of saying "you're welcome."

芭卡洛儿：在克雷莫纳，哪怕是再不学无术的家伙——也不会朝着路过的可怜小狗这样丢石子！
Barcarola: Not even the rudest stunad in Cremona would attack someone for saying thanks!

某个陌生的名词在恼怒的唇齿间脱口而出，又落入另一双好奇的耳朵里。
An unfamiliar term springs from her lips, sparking Fatutu's curiosity.

图图石子：克雷……莫纳？
Fatutu: Cremona? Where's that?

芭卡洛儿：……我什么也没说！
Barcarola: That's really not what matters here!

淑女格蕾丝：放松下来，朋友们，这只是个令人发笑的小误会，不是么？
Ms. Grace: Settle down please, ladies. This was only a small misunderstanding, wasn't it?

淑女格蕾丝：作为船长，也作为你们的朋友，我很希望你们将来能成为要好的同伴。
Ms. Grace: As both your captain and your friend, I hope that you might be able to resolve this. I do believe I could see you two becoming fast friends.

船长的拉拢毫不遮掩。
The captain's overtures are anything but subtle.

淑女格蕾丝：我想，图图石子小姐很乐意了解更多关于外面的事，而我们的芭卡洛儿小姐，恰好藏着许多故事，不是么？
Ms. Grace: Fatutu here is eager to learn about the outside world. And I'm sure you must have many stories to share, don't you?

淑女格蕾丝：嗯……就当做“罗盘灼灼”的报答好了。
Ms. Grace: Consider it a favor in exchange for those Sea Mother's Eyes.

图图石子＆芭卡洛儿：……
Fatutu & Barcarola: ...

将语塞的客人们留在原地显然不是一位经验丰富的船长应有的待客之道。
It simply wouldn't do for a captain to leave these two in such a state.

淑女格蕾丝：请到这边来，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Ms. Grace: Why don't you take a seat, Ms. Barcarola?

她往一旁挪了挪，在光洁如新的甲板上留出了一个足够的空缺。
She moves aside, extending two delicate hands to them.

女孩们任由一双亲昵的手牵引着靠在了一起。
The girls take her hands, allowing themselves to be drawn close. Then, they lean together on the railing.

海风攀上甲板，吹散了片刻前的尴尬。
The sea breeze sweeps across the deck, dispersing whatever awkwardness there was between them.

淑女格蕾丝：克雷莫纳，这是一个难以启齿的名字吗？
Ms. Grace: You were quick to gloss over your hometown. Cremona, wasn't it?

船长的语气温和而柔软，年轻的乐手终于放松了紧绷的琴弦。
Grace's voice is gentle and soft. Barcarola finally loosens the tension in her strings, speaking as she looks out over the moonlit water.

芭卡洛儿：不。它是我的家乡，世人口中的小提琴之乡，一个古板又令人讨厌的陈旧地方！
Barcarola: Cremona, the "City of Violins," as they say. Sì, I was born in that awful, dreary old place. But I don't like to talk about it, Ms. Grace.

另一颗好奇的心也凑了上来。
Fatutu examines Barcarola's expression.

图图石子：可是……你的语气听上去并没有厌恶呀。
Fatutu: Hmm. But it sounds like you still miss your home, so why speak of it that way? Is there something wrong with it?

图图石子：在努库泰澳，如果讨厌什么，我们会将它和臭芥草儿缠在一块儿，再用力把它抛向海里，让它永永远远地沉在水底，再也不会想起来。
Fatutu: In Nukutaeao, when we find something rotted in our village, we wrap it up in stinky grass and throw it in the ocean.

图图石子：难道外面的人们不会这么做吗？
Fatutu: Do you outsiders not do this as well?

芭卡洛儿：它……它当然还没有那么糟糕。
Barcarola: W-Well, it's not completely rotted exactly. It's just ...

少女皱了皱眉头，像是在努力寻找合适的措辞。
She furrows her brow, seemingly searching for the right words.

芭卡洛儿：我们整天浸泡在小提琴的琴盒里，学习关于它的一切知识。乐理、演奏、世代相传的小提琴修复技艺，到处都是名头唬人的音乐大师们！
Barcarola: In Cremona, everything is bound up with the violin. How it's made, how it's played, even the science of it. It fills the air, and every conversation. You can't walk to the restaurant without tripping over a virtuoso!

芭卡洛儿：许多人都慕名到这儿来，柏林人、伦敦人、格拉茨人、费拉拉人、乌普萨拉人……他们在任何你能发现的地方举办演出、古典音乐会、音乐节，或是别的什么。
Barcarola: They come from Rome, Berlin, London, New York, Nairobi, Tokyo, Uppsala, people from far and wide, all crammed into one town. Not a day goes by without a concert, a symphony, or a festival musicale.

图图石子：可……这听上去很有意思呀？
Fatutu: Am I misunderstanding you? Because to the Nukutai, the idea of a place with music and festivals every day sounds very fun.

芭卡洛儿：一点儿也不好。
Barcarola: That's where you're wrong, Miss. It's no fun at all.

芭卡洛儿：克雷莫纳的人们都为出生在这座城市而骄傲，除了我。
Barcarola: At least, for me. To be Cremonese is to take pride in its music, its history, and above all, its violins.

芭卡洛儿：克雷莫纳比你想象的还要单调无数倍！那儿只有小提琴、中提琴、大提琴、低音提琴……各种各样的提琴！
Barcarola: And you must learn to love the violin, the viola, the violoncello, and the bass! Because there is nothing else! Every quartet is a string quartet. Every concerto is Vivaldi! Strings, strings, strings! The monotony is unbearable!

芭卡洛儿：要知道，音乐的世界可是多么精彩、多么繁盛！就连你脖子上的贝壳，只要找准发声位置，它也能成为一件特别的乐器呢！
Barcarola: The world has so very many instruments as diverse and as varied as the people that fill it! Even the shell around your neck could sing if you knew just where to tap it!

芭卡洛儿：如果不离开家乡，我就没法将“啪叽咒”运用得更好，没法做出更好的啪唧匣子……当然也见不到世界上那么多稀奇古怪的乐器了！
Barcarola: But not in Cremona. That's why I speak of it that way, Fatutu. Because, if I had stayed there, I would never have seen the music of the world and its instruments, and my Crackling Box would never have been able to know their sounds.

图图石子：可……努库泰澳人一直待在自己的岛上，我们并不会感到枯燥。
Fatutu: The Nukutai don't have many instruments—not so many as you anyway—but we were never bored with what we had.

图图石子：或许你也可以尝试找找那儿的贝壳、礁石，或者是海藻之类的漂亮小玩意儿～
Fatutu: I'm certain that your island holds great beauty beyond its music. If ever we grow tired of singing and dancing, we'd go searching for shells or swimming in the reefs.

芭卡洛儿：唉……你太年轻了，图图石子小姐，事情可没你想的那么简单。
Barcarola: *sigh* You still have much to learn about the world beyond your islands.

淑女格蕾丝：芭卡洛儿女士，你不打算再回去了么？
Ms. Grace: Then you have no intention of ever returning home, Ms. Barcarola?

这似乎只是一个无比寻常的问题。
A seemingly most ordinary question.

芭卡洛儿：……当然！
Barcarola: Return? No, never!

芭卡洛儿：克雷莫纳的家伙们完全不能理解我的创举！在他们眼里，我只是个叛逆的孩子，他们排挤我，讥笑我……
Barcarola: They're too set in their ways, like old fossils. My vision of music grew beyond them, and I did too.

芭卡洛儿将双手拢在嘴边，朝着薄雾笼罩的海平面高声呼喊。
Barcarola cups her hands around her mouth and hollers out into the fog-covered horizon.

芭卡洛儿：我永远也不会回到那儿——！
Barcarola: I won't force myself back into their little world!

淑女格蕾丝：我很欣赏你的坚决。
Ms. Grace: Your determination is admirable indeed.

芭卡洛儿：……看来我不必担心遭到解雇了。
Barcarola: Glad to hear it. Then my position is safe for another day.

淑女格蕾丝：当然，“自由海风号”上的明珠，我们最受人追捧的游轮甜心。
Ms. Grace: How could it not be? You are the very star of the "Free Breeze."

芭卡洛儿：嗯哼～
Barcarola: Uh-huh!

难掩得意的芭卡洛儿小姐脸上又重新焕发了光彩。
Barcarola's face lights up with renewed pride.

图图石子：那么您呢……？格蕾丝女士。
Fatutu: What about you, Ms. Grace?

图图石子：您的故乡又在哪儿？
Fatutu: You've never told us about your home.

淑女格蕾丝：只是个毫无意义的小镇子罢了。
Ms. Grace: It's a place of little interest to anyone, not even worthy of naming.

船长的态度显然要比絮絮叨叨的乐手更加轻描淡写。
Her demeanor is far more composed than the rambling chatter of Barcarola.

芭卡洛儿：“真正的音乐大师应该抛去那些影响自己创作灵感的杂念”，是这样吗？
Barcarola: They say a musician must be free of attachments to be truly creative. Perhaps this is true of captains as well.

图图石子：不，不是这样的。
Fatutu: No. That can't be right!

图图石子：哥哥曾经告诫我，努库泰澳人决不能远离家乡太久。否则，我们的“象形贝壳”将会生出缝隙，多少努努胶水都无法弥补它的裂痕。
Fatutu: The Nukutai believe that to stray from our home is the death of the spirit. If we travel too far and too long, our Spirit Shells develop cracks that no amount of Nukuglue can mend.

图图石子：那是一种让人非常不好受的情绪。老人们都叫它……
Fatutu: And from these cracks come an intense sadness, the elders call it ...

图图石子：乡愁。
Fatutu: Home sick.

芭卡洛儿：失眠的水手们似乎常常提起这个词……接着，他们会邀请我为他们演奏一些我从没听说过的曲子，好在我的啪唧匣子里有数不完的乐器——
Barcarola: Homesickness—sì, we have this word as well. The sailors aboard often ask me to play the songs of their youth when they are missing their homes. So many different melodies. Thankfully, my Crackling Box has all kinds of instruments to suit their needs.

芭卡洛儿：它是一种疾病吗，就像是缺少橘子的坏血病之类的？
Barcarola: I imagine it must be difficult for your people now.

芭卡洛儿：请别担心，图图石子小姐。如果你也患上了这样的症状，我很愿意帮忙——就像你帮助船上的客人那样。
Barcarola: If you'd like, I could learn to play some of your songs and perform them. I'd be more than happy to help, after all you've done.

图图石子：嗯——！
Fatutu: That's kind of you.

图图石子：谢谢你，芭卡洛儿小姐，我们的族人一定很需要它！
Fatutu: I'm sure it will be of great help to us.

芭卡洛儿：这是乐手的使命～
Barcarola: I'm more than happy to help, Fatutu! It is my job, after all!

少女们的话题似乎永远没有尽头，但不时揉搓的双眼仍然清晰地证明着时间的流淌。
The girls' conversation seems to stretch on forever, but the increasing frequency with which they rub their eyes clearly marks the passage of time.

天光逐渐亮了起来，窗外织起了一条无边的蓝色绸缎。在缓缓驶向前方的汽笛声中，缎面泛起一圈圈动荡的褶皱。
Eventually, the sun climbs above the sea, painting its surface a satin blue, and, as the ship's horn sounds, gentle ripples spread across its surface.

淑女格蕾丝：时候不早了，女士们。
Ms. Grace: It appears the sun has caught up with us, ladies.

芭卡洛儿：——！
Barcarola: ...!

芭卡洛儿：天呐，居然已经到这个时候了！我的演出——
Barcarola: Mamma mia! The concert!

芭卡洛儿擦着惺忪的睡眼，瞄见了船长轻轻摇晃的怀表。恍惚间，她终于想起了另一件同样重要的事。
As she rubs her eyes, Barcarola catches a glimpse of the captain lightly shaking her pocket watch and remembers something equally important.

芭卡洛儿：我答应过星锑小姐，我会帮助她举办一场最好的海上摇滚音乐会……我还没有询问她需要什么音色呢！
Barcarola: I promised Ms. Regulus a rock-and-roll concert. But I haven't even asked her what instruments she needs!

芭卡洛儿：再见，格蕾丝女士，图图石子小姐。
Barcarola: Bye, girls!

在一阵急匆匆的踩踏台阶声中，少女的身影迅速消失了。
With hurried footsteps clattering down the stairs, Barcarola quickly vanishes.

图图石子：谢谢您陪我们聊了一整夜，格蕾丝女士。
Fatutu: Thank you for talking with us, Ms. Grace.

确认乐手的背影再也看不见之后，图图石子终于张了张口。
She has waited for Barcarola to be clearly out of sight before speaking.

淑女格蕾丝：不必道谢。我什么也没帮上你，图图石子小姐。
Ms. Grace: Don't mention it. I only hope that it was helpful for you.

图图石子：我……我还有最后一个问题。
Fatutu: I-I have one last question.

图图石子：您究竟是如何令自己变得如此坚定的？
Fatutu: I was wondering how do you stay so determined?

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

LEE-12 三个音乐家 / Clashing Genres

躁动与兴奋的呼声统治了这里。
The air is buzzing with anticipation.

台上的少女欢呼雀跃，跳起欢快的扭扭舞。
Regulus stands on stage, cheering and dancing in a lively twist.

星锑：嗨！女士们、先生们，所有当下的和未来的摇滚乐迷们！
Regulus: Hello, "Free Breeze"! Listen up all my rock 'n' roll stars, fans, and wannabes!

星锑：欢迎你们来到这个时代最伟大、最美妙、最最最激情的摇滚现场——！！
Regulus: You lot are in luck, because you are about to experience the greatest, grandest, most radical rock 'n' roll party of the era!

客人众：喔——！
Guests: Woo-hoo!

星锑：嘿——那边还在打瞌睡的家伙们，趁现在，活动起来，让你们僵硬的骨头嘎嘎作响！
Regulus: Now get up on those feet and drag those little legs of yours on deck. Because it's time to get those old bones jumping!

星锑：当你们老了，坐在火炉边上吹嘘自己的时候，所有听说这个故事的人都会为你们的经历嫉妒得发狂！
Regulus: Just think, folks, one day you'll be sitting by a fireplace, telling your grandkiddies that you were here. This is the night you become a legend!

芭卡洛儿：嘿，星锑——
Barcarola: Hi, Regulus!

哒哒的脚步声急匆匆地奔向了这儿。
Barcarola bursts into the room.

星锑：你好，我亲爱的朋友～
Regulus: Well, if it isn't our star musician!

芭卡洛儿：这和我们说好的不一样，我原以为我们会做好更充分的准备……
Barcarola: This isn't what we agreed on. I thought we'd make our preparations together.

星锑：准备？
Regulus: Umm, what preparations?

芭卡洛儿轻拍胸膛，努力让自己的呼吸平稳下来。
Barcarola pats her chest as she tries to steady her breathing.

芭卡洛儿：是的。我们得先为船上的客人们分发调查问卷，根据客人们的品味挑选合适的曲目，还需要考虑曲目之间的流畅过渡，以及整个音乐会的节奏和情感变化……
Barcarola: To begin with, we must do a survey of our guests' musical preferences, then prepare a song list to match. Then we must carefully organize our transitions to optimize the flow of the concert.

星锑：等等、等等！
Regulus: Wait, wait, wait!

星锑：音乐会？我们可不是在举办音乐会！
Regulus: Arrangements? Concert? What are you on about? This is rock 'n' roll, love! A proper rock 'n' roll party!

——这是摇滚！摇滚！

芭卡洛儿：可克雷……之前的老师们不是这样说的……
Barcarola: No arrangements? No song list? This isn't what I was taught to do in Cremona.

芭卡洛儿：当我们拨下第一个和弦，吹响第一段旋律，我们便肩负起了对听众体验负责的使命。完整的表达才能让听众们跟上脚步，体验音乐的情感起伏和结构美……
Barcarola: As musicians, we have a responsibility to ensure that every listener enjoys an exquisite and seamless experience. We must allow them to savor the emotion and artistry of each piece!

星锑：摇滚乐从不在乎这些细枝末节，重要的是精神！
Regulus: Sounds a bit stuffy, doesn't it? C'mon, no reason to get all hung up on the details. Music is freedom! The only thing that matters in rock 'n' roll are the vibes!

毫无疑问，摇滚海盗对任何繁文缛节都深恶痛绝。
Regulus clearly holds no space for unnecessary formalities.

星锑：放松你紧绷的脑袋，我的朋友～然后，用力地甩动它们！
Regulus: You don't use your brain. You feel it in your heart, babe.

星锑：音乐课堂可学不到这些。
Regulus: Guess your miserable old music teachers never taught you that, eh?

游轮乐手的眉头紧蹙，又逐渐舒缓下来。
Barcarola furrows her brow, but eventually her expression relaxes.

芭卡洛儿：……好吧。
Barcarola: Fine.

芭卡洛儿：但我必须声明，仅此一次。
Barcarola: But just to be clear, next time we do it my way.

星锑：喔——所有的音乐大师都该学习你的胸怀！
Regulus: Ha! Cheers, love. You're an inspiration to musical directors the whole world over!

芭卡洛儿：……
Barcarola: ...

这当然是一句效果斐然的咒语。
Flattery is often more effective than any incantation.

芭卡洛儿：咳、唱片机就在舞台帘幕的后面，第五个柜子里。
Barcarola: You can find the record player in the locker backstage.

得到特许的海盗激动地向目的地奔去。
Regulus immediately darts backstage.

星锑：喔哦——！
Regulus: Fab!

关闭灯光。
Turn off the lights.

连接音响系统，检查唱针，挑选出一张备受期待的唱片。
Connect the sound system, check the stylus, pick a record.

定位音臂，高举双手，等待一场——
Position the tonearm, raise your hands high, and get ready for a—

芭卡洛儿：星锑小姐，你播放的是重金属曲目吗？
Barcarola: Is this what you call "heavy metal"?

星锑：什么？我选中的明明是迷幻摇滚的代表作之一！
Regulus: Uh, what's that? No, no! First up is an iconic taste of psychedelic rock!

星锑：更何况，我还没找到音响电源呢……
Regulus: Uhh. But I haven't even found the power socket yet.

金属碰撞的震响声从下层甲板传来，它们愈发嘈杂，也愈发清晰。
The clanging of metal echoes from the lower decks, growing louder and clearer.

随之而来的还有某种奇异的怪叫声。
Then, an eerie, otherworldly shrieking follows.

像是一场发生在“自由海风号”上的突兀地震。
Followed by what feels like an earthquake.

厅堂中的客人们面面相觑，警觉的助手小姐敏锐地觉察到了些许异样。
While the guests exchange uneasy glances, Sonetto has sensed that something is amiss.

十四行诗：司辰，您也对这种噪音感到耳熟吗？
Sonetto: Timekeeper, those sounds are familiar, aren't they?

维尔汀：金属，打击乐，刺耳的怪叫，难道是……
Vertin: Metallic percussion sounds, sprinkled with screams of pain ...

维尔汀：重塑之手！
Vertin: It's Manus Vindictae!

随着这个熟悉的名词一同出现的，是那些黝黑的古怪铁皮们。
Those blackened, bizarre metallic creatures rear their heads once more.

重塑·门徒：ㄞ——！！筛选……
Disciple of the Manus: *roar* Sift ...

源源不断的铁皮乐器们从下层的楼梯间涌出，像是从井口喷薄而出的石油。
A torrent of metal instruments surges up from the stairwells to the lower levels, like oil gushing out of a pipe.

重塑·门徒：……试……炼！ㄢ——！！
Disciple of the Manus: And ... trial ...! *roar*

突如其来的变故让客人们炸开了锅。
The sudden commotion sends the guests into an uproar.

人群开始窃窃私语，退缩着挤成一团。
They huddle together, whispering nervously to one another.

星锑：什么？！怎么哪儿都有你们这些阴魂不散的家伙！
Regulus: What?! These persistent pests again?! Which hellhole did they crawl out of this time?!

芭卡洛儿：别担心，星锑小姐，我不会让他们影响你的音乐会的！
Barcarola: Don't worry, Ms. Regulus. I won't let them disturb your rock party!

气势汹汹的乐手冷静地站在了对方的面前。
She stands calmly but fiercely before them.

芭卡洛儿：嘿，格蕾丝船长明明向所有人保证过了，她绝不会让你们这些笨手笨脚的船员吓坏客人！
Barcarola: You oafish barnacles are ruining the atmosphere and scaring our guests! I very much doubt you're doing this with the approval of Captain Grace.

芭卡洛儿：你们应该乖乖地待在机械室，管好那些发动机和螺旋桨，而不是跑到甲板上来制造噪音——！
Barcarola: You should be working in the engine room, not making noise up on deck!

芭卡洛儿：难道你们忘记了《船员守则》吗？
Barcarola: Have you all forgotten the Seafarers' Code of Conduct?

对方似乎毫不动容，意识到危机的基金会调查员们挡在了芭卡洛儿的前面。
They appear unmoved. The Foundation's investigators step forward, immediately taking command of the situation.

维尔汀：注意疏散人群，十四行诗，星锑。
Vertin: Sonetto, Regulus, get the crowd out of here.

维尔汀：准备拦截重塑之手。
Vertin: Get ready to engage with these Manus thugs.

十四行诗：明白！
Sonetto: Understood!

十四行诗：芭卡洛儿小姐，请远离它们！
Sonetto: Ms. Barcarola, I'll ask you kindly to step back from these brutes.

芭卡洛儿：十四行诗小姐，它们只是些长相古怪的轮机工罢了。请放心，我会处理好这一切的。
Barcarola: Please, Miss. There's no need for alarm. I know they may look a little strange, but they're just engine crew. They work here.

芭卡洛儿：维持“自由海风号”的秩序，令每一位客人都能维持美好的心情，是游轮乐队的职责之一。
Barcarola: And as such, as our musical director, I have some authority over them. Moreover, it is my duty to ensure all our guests have a safe and enjoyable stay.

维尔汀：……我想我明白重塑是如何隐藏踪迹的了。
Vertin: Now I see how the Manus kept themselves hidden.

人群仍然惴惴不安，图图石子被迫挤在当中。
Fatutu quickly finds herself trapped amid the restless crowd.

她努力踮起脚尖，无数漆黑的阴影与明亮的日光交叠在一起，令人眼花目眩。
She stands on tiptoe, dazzled by the countless overlapping shadows and rays of sunlight.

图图石子：芭卡洛儿小姐……她在做什么呢？
Fatutu: Is that Barcarola? What's she doing over there?

在无数道或好奇或惊异的目光中，一抹纯净的白缓缓靠向了那摊石油。
Amid curious and astonished gazes, Barcarola gradually approaches the dark mass of Manus followers.

芭卡洛儿：嘿！如果你们也希望接受一些音乐上的熏陶，提高一点儿音乐品味，我可以在这一场演出结束后为你们演奏……但不能是这儿。
Barcarola: If you've come to be entertained, or perhaps for some music lessons, I would be more than happy to assist you in the crew quarters later.

芭卡洛儿：大多数客人对金属乐的理解并不多，你们应该照顾更多的普通人……
Barcarola: However, your musical talents will not be needed at this time, as we already have a scheduled performance.

重塑·门徒：ㄒ……新时——！！
Disciple of the Manus: *roar* New ... era—

似乎对芭卡洛儿的建议置若罔闻，一柄敲击锤高举了起来。
No heed is taken. Instead, a hammer is raised high.

维尔汀：阻止它们！
Vertin: Stop them!

越来越多的重塑门徒挤满了大厅的外围，人们如同被圈养的羊群瑟瑟发抖。
More and more Manus disciples fill the perimeter of the hall, surrounding those inside like trembling penned sheep.

芭卡洛儿：这、这不对……为什么这些新招募的船员，看上去这么疯狂呢？
Barcarola: W-What's happening!? Why are they acting crazy?

她努力站在所有客人的前方，大口呼出的热气喷薄在微微颤抖的啪唧匣子的琴颈上。
She stands resolutely, putting herself between the guests and the crazed Manus disciples, her heavy breathing condensing on the neck of her Crackling Box.

芭卡洛儿：我是“自由海风号”的乐队负责人……我有义务对每一位客人的安全负责……
Barcarola: As the musical director of the "Free Breeze," I can't allow you to harm our guests.

？？？：哼……聒噪的外族人。
???: Hmph, enough of your nonsense, foolish outsider!

一道冷光嗖地袭来。
A flash of cold light streaks through the air.

图图石子：不——！
Fatutu: No!

图图石子：“ *坚硬如椰壳！ ”
Fatutu: *Popo protect!

贝壳状的波纹拦下了那支冰冷的箭羽。
A shell-shaped ripple appears, deflecting the icy arrow.

芭卡洛儿：——！
Barcarola: ...!

图图石子：你没事吧……芭卡洛儿小姐？
Fatutu: Are you okay, Barcarola?

她蹿出人群，关切地奔向那个受惊的身影，罔顾身后数道讶异的目光。
Fatutu darts out from the crowd, rushing over to Barcarola with no regard for the surprised stares of the Nukutai behind her.

？？？：……你在做什么？
???: What are you doing, Fatutu?!

？？？：图图石子，你还记得自己的身份吗——！
???: That is an outsider! Have you forgotten your duty to your people?

熟稔的严厉训斥在耳边炸响。
A stern, familiar reprimand booms in her ears.

扶稳并无大碍的乐手后，图图石子紧张地转过身来。
After steadying the shaken musician, Fatutu nervously turns around.

哥哥的身体隐没在人墙的阴影里，令人心生紧张。
Her brother's figure looms in the shadows of the crowd. For the first time, this image deeply unsettles her.

图图石子：不……哥哥……不是这样的……
Fatutu: No, never, but ...

图图石子：努库泰澳人……保护家园的武器……不应该用来复仇……
Fatutu: Kamuta, this is not defending our home, and it doesn't feel like avenging it either.

图图石子：我们遭、遭受的一切……不关他们的事……也、也许……我们能找到更好的解决办法……
Fatutu: What we suffered was not these people's fault! There has to be a better solution to all this!

图图石子：……现在还不是复仇的好时候。
Fatutu: This isn't our way. It isn't right.

脚步声缓缓逼近，图图石子惊惶地仰起头来。
Fatutu stares fearfully as her brother draws closer.

正对上一张熟悉而陌生的脸。
As he comes into the light, she finds herself staring into a face that is both familiar and strange.

图图石子：哥哥……
Fatutu: Kamuta ...

卡穆塔：……
Kamuta: ...

对方轻轻摇了摇头，漆黑如墨的液体从古铜色面具的缝隙中滴落。
Kamuta gently shakes his head. Inky black liquid drips from the seams of his mask.

卡穆塔：图图石子，我们别无选择。
Kamuta: Fatutu, we have no choice.

LEE-13 太阳之死 / End of the Sun

金属的噪音取代了摇滚乐，肃穆与恐慌笼罩在船舱中的每一位客人脸上。
The sound of scraping metal brings an end to the pumping rock music, painting a look of solemnity and fear on the faces of every guest.

灵巧的身影款款登上了舞台。
A lithe figure steps gracefully onto the stage.

淑女格蕾丝：首先，为你们自己举杯吧——
Ms. Grace: We should raise a toast. One and all.

淑女格蕾丝：登上“自由海风号”的幸运儿们。
Ms. Grace: For we're in luck's good graces to be aboard this ship.

淑女格蕾丝：或者说，它应该拥有一个更准确的名字，诺亚方舟。
Ms. Grace: A ship, hmm, perhaps one ought to think of it more as an ark.

台下的游客们面面相觑。许久，终于有人试探着开口询问。
The guests exchange uneasy glances. After a long silence, one guest hesitantly breaks the silence with a question.

客人Ⅰ：格、格蕾丝船长……你是不是搞错了什么？
Guest I: Just what are you getting at?

客人Ⅱ：噢！我明白了，这一定是游轮为我们准备的惊喜派对，对吧，芭卡洛儿小姐？
Guest II: Oh, I get it! Is this some kind of surprise theme party, like a murder mystery?! Is that right, Ms. Barcarola?

茫然的乐手抬起头来。高台上的身影陌生而冷冽，这显然无关任何一场精心彩排的演出。
Barcarola looks bewildered. The captain's sudden and strange appearance on the stage was certainly not part of any performance. At least, not one she had prepared.

芭卡洛儿：不……不是这样的。
Barcarola: No, I didn't plan for any of this.

淑女格蕾丝：这当然能够称得上是一份惊喜，马修先生。
Ms. Grace: You aren't entirely wrong though, Mr. Matthews, for this is certainly a surprise, if not so much a party as a ceremony.

淑女格蕾丝：恭喜你们，诸位凭借着天赋、财富，或是某种秘不视人的珍宝，通过了“自由海风号”的第一次筛选，得到了一个加入重塑之手的机会。
Ms. Grace: Allow me to congratulate you, our honored guests. Each of you, with your unique talents, resources, and powerful connections, have earned a chance to join Manus Vindictae.

客人Ⅱ：您的话语太过晦涩难懂了，格蕾丝女士。如果这是一出情景剧，我希望您与您的道具演员们能立刻停止它，这一点儿也不好笑！
Guest II: If this is some kind of joke, Captain, I don't find it funny! So how about you knock it off!

淑女格蕾丝：您的意思是……您打算放弃前往新时代的宝贵名额？
Ms. Grace: There's no joke at all. Unless you plan on throwing away your precious opportunity to join us in the new era.

客人Ⅱ：什么新时代旧时代的……我半个字也听不懂！
Guest II: What the hell is that supposed to mean? Have you gone insane!?

满脸怒容的客人们正欲离开，脸覆面具的年轻人毫不客气地拦住了他们。
In their fear and anger, the guests make to leave, but a young man in a mask swiftly blocks the doorway.

托阿：不许污蔑我们的救世主——！
Toa: How dare you blaspheme our savior?!

塞洛尼：托阿……你太激动了……戴上面具之后，你就像完全变了个人……
Selone: Toa, ever since you put on that mask, you've been acting strangely, like a different person.

来自好友口中的古怪腔调格外刺耳。
She can hardly recognize her dear friend at all.

托阿：自从离开麦黎以后，我从没感觉脑袋如此清晰过……塞洛尼。
Toa: You're wrong, Selone! I was lost after we left Meli. But now, I've never felt so certain of myself.

托阿：你也应该为之后的面具试炼多做些准备的。我可不希望到了新时代之后，我们在独木舟赛上落败。
Toa: You must ready yourself for the mask trial, too. We must all be willing to sacrifice to bring our people into the new era!

他骄傲地拍了拍胸膛，居高临下地蔑视着瑟瑟发抖的众人。
He proudly pounds his chest as he glares disdainfully at the trembling crowd before him.

托阿：而他们，这些愚昧无知的外乡人……哼，他们永远不会理解自己做错了什么，又将会承受什么样的惩罚！
Toa: As for these ignorant outsiders, hmph, they will never understand the depth of the crimes they've committed or the punishment they deserve!

卡穆塔：托阿，冷静点儿……没必要理会这些家伙，他们在乎的只有自己。
Kamuta: Calm down, Toa. Don't bother with these outsiders. They only care about themselves.

卡穆塔：——只有“暴雨”，才能够为我们改变这一切！
Kamuta: Only the "Storm" can bring the change we need.

古怪的面具、狂热的谶言、叮叮作响的畸形贝壳，在一台从未预告的舞台剧上尽情舞蹈着。
With bizarre masks, fervent prophecies, and the clinking of misshapen shells, they perform their unannounced stage play.

“观众”们瑟缩着挤作一团。
Its "audience" cowers together in fear.

客人Ⅰ：疯……疯子！
Guest I: Lunatics!

十四行诗：司辰，我听错了么？……那位先生在宣扬“暴雨”！
Sonetto: Timekeeper, it seems as though the islanders aboard are working with Manus Vindictae!

维尔汀：重塑之手一定还藏着更多的后手，我们必须尽快向外求援。
Vertin: There's no telling what else the Manus have up their sleeve. We need to call for support as soon as possible.

十四行诗：可我们的通讯器信号已经被阻断了……
Sonetto: But our communications are jammed.

维尔汀：星锑，你能联系上乌尔里希吗？
Vertin: Regulus, are you able to reach Mr. Ulrich?

星锑：把“小东西”还给我以后，它就喊着什么“声波频率”、“非对称核素R浓度”之类的话，抱着那台怪声怪叫的机器跑得没影了。
Regulus: I should be. I've got no clue where he's at now. He dashed off with the roaring machine, mumbling something about "sound wave frequency" and "nuclide R."

星锑：让我试试吧……如果我还能回想起科算中心的内部频段的话！
Regulus: Still, I might as well give it a shot, if I can still recall Laplace's internal frequency, that is.

维尔汀：十四行诗，我们必须尽可能安抚更多的人，以免出现更严重的混乱。
Vertin: Sonetto, we must calm the situation before things escalate further.

十四行诗：是——！
Sonetto: On it!

命令有条不紊地下达着。
Orders are issued methodically.

台上的女士饶有兴趣地望着那一抹融入人群的蓝灰色礼帽，无声地笑了笑。
Grace watches with interest as a navy top hat moves through the crowd. A gentle smile creeps across her face.

淑女格蕾丝：先生们，女士们。
Ms. Grace: Ladies and gentlemen.

淑女格蕾丝：也许你们还不理解，“暴雨”究竟意味着什么。
Ms. Grace: Perhaps you have yet to understand what the "Storm" really is.

客人Ⅰ：格蕾丝女士，我可是清楚地记得你们宣传单上的内容。
Guest I: No, perhaps we don't. Because I remember what you wrote in all the flyers!

客人Ⅰ：“自由海风号”采用了双壳体设计，配备了最先进的船稳系统与国际通信系统，确保在任何情况下都能与陆地基地和其他船只保持联系……
Guest I: The "Free Breeze" is equipped with a double-hull and the most advanced communication systems available, capable of contacting rescue and support under any circumstances.

客人Ⅱ：你们保证过任何恶劣的天气都不会对“自由海风号”产生任何损坏。
Guest II: Yeah, and something about a stabilizing system. Why should we be worried about some heavy weather?

客人Ⅱ：难道这些宣传语都不过是夸大其词吗——！
Guest II: Or were you lying to us?

淑女格蕾丝：它们当然是真的，马修先生。
Ms. Grace: Oh, the specifications of the ship are all very much true. No natural weather phenomenon could endanger us here.

淑女格蕾丝：但这些脆弱的、毫无意义的设备，又如何能抵挡一场真正的、足以倾覆世界的“暴雨”呢？
Ms. Grace: However, the "Storm" I speak of is not a mere matter of churning wind and thunder. And no double-hull nor stabilizing system could stand against it.

客人Ⅰ：……您口中的“暴雨”究竟是什么？
Guest I: So, what the hell is this "Storm"?

淑女格蕾丝：一台根治所有弊病的手术。
Ms. Grace: It is a cleansing—a deluge that will come to eradicate all the sickness of this world.

客人众：——！
Guests: ...!

淑女格蕾丝：它向我们索取一点儿无关紧要的代价，又一次次给予我们回到过去的机会。
Ms. Grace: And an opportunity, a chance to reverse our course. All that is asked of you is an insignificant price.

客人Ⅱ：回到过去……代价……您究竟在说些什么呀……
Guest II: Reverse? Price? What are you talking about?

淑女格蕾丝：在90年代，那些消费主义的血管都成了电线；80年代，愚笨的脑袋被变成了一个个立体几何。而60年代就更有意思了——
Ms. Grace: In the '90s, veins turned into wires. In the '80s, skulls turned into geometric shapes. Oh, and the '60s, what fun we had then!

淑女格蕾丝：整个世界都成了一幅可笑的广告画。
Ms. Grace: The entire world became a pop art spectacle!

淑女格蕾丝：而重塑之手，为之奋斗了许多个年头。
Ms. Grace: And Manus Vindictae have seen us through each one, for all these many years.

人群的低语声越发汹涌。
The crowd's murmuring grows louder and more chaotic.

客人Ⅰ：您的意思是，这个时代也会毁灭——
Guest I: So, you're saying that the world is going to be transformed?

客人Ⅰ：连我、我们的脑袋也会变得……如此古怪吗？
Guest I: And something weird will happen to our bodies, too?

淑女格蕾丝：很遗憾，是的。
Ms. Grace: You're exactly right.

客人Ⅱ：这些都是重塑之手的手笔？……你们为什么要这么做？
Guest II: And the Manus were behind all of this? Why?!

淑女格蕾丝：您不该苛责我们的，马修先生。重塑已经尽了最大的努力。
Ms. Grace: Now, now, don't be so harsh on us. We've made heroic efforts to cleanse this world of its sickness.

淑女格蕾丝：地球上的人换了一批又一批，可他们总会犯下同样的错误。经济崩溃、环境污染、数不清的战争与硝烟……
Ms. Grace: But each generation keeps making the same mistakes: economic collapse, environmental crisis, endless wars and bloodshed ...

淑女格蕾丝：于是我们不得不一次又一次地进行新的手术，迎接一场新的“暴雨”——
Ms. Grace: We had no choice. The wounds of this world must be cleansed. One deluge at a time. Now, we are welcoming a new "Storm."

淑女格蕾丝：以回到更遥远的过去。
Ms. Grace: One that will reverse us to an even more distant past.

惊惧与恼怒相互渗透着迸出火花，有如随时迸发的火山口。
Fear and anger intertwine. The crowd is like a volcano on the verge of eruption.

客人Ⅲ：格蕾丝女士，我很确信，你现在需要一场心理治疗。
Guest III: You're a lunatic, Captain. You need your head examined.

客人Ⅲ：只有心理医生才会附和你这套灭绝人性的说法——！
Guest III: Lady, you need a psychiatrist!

客人Ⅳ：……
Guest IV: ...

客人Ⅳ：您所展示的这些……它们都是真的么？
Guest IV: But these things you're showing us ... they really happened?

淑女格蕾丝：关于这一点，你很快便能见证了。
Ms. Grace: No need to take my word for it. You will all bear witness to it soon.

人群惶悚不安。在近乎鬼魅的低吟中，连窗外泛起的海浪声都清晰可闻。
The crowd descends into a hushed panic. Every lapping of the waves can be heard amid their almost ghostly murmurs.

一个稳定人心的好时机。
This is the perfect moment to calm the crowd.

维尔汀：“暴雨”绝不会在现在发生。
Vertin: The "Storm" is NOT coming.

维尔汀：我们来自圣洛夫基金会。
Vertin: We are from the St. Pavlov Foundation—

维尔汀：一个……维护人类与神秘学家安全与权利的机构。
Vertin: An organization dedicated to the protection and rights of humans and arcanists.

淑女格蕾丝：呵。
Ms. Grace: Huh.

客人Ⅰ：……是那个官方组织！
Guest I: Ah, thank goodness!

维尔汀：我以圣洛夫基金会的“司辰”身份保证——
Vertin: As the Timekeeper of the St. Pavlov Foundation, I can assure you:

维尔汀：目前发生的一切，只是重塑之手捏造的骗局。他们希望通过仇恨与极端的言辞、夸大其词的恐吓，引导出我们内心对于未知事物的恐惧！
Vertin: What she showed you won't happen here. Manus Vindictae are just trying to manipulate you into buying into their deception and hatred. Don't give in to this false fear!

维尔汀：请大家冷静下来。
Vertin: Please, everyone, remain calm.

相似的竹制利箭又一次袭来。
Another bamboo arrow shoots through the air.

托阿：维护我们的安全，胡说八道——！
Toa: Protect us? You? Don't make me laugh!

一旁的女孩赶紧拦下急躁的同伴。
Fatutu doesn't hesitate to stop him.

图图石子：托阿……等等！
Fatutu: Toa, wait!

图图石子：如果她没有说谎，说不定……说不定基金会也能帮上我们的忙！
Fatutu: She seems trustworthy. Maybe we should listen to what they have to say.

托阿：图图石子，这就是你准备好的重建家园的“完美”计划吗？
Toa: Really? You think these people care about rebuilding our home?

托阿：要、要是他们真像自己夸耀的那么伟大，那努库泰澳、我们的家园被淹没的时候，他们又在哪里——？！
Toa: Were they there when Nukutaeao was hit by the great waves? Where was their protection then?

图图石子：不是的……我只是不希望大家做出草率的判断……不希望大家的贝壳上……出现更多斑驳的划痕……
Fatutu: I'm not sure, but I just can't bear the thought that we might make a decision we'll regret later. I don't wanna see any more cracks and scratches on our shells.

少女的失声抵不住船上客人们的窃声私语，更无法阻止族人们高涨的怒火。
Her cries cannot overpower the murmuring of the guests, nor can they quell the rising fury of her kin.

当然也抵挡不住任何一支急促飞来的毒箭。
And they certainly cannot stop another poison arrow.

十四行诗：*Ed è sübito sera——！
Sonetto: *Ed è sübito sera——！

十四行诗：场面快要失控了，司辰小心！
Sonetto: This is getting out of hand. Be careful, Timekeeper. They're coming for us!

大厅一片狼藉。
The hall is in utter disarray.

喘息声、叹气与低声的哭腔混杂在一起，像是一锅粘稠的复合汤药。
Labored breathing, sighs, and sobbing blend together like a sickly pot of thick stew.

图图石子：不……这样是不对——
Fatutu: No. This isn't right.

她还想说些什么，一阵熟悉的草药熏香猛然窜入了她的鼻腔。
She wants to say more, but the familiar scent of herbal incense suddenly overwhelms her.

安睡芦苇，在努库泰澳祭司的手术台上，它被用于减轻不必要的痛苦。
Sleepy Reeds—a herbal anesthetic used by Nukutai priests during surgeries.

卡穆塔：你需要休息，图图石子。
Kamuta: I think you need some rest, sister.

图图石子：……！
Fatutu: ...!

塞洛尼：抱歉，图图石子。
Selone: I'm sorry, Fatutu. This needs to be done.

昏迷的女孩落入另一副柔软躯体的怀中。
Selone catches her as she falls unconscious.

而另一端的争执显然要剑拔弩张得多。
The ongoing confrontation on the other side of the hall is evidently far more intense.

淑女格蕾丝：演讲很精彩，维尔汀小姐。
Ms. Grace: A fine speech, Ms. Vertin, such delectable righteous indignation.

维尔汀：放弃吧，格蕾丝女士，你欺骗不了任何人。
Vertin: Surrender, Ms. Grace. Your lies will not succeed here.

淑女格蕾丝：当然。连再小的孩子也明白这样一个浅显的道理：当谎言被揭穿时，说谎的人将遭到何等剧烈的反噬……
Ms. Grace: Why, of course. To tell a lie brings the harshest of consequences, even a kindergartener knows that.

格蕾丝环顾四周，无数道目光死死地盯着她。
Grace surveys the hall. Countless eyes are fixed on her.

愤怒、敌视、迷惘，鄙夷，她从中走过，不留下丝毫痕迹。
Anger, hostility, confusion, disdain—she has walked through it all before and never left a trace.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀：各位，我的手表能够预测“暴雨”，从它的读数就能——
Vertin: Everyone, whenever there's an imminent "Storm," my watch here starts a countdown, but there have been no signs of—

她高举手臂，另一只苍白的手却突兀地搭在了她的手上。
Grace places a delicate hand on her raised arm, interrupting her speech.

淑女格蕾丝：多么巧合啊，维尔汀小姐～我也有一块记录时间的怀表。
Ms. Grace: What a coincidence, Ms. Vertin. I so happen to have a similar device myself.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

淑女格蕾丝：三。
Ms. Grace: Three.

淑女格蕾丝：二。
Ms. Grace: Two.

维尔汀：——！
Vertin: ...!

淑女格蕾丝：一。
Ms. Grace: One.

维尔汀：——这不可能！
Vertin: Impossible!

淑女格蕾丝：维尔汀小姐。
Ms. Grace: Ms. Vertin.

淑女格蕾丝：……试图以谎言与虚假承诺蒙骗所有人的，究竟是谁呢？
Ms. Grace: As you said, lies will not succeed here. The question is, who here is the liar?

淑女格蕾丝：女士们，先生们。好好珍惜眼前的一切吧。
Ms. Grace: Ladies and gentlemen, I invite you to relish the sight before you.

淑女格蕾丝：我们迎来了……
Ms. Grace: Here we are ...

淑女格蕾丝：地球上最后的夜晚。
Ms. Grace: The last evening on earth.

LEE-14 紧急通讯 / A Call for Help

奔走的仓促身影堪堪避过了眼前的又一个集装箱，任由磁流体在缸中激烈地震荡。
The figure running down the corridor narrowly avoids another container, the ferrofluid violently swirling in his tank.

乌尔里希：见鬼，这儿就不能把这些灰扑扑的壁灯都换成卤素灯和荧光灯吗——！
Ulrich: Flux's sake, I can't work under these dim lights. Could this cheapskate cruise liner not spring for some decent halogens or fluorescents?

乌尔里希拎着手提箱在走廊上快步前行，里面的非对称核素R采集仪嘀嘀作响。
Ulrich briskly makes his way down the corridor, the asymmetrical nuclide R collector inside his briefcase buzzing loudly.

采集仪：嗡嗡——嗡嗡嗡——！
Collector: Bzz ... BZZZ ... BZZZZZZ!

乌尔里希：果然没错，越靠近这里，采集仪的指针跳跃得就越紊乱——必须尽快搞清楚这艘船当前的坐标！
Ulrich: Just as I expected. The closer I get, the more erratically the collector's gauge reacts. I must pinpoint this ship's current location as soon as possible!

乌尔里希：不、读数不对……该死的，难道它被海水腐蚀了吗？！还是说，这片海域里就存在一座“非对称核素R”的矿场？
Ulrich: Wait, the readings are a bit off. Ugh, is it because of the seawater?! Or is there an abundant load of nuclide R in this area?

它猛然蹲下身来，用力拍打箱子里的仪器。
He crouches down, laying the suitcase on the ground and pounding on it.

采集仪：———/*&@！#*（！
Collector: ———/*&@!#*(!

乌尔里希：**的[拉普拉斯脏话]，负责维护这台玩意儿的到底是哪个蠢蛋！
Ulrich: This thing must be broken. When I get my hands on the engineers responsible for maintaining this, I swear I'll—

乌尔里希：冷静想想，乌尔里希。你是不是还漏了什么重要信息……
Ulrich: Calm yourself and think, Ulrich. Did you miss anything crucial?

乌尔里希：——！
Ulrich: ...!

乌尔里希：船舱底部的电力供应室存在几摊不明黏液，尽管只经过了简易的提取处理，但样品的折光率与红外光谱都与重塑之手高度吻合。
Ulrich: Ah, yes! The oily slime in the power supply room. A rudimentary test showed that its refractive index and infrared spectrum closely matched our samples from Manus Vindictae.

通讯器：滴——滴滴——
Communicator: Beep beep! Beep beep!

突兀响起的通讯器打断了乌尔里希的沉思。
The ringing of the communicator interrupts his thoughts.

乌尔里希：嗯……星锑？
Ulrich: Huh, who's calling? Regulus?

星锑：乌尔里希组长，我终于联系上你了！
Regulus: Finally! I've been trying to reach you for a while now, Ulrich!

乌尔里希：你是来关心“人工暴雨”项目的？没那么快，实验暂时卡住了，我还不需要协助人手。
Ulrich: Calling to check on the "Artificial Storm" project, are you? I still have a way to go. I'll call you when I need a hand or two.

星锑：不、不不——！尽管原则上我和维尔汀都应该援助你的行动，但现在——
Regulus: No, no, no! I'm afraid I'm not offering you a hand. I'm asking for one!

星锑：你先来救救我们吧，组长——！这儿出现了好多重塑之手！
Regulus: We need you topside you fabulous Fish Tank! There's a gang of Manus thugs here!

乌尔里希弹射了起来。在刺耳的电流声里，它准确地抓住了最关键的信息。
Ulrich leaps to his feet. Amid the static, he has caught the most crucial piece of information.

乌尔里希：重塑之手……
Ulrich: The Manus ... huh ...

乌尔里希：他们的面具里一定保存着不少非对称核素R。说不定，我完全不需要这个时灵时不灵的鸟机器了！
Ulrich: There's sure to be a considerable amount of nuclide within their masks. Perhaps I don't need this unreliable scrap of metal after all!

乌尔里希：立刻向我报告坐标，星锑研究员！
Ulrich: Send me your location straight away, Regulus!

乌尔里希：重塑之手在哪儿？！
Ulrich: Where are these Manus thugs?!

黑压压的一片挤满了乌尔里希的全部视野。
A surging dark mass of people blocks Ulrich's view.

乌尔里希：该死的，这儿的人也太多了！
Ulrich: Flux's sake! This is a bigger crowd than I expected!

发亮的“灯泡”在人群中过于晃眼了，人们颤抖着后退。
His "bulb" stands out amidst the crowd, causing the spread of a new panic as they retreat from him.

客人Ⅰ：它是谁……？！
Guest I: Who is this walking lightbulb?!

客人Ⅱ：天呐——我、我可不想变成灯泡脑袋！
Guest II: Oh, my God! I don't want to end up with a lightbulb for a head!

乌尔里希：嗯？你们在说——
Ulrich: Huh? What are you talking ab—

重塑·门徒：禁止……ㄨ——！
Disciple of the Manus: Stop ...! *roar*

组长灵巧地躲过砸下的铁锤，剧烈的思维电流迅速漫过了对方全身。
Ulrich nimbly dodges the hammer blow, intense electrical impulses surging through his body.

重塑·门徒：唔……
Disciple of the Manus: Uggghhh!

乌尔里希：很好，又是一剂非对称核素R！
Ulrich: There we are, another extract of asymmetrical nuclide R!

摩拳擦掌的组长正打算大展拳脚，等待解救的人质们及时地阻止了它。
Though poised to take action, Ulrich is promptly stopped by the pleading hostages.

星锑：组长，我们在这儿！
Regulus: Ulrich, we're over here!

乌尔里希：看来那边有更多的重塑库存——！
Ulrich: Wonderful, I should be able to extract even more over th—

然而，发声元件中的高呼在挤入人群的一瞬便戛然而止。
He is immediately cut short upon entering the crowd.

重塑·门徒：杀……ㄙ——！
Disciple of the Manus: Kill ...! *roar*

乌尔里希堪堪躲过一击，终于成功与组织会合。
Ulrich narrowly avoids another attack before finally reuniting with the others.

乌尔里希：星锑研究员，你可没说过这儿的重塑之手有这么密集！
Ulrich: This seems to be a bit more than a gang—closer to a horde, really. You understated your situation, Regulus!

维尔汀：感谢你的增援，乌尔里希组长。
Vertin: Your help is much appreciated all the same, Mr. Ulrich.

乌尔里希：我恐怕帮不上什么忙，司辰。和重塑之手打群架还没有被列入拉普拉斯组长的考核标准。
Ulrich: Help? Well, I'm afraid I won't be much help to you, Timekeeper. Fighting is far from my specialty.

星锑：什么？！
Regulus: Blimey!

摇滚海盗只觉前途一片渺茫。
Regulus feels utterly lost.

十四行诗：那些重塑之手似乎并不打算攻击客人们，它们只是想把我们圈禁在这里……
Sonetto: They seem to be corralling the guests. At least, they aren't hurting them for now.

维尔汀：格蕾丝打算在这儿募集新的重塑信徒。
Vertin: It isn't about hurting them. She wants to recruit more followers.

无数看不出情绪的钢铁目光冰冷地扫视着大厅里的人群。
Countless steely, emotionless eyes scan the crowd with icy precision.

星锑：——难道全世界就没有一艘既不属于重塑，也不属于基金会的自由小船儿吗！
Regulus: Is there a single ship in this whole bleeding world that doesn't belong to either the Foundation or the Manus?

维尔汀：乌尔里希组长，科算中心拥有能够作为辅助验证的“暴雨”预警技术吗？
Vertin: Mr. Ulrich, does Laplace possess any technology that could detect an imminent "Storm"?

乌尔里希：第二次“暴雨”后，我们曾开展过不少相关项目，但最终都以失败告终。
Ulrich: We made several attempts to do so in the aftermath of the second "Storm," but none of them proved effective.

乌尔里希：在这之后，“暴雨”相关的一切预警事由都交给了基金会，也就是你，司辰。
Ulrich: Since that time, we've become reliant on the "Storm" alerts from the Foundation, or more specifically, from you, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：格蕾丝宣称“暴雨”即将到来，她甚至成功预言了异象的出现……
Vertin: Ms. Grace claimed that the "Storm" was coming, and she managed to accurately predict the occurrence of the anomaly outside.

维尔汀：可我的手表却没有任何变化。
Vertin: Yet, my watch has shown no sign of an imminent "Storm."

雨点不时敲打着一片漆黑的舷窗，十四行诗不自觉地捏紧了衣袖上的口子。
Light rain is tapping on the porthole. Sonetto unconsciously tightens the cuffs on her sleeve.

十四行诗：我相信您的判断，司辰。
Sonetto: In any event, I believe in you, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：谢谢你，十四行诗，但我们必须说服更多的人。
Vertin: Thank you, Sonetto. But it isn't you that I need to convince. It's them.

环顾四周，无数恐慌、怀疑、敌视的目光不曾从她们身上挪开分毫。
Countless eyes filled with fear, suspicion, and hostility remain fixed on them.

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：难怪非对称核素R的采集仪读数的显示失常了……
Ulrich: No wonder my readings were going wild.

乌尔里希：很抱歉，司辰。我无法否定“暴雨”来临的可能性。
Ulrich: Apologies, Timekeeper. Though nothing would make me happier than disproving Manus Vindictae, I can't deny the possibility that these phenomena are precursors to the "Storm."

这显然不是个令人安心的答案。
This is not a reassuring answer.

风在猎猎作响。
The wind howls fiercely.

海平面已经几乎看不见了。远处的海岛、风声与隐约可见的礁石溶在了一起，像是被抹上了一层更加漆黑的油彩。
The horizon has become almost completely obscured. Far-off islands and faintly visible reefs blend into one another, as if smeared with an even darker shade of paint.

人群三三两两地颓然坐倒，四周飘荡着隐约的抽泣声。
Amid the crowd, people slump to the ground, their sobs lingering in the air.

芭卡洛儿：大家……请冷静下来……
Barcarola: Please, everyone, listen. We have to stay calm!

努力倚靠着“啪唧盒子”站起身来，乐手重新拾起了自己的责任。
Struggling to her feet with the help of her Crackling Box, Barcarola rises to fulfill her duty once again.

芭卡洛儿：请相信我，相信“自由海风号”……
Barcarola: I ask you to put your faith in me, and in the "Free Breeze."

客人Ⅲ：早知道就不参加什么音乐派对了……
Guest III: I should have never come to this party.

客人Ⅳ：呜呜……我、我想回家，这儿太可怕了……
Guest IV: *sob* I want to go home! I'm scared.

客人Ⅴ：谁……谁能救救我们……
Guest V: Someone help us, please!

声嘶力竭的游轮乐手跌坐在地，苍白的呼吁声淹没在乱哄哄的人海里。
Barcarola's voice is utterly drowned out by the wails of the crowd.

芭卡洛儿：这、这究竟是怎么一回事呀……
Barcarola: What can I do to get these people's attention?

“咚——！”
*thud*

一声巨大的震响从船头的位置传来，晃荡的船身把许多人都甩在了地上。
A massive sound resonates from the bow of the ship, sending a vibration so strong that many are thrown to the ground.

惶恐的客人：发、发生什么了……！
Frightened Guest: What? What's happening?!

船舱广播：很抱歉，目前海面能见度低，视野受限，“自由海风号”将暂停一部分公共服务。
Cabin Announcement: Due to low visibility at sea, some public services on the "Free Breeze" will be temporarily suspended. We apologize for any inconvenience caused.

船舱广播：前方为暗礁区，覆盖范围约752海里。
Cabin Announcement: We are now entering an area of treacherous reef. During this time, there may be some sharp shifts in course.

客人众：……
Guests: ...

船舱广播：为了尽快抵达新的时代，我们将全速前进。
Cabin Announcement: In order that we might reach the new era as soon as possible, the "Free Breeze" will forge ahead at full speed.

船舱广播：请各位乘客务必减少大规模移动，抓稳扶手，以免落入海中。
Cabin Announcement: Please stay indoors and, in case of emergency, hold on to the handrails.

船舱广播：重复，请各位乘客务必减少大规模移动，抓稳扶手，以免落入海中。
Cabin Announcement: I repeat. Please stay indoors and hold on to the handrails.

惶恐的船员：格蕾丝船长，为什么“自由海风号”要在这么危险的情况下全速前进？！
Frightened Crew Member: Captain Grace, why in the world is the "Free Breeze" going full speed through these reefs?

淑女格蕾丝：当然是为了尽快抵达一个更美好的未来。
Ms. Grace: To embrace the future.

惊讶的船员：可……这样很可能会让“自由海风号”沉没！
Surprised Crew Member: But if we strike any of these reefs, the damage could be catastrophic!

淑女格蕾丝：在真正的“暴雨”前，这些又算得了什么呢？
Ms. Grace: Not as catastrophic as missing our chance to embrace the "Storm."

轻飘飘的话语被掷在了地上。
Her softly spoken words fall on deaf ears.

愤怒的客人：你这个该死的骗子，我不会再相信你的任何话术了！
Angry Guest: You deranged loon! I won't stand for this. You're just trying to scare us into joining your cult!

愤怒的客人：我要亲眼去外头看看，就现在！
Angry Guest: I'll bet there's no reef, no storm at all. This is trickery, and I intend to prove it!

淑女格蕾丝：如您所愿，先生。
Ms. Grace: Do as you wish, sir.

淑女格蕾丝：但请千万小心，外面的风浪很大。
Ms. Grace: Please watch your footing. The wind is howling outside.

船长礼貌地点了点头，大步朝着舱门走去的客人没有受到任何阻拦。
She gives a polite nod as the guest storms out of the cabin.

愤怒的客人：瞧，我现在不就好好地待在……
Angry Guest: Look, I'm standing firm as a bould—

客人踩在甲板上，像是在斯库拉巨岩与卡律布狄斯旋涡之间高歌的勇士。
The guest stands firm on the deck, like a warrior singing triumphantly between Scylla's cliffs and Charybdis' whirlpool.

直到一阵强风袭来。
That is, until he's struck by the power of the wind.

愤怒的客人：啊——
Angry Guest: Ahhhh!

拖长的痛呼声被暴风雨撕得粉碎，随后悄然隐没在一片漆黑中。
His scream is quickly drowned in the storm as he vanishes into the void.

客人众：……
Guests: ...

舱门再一次合拢了，呼啸的风声被挡在了唯一的安全居所之外。
One guest pulls the hatch closed again, blocking out the howling wind outside and returning their one safe haven to silence.

十四行诗：先生——！
Sonetto: The gentleman is gone!

维尔汀：格蕾丝，你这是在杀人。
Vertin: Ms. Grace, you murdered that man.

淑女格蕾丝：真奇怪，选择权不是在各位自己的手里吗？
Ms. Grace: What an utterly baffling accusation. Have I shot him, stabbed him? No. The choice was always in his own hands, wasn't it?

厅堂一片寂静。
The hall remains silent.

许久，有人战战兢兢地站起身来。
After a long while, one quivering guest steps forward.

惶恐的客人：格、格蕾丝小姐……只要我们加入了重塑，您便能拯救我们吗？
Frightened Guest: Captain, you said you'd save us if we joined Manus Vindictae, right?

淑女格蕾丝：拯救当然不是这么轻易的事，尤金先生……你还需要通过一场小小的考验。
Ms. Grace: It's not as simple as that, I'm afraid. But relax; there is only a small trial to pass, then the new era awaits.

顺着船长的目光，那张令人眼熟的古铜色面具无声无息地俯扣在桌上。
She gestures to an all-too-familiar mask sitting silently on the table.

淑女格蕾丝：试炼中，你只会感受到一点儿轻微的迷惘。
Ms. Grace: You may feel a little disoriented, but your body will be in no danger.

犹豫的客人：戴上面具后，我们真的会从这场噩梦中醒过来吗……？
Hesitant Guest: So, if we all put on these masks, then this nightmare will be over?

激进的客人：反正情况也不会比现在更糟糕了，不是吗？把面具给我——
Desperate Guest: Things can't get any worse than they are now, can they? Give me the mask!

胆怯的孩子：呜呜……
Scared Child: *sob*

淑女格蕾丝：当然，迷途的羔羊们啊，这将是你们对围栏最勇敢的一次翻跃。
Ms. Grace: O, lost lambs, this will be the bravest leap you've ever taken over the fence.

橘发姑娘勇敢地站起身来。
Sonetto turns to the crowd.

十四行诗：各位，不要再被重塑蒙蔽了。
Sonetto: Please, everyone. Don't fall for her lies!

十四行诗：你们被剥夺了真正的选择权，重塑在隐瞒事实！
Sonetto: She doesn't offer you salvation, but slavery! Don't give up your free will!

星锑：说的没错，我们是自由的，就像音乐！
Regulus: Listen to her! We've got to be free to choose for ourselves!

星锑：每一位听众都应该有自由选择的权利，不论是摇滚、布鲁斯还是古典乐，又或是一段噪音！
Regulus: Rock, blues, classical, or heavy metal—it doesn't matter! Each of us is our own melody! The Manus will take that from you!

乌尔里希：采取行动吧，司辰。
Ulrich: It's our turn, Timekeeper.

乌尔里希：乌尔里希，接受您的调遣！
Ulrich: I'm at your command!

维尔汀：优先安抚民众。
Vertin: Alright. Our priority is to bring the guests back to their senses.

信者与不信者有如天平的两端，再高声的呼喊也无法压过近在眼前的漆黑现实。
The guests remain in turmoil as the believers and skeptics argue among one another.

恐惧在人群之中迅速扩散，像是滴入水中的墨迹。
Fear and confusion quickly spread through them, like ink in water, and soon ...

成功的选民Ⅰ：哈哈——我戴上面具了！
Trial Taker I: Haha! I did it! I put on the mask!

成功的选民Ⅱ：我、我也得救了……
Trial Taker II: I-I'm saved!

成功的选民Ⅱ：感谢您，伟大的格蕾丝女士！
Trial Taker II: Thank you, thank you, Ms. Grace!

失败的选民Ⅰ：痛……太痛了……
Forsaken I: It hurts! It hurts so much.

失败的选民Ⅱ：格蕾丝女士，救……ㄥ——
Forsaken II: Help ... *roar*

十四行诗：糟糕，越来越多人倒向重塑之手了……
Sonetto: We can't let more of these people give in to their fears!

愈发式微的声音被淹没在汹涌的人潮之中。
Her voice is almost entirely drowned out by the roaring crowd.

卡穆塔：将这些死不悔改的家伙关押起来——！
Kamuta: These stubborn outsiders must be silenced! Take them away!

卡穆塔：努库泰澳的复仇大业，就从他们开始吧。
Kamuta: Let our revenge begin with them!

托阿：——是！
Toa: For Nukutaeao!

卡穆塔：塞洛尼，把我那不成器的妹妹送回房间。软弱蒙蔽了她的智慧，她的贝壳告诉我，她还不足以应付生活的剧变。
Kamuta: Selone, take my troubled sister back to her room. The softness of her heart has clouded her judgment, just as her shell shows.

塞洛尼：首领……
Selone: Chief ...

漆黑的墨渍几乎晕染了每一个人的脸。
Black ink seems to stain every one of their faces.

生活的剧变笼罩了努库泰澳人，当然也摧毁了更多无名的普通人。
The upheaval has engulfed the Nukutai along with countless other innocents.

无知的孩子：妈妈……我想回家……
Child: Mum, I wanna go home.

痛苦的母亲：好孩子，想点开心的事儿……
Grieving Mother: Just think of something happy, sweetheart.

痛苦的母亲：爸爸肯定为你买了新款的汽车玩具……只要戴上了面具……我们就能回家了……
Grieving Mother: Remember that toy your dad bought you? It's waiting for you at home. We'll be there soon. Just put this on. We'll be there soon.

在母亲颤抖的手中，那副面具缓缓贴向了孩子一无所知、泛着泪光的面庞。
Trembling, the mother slowly lowers the mask to her child's face.

芭卡洛儿：不——！
Barcarola: No!

恍惚了许久的游轮乐手本能般地扑上前去，将重塑面具推到一旁。
Barcarola lunges forward, knocking the Manus mask out of her hand.

淑女格蕾丝：打扰客人是相当不礼貌的，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Ms. Grace: I don't believe your job description permits you to interrupt our guests, does it, Ms. Barcarola?

芭卡洛儿：格蕾丝女士……“自由海风号”……我们的客人……这儿的一切都变得好陌生……
Barcarola: I don't understand, Captain Grace. Why are you letting this happen? Why are you doing this?

亲切的船长拾起了那副仍发着嗡鸣的面具，她细心地拭去上面沾染的灰，又不紧不慢地走上前来。
Grace carefully picks up the still-humming mask and brushes off the dust. She steps forward.

淑女格蕾丝：上前来，好姑娘——就像你一直站在“自由海风号”上那样。
Ms. Grace: Cheer up, dear girl. Hold that chin up high. Now that's the spirit, the brightest star of the "Free Breeze" forever and always.

淑女格蕾丝：瞧，马修先生、艾琳娜小姐、卡米拉女士……多少熟悉的客人们都在巴巴地张望着你呢？
Ms. Grace: Just take a look. Your loyal fans are waiting for your next show.

淑女格蕾丝：你不打算再为他们弹奏那些美好的歌儿了吗？
