Ms. Grace: Won't you play some of those beautiful melodies for them again?

芭卡洛儿：格蕾丝船长，我不明白您说的那些……世界的疾病……“暴雨”……无比美好的新时代……
Barcarola: But Ms. Grace, what do you mean by the "Storm" and diseases of the world, and this new era?

淑女格蕾丝：当然是最简单的字面意思了～我们的海上明珠，万众瞩目的游轮甜心。
Ms. Grace: Oh, it's all so much simpler than you think, Ms. Barcarola.

淑女格蕾丝：那些糟糕的、令人厌烦的、你再也不想见到的东西都会消失得彻彻底底，连一点儿骨头渣滓都不会剩下——
Ms. Grace: In the new era, all that you hated in this time will vanish, as if it had never been there at all.

淑女格蕾丝：噢，就像克雷莫纳，古板陈腐的小提琴之乡，你发誓绝不会回去的地方……你不是一直讨厌着那儿吗？
Ms. Grace: The "City of Violins" you swore you'd never return to will soon be forgotten, washed away in the coming "Storm."

淑女格蕾丝：现在你总算有机会离开它了，永远地。
Ms. Grace: Your wish will come true. You'll never need return to it. You couldn't even if you tried.

芭卡洛儿：永远……？
Barcarola: Never again?

曾经熟稔的一切好似阴魂不散的幽灵，它们沉默着升腾起来，占领了脑海中的全部空档。
Memories of her home return to her as if she were there just yesterday.

高耸的大教堂与钟楼，吱呀作响的码头浮桥，从不曾记下她名字的克雷莫纳音乐节选手名单，遥遥飘来的托尔塔蛋糕与奶酪烩饭的香气。
The towering bell tower of the cathedral, the creaking footbridges of the dock, the Cremona Music Festival competitor list that never displayed her name, and the distant scent of torta and risotto.

像是一阵遥远的风儿，它与那张陈旧的成绩单与鲜红笔迹阔别了许久，却又偶然地、无比真实地在眼前呼啸着掠过。
She has been far away from that world for so long, yet there before her eyes, she sees it again: the report card scribbled with red ink soaring on the wind.

淑女格蕾丝：“如果留在那个糟糕的地方，便永远不会有芭卡洛儿和她的啪唧匣子了”——你正是这么说的，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Ms. Grace: What was it you said about that rotten little town? The monotony of sound, the disappointment of those old fossils and their little worlds—is that right?

芭卡洛儿：“我永远也不会回到那儿——！”……
Barcarola: Yes. I said I never, never wanted to go back.

淑女格蕾丝：这次可要拿稳它了，好姑娘。
Ms. Grace: Now, keep your hand steady this time, my dear. You must be certain.

金属与手背抵在一起，冰冷的触感让她打了个激灵。
Cold metal meets Barcarola's hand, jolting her back to reality.

微微发颤的手逃难般地抚上了怀中古怪而沉默的巨大乐器。
Her trembling hand reaches for her peculiar, silent instrument. She cradles it in her arms.

芭卡洛儿：啪唧匣子……
Barcarola: My Crackling Box.

黏合剂与木质结构的连接件，熟悉的触感令她安心。像是汲取氧气的运动员，她的手指贪婪地拂过上面的每一寸纹理。
The familiar texture of the adhesive holding it together reassures her. She runs her fingers over it before greedily moving on to the rest.

在繁复而精巧的乐器嵌合体中，她摸到了一个熟悉的轮廓。
Then, in the intricate structure of the instrument she created, she finds all the pieces of that familiar thing.

指板，琴弦边，音柱，琴桥，调弦器……
A fingerboard, strings, a sound post, a bridge, tuning pegs ...

一柄单调的小提琴。
A violin.

芭卡洛儿：不——
Barcarola: No!

一股不知从何而来的温度令她推开了那副面具。
A sudden warmth bursts forth within her, urging her to push the mask aside.

LEE-15 海风儿在翻阅 / A New Page Turned

塞洛尼：托阿，我们只需要把这些家伙关起来，而不需要……处决他们？
Selone: I-I'm confused, Toa. If these disbelievers are a danger to our vengeance, why are we only locking them up? Shouldn't we just toss them overboard?

托阿：没、没错！
Toa: T-The chief wants Fatutu to decide how to deal with them! A test of her allegiance and her conviction.

卡穆塔更希望图图石子成熟起来，由她来决定如何处置这些坏家伙！

托阿：当然，得在图图石子戴上面具之后。
Toa: After she puts on the mask, of course.

塞洛尼：……
Selone: ...

托阿：别害怕，塞洛尼，重塑的试炼并不困难。你瞧，我不也好好的吗？
Toa: You're afraid, Selone. Don't be. The trial isn't difficult. I see things so clearly now.

塞洛尼：我不知道，托阿，我不知道。
Selone: I don't know, Toa.

塞洛尼：卡穆塔的命令也许是对的，可我还是感到害怕……
Selone: I trust in Kamuta's leadership, but still ...

托阿：难道你要成为最后一批戴上面具的懦夫吗？！
Toa: Just like always. You're waiting for everyone else to test the water before you jump.

塞洛尼：我……我只是觉得这样不对……
Selone: I-I just feel that there's something wrong.

塞洛尼：托阿，你在握着锁链的时候，手指不也一直在发抖吗？
Selone: You say you're not afraid, Toa, but I hear your chains clinking. You're shaking, too.

托阿：闭、闭嘴——这儿可是冷库，难不成你认为我、我在害怕吗？！
Toa: Shut up! That's only because we're in a freezer!

一处令人熟悉的居所。
A familiar place.

星锑：天呐！难道我在20岁以前就能达成环游世界监狱的成就吗？——这都快超过我待在家里的时间了！
Regulus: Blimey, locked up again. At this rate, I'll have my "imprisoned on all seven continents" bingo card before I turn 20. It's an honest bet I've spent more time behind bars than my own home.

十四行诗：星锑，你也有自己的家吗？
Sonetto: I wasn't aware that you had a home, beyond the ship, I mean.

星锑：毫无疑问，朋友。整座伦敦城都是我的家。
Regulus: Course I do, love! The whole of London is my home!

星锑：我在那儿生活，为那儿无数的人们与他们热爱的音乐而战斗，你怎么能忽视那座城市在我灵魂上留下的烙印！
Regulus: I've walked its streets! I've inspired its people! I fought for its music! Its spirit's stamped on my very soul!

她振振有词地疾呼着，在不大的牢房里来回踱步。
She paces back and forth in the cell as she passionately proclaims her cause.

反叛艺术家常有如此激进的表现。
Rebellious artists often fall into such radical expressions.

星锑：伦敦永远都会为APPLe号留下一处停泊的港湾，以致敬——
Regulus: And jolly old London will always have a harbor open for this captain and her APPLe as a token of—wait, Barcarola, what are you doing here?!

等等，芭卡洛儿，你怎么在这儿？！

无比眼熟的古怪轮廓突兀地出现在监牢大门的窗口中。
A familiar silhouette appears in the prison door window.

星锑：该死的，我就知道这些铁皮脑袋不会放过任何一位艺术家，它们试图打压音乐品味远超它们的所有人——
Regulus: Well, I suppose those tinheads aren't the type to appreciate a true artist. Jealous of our talents, no doubt.

托阿：芭卡洛儿小姐……尽管你是格蕾丝船长口中的贵宾。但在正式加入重塑之手前，你不应该参与我们的行刑工作！
Toa: Ms. Grace said to give you special treatment, Barcarola. But I warn you, these prisoners are ours to deal with. So don't get any ideas!

星锑：……什么？
Regulus: What?!

星锑：芭卡洛儿？——你与那群音乐笨蛋同流合污了？！
Regulus: Barcarola, don't tell me you're siding with these tone-deaf goons!

铁门缓缓打开，星锑踉跄地退后了几步。
The door creaks open, and Regulus stumbles back a few steps.

映入眼中的并非令人眼熟的游轮甜心、优雅的演奏家，只是一副泪眼涟涟、甚至有些狼狈的无助脸庞。
What greets her isn't the familiar sweetheart of the ship, nor the elegant musician, but a tear-streaked, almost disheveled and helpless face of a young girl.

星锑：——！
Regulus: ...!

芭卡洛儿：我、我不知道……我的选择是对的吗……
Barcarola: I'm just confused. It seems like there's only one way forward, but ...

芭卡洛儿：格蕾丝女士告诉我们，“暴雨”会改变我们的时代，只有戴上面具的船员们才能免于回溯。
Barcarola: The captain said that only those who put on the mask have a chance to survive the "Storm."

芭卡洛儿：……而那些不被选召的可怜人，他们会和这个时代一同消失得无影无踪。
Barcarola: And that everyone else, the unbelievers, the forsaken ... will vanish.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

芭卡洛儿：维尔汀小姐。
Barcarola: Ms. Vertin.

Barcarola: Tell me the truth, please. What will happen if I put it on?

她的声音几乎脱力。
Her voice is almost entirely drained of strength.

芭卡洛儿：如果我真的抵达了格蕾丝女士口中的、那无比美好的崭新时代……我记忆中的街道，教堂与钟楼，邻居与朋友们的狗儿……
Barcarola: If I reach this beautiful new era Ms. Grace speaks of, what will happen to Cremona? The streets, the cathedral, all of the people I grew up with ...

芭卡洛儿：我……还能找回它们吗？
Barcarola: Will I ever be able to see them again?

维尔汀：很遗憾……
Vertin: The truth is ...

维尔汀：世界上仍会有一座名为“克雷莫纳”的小镇，但……
Vertin: After the "Storm," there may still be a Cremona, but ...

维尔汀：在你记忆中的每一张脸庞、每一首曲子，甚至是每一块砖瓦，它们都将变成另一种模样。
Vertin: Every face, every song, every brick from each house to the cathedral—will be different.

维尔汀：“暴雨”会冲刷走这个时代的所有痕迹。
Vertin: The "Storm" will wash away almost all traces of this era.

芭卡洛儿：……
Barcarola: ...

维尔汀：我希望你能帮助我们，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Vertin: But you can still help us, Ms. Barcarola.

芭卡洛儿：我……吗？
Barcarola: Me? How?

维尔汀：不论“暴雨”何时到来，我们都应该努力到最后一刻——
Vertin: No matter when the "Storm" arrives, we must fight till the last second.

维尔汀：让更多的人活下来。
Vertin: To help as many people survive as possible.

芭卡洛儿：我、我得好好想一想……
Barcarola: I-I need some time to think.

“哐——”
*bang*

门又一次被推开了。
The door slams open again.

塞洛尼：对“囚犯”的探视时间已经结束了，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Selone: Your visiting time is over, Barcarola.

塞洛尼：格蕾丝女士对你的优待并不包括住在监牢里，你必须马上离开。
Selone: Better not overstay your welcome.

芭卡洛儿擦了擦眼角的泪水，深吸了几口气，努力让自己平静下来。
Barcarola wipes the tears from her eyes, taking deep breaths as she tries to steady herself.

芭卡洛儿：女士，我还有最后一个问题。
Barcarola: I have another request.

芭卡洛儿：请告诉我，图图石子在哪儿？
Barcarola: Could you tell me where Fatutu is?

塞洛尼：……
Selone: ...

芭卡洛儿：别误会，我只是想去看看她，以一位朋友的身份。
Barcarola: I just wanna see her, is all, as a friend.

船长室显然不需要如外头一般酝酿某种刻意的可怖气氛。
The captain's cabin is calm compared to the carefully crafted atmosphere of fear and eeriness on the rest of the ship.

“咔嗒——”
*click*

旋钮被轻轻地拨动，切换到另一个更隐秘的频段。
A delicate hand turns the knob on the radio, switching it to a more secretive frequency.

？？？：祂已了然你的奉献。
???: THEY are well aware of your contribution.

淑女格蕾丝：我们追奉至高的福音，我们抛却骨肉与思想。
Ms. Grace: To follow THEIR divine guidance, we must be willing to renounce both body and mind.

勿忘我：做得很好，格蕾丝使徒。
Forget Me Not: Well done, Apostle Grace.

勿忘我：那些愚蠢的灰白帽子永远都在不遗余力地逗人发笑，居然误以为自己抓住了我们的小辫子……我都已经迫不及待见证他们捶胸顿足的夸张表演了。
Forget Me Not: To think those white suits are so sure they've caught us off guard. Oh, I can't wait to see the despair in their eyes when they fall flat on their faces.

勿忘我：“为本次调查行动的牺牲者默哀，他们是一座永恒的丰碑。”
Forget Me Not: I can imagine it now: "Let us all observe a moment of silence for those lost in our latest failure. Let us honor them as eternal monuments of our cause." How pathetic.

嘈杂的信号如实传递着对方情绪里的讥讽。
Despite the static, the ridicule in Forget Me Not's tone rings clear.

勿忘我：对了，听说一只科算中心的老鼠潜入了“自由海风号”？
Forget Me Not: Oh, and what about this Laplace rat that I hear has stowed away on board?

淑女格蕾丝：乌尔里希，本体为磁流体，是一位意识唤醒者。它参与了之前平衡伞的研发。
Ms. Grace: Yes, the Awakened ferrofluid sample named Ulrich—one of the major contributors to the creation of the Equilibrium Umbrella.

勿忘我：哼，希望平衡伞能帮上它的忙吧。
Forget Me Not: Hmph, let's hope his little umbrella keeps him dry.

勿忘我：否则，对于磁流体而言，这倒是一个回归故土的好时机了。
Forget Me Not: Because if he isn't careful, he may end up in much deeper waters.

淑女格蕾丝：另外，仪式材料的收集已基本完成，目前仅剩小部分材料尚未取得……我们正在加快推进新信徒们的重塑仪式。
Ms. Grace: The ritual materials are nearly assembled, and we are accelerating our recruitment.

淑女格蕾丝：努库泰澳的象形贝壳仍有部分欠缺。如果没能让他们的自我意识浸润在纯粹的负面情绪中，我担心会影响仪式的稳定性。
Ms. Grace: But the Nukutai Spirit Shells have yet to reach their most optimal form. It could hinder the stability of the ritual if they're not immersed in pure negative emotion.

勿忘我：尽管我们希望能得到更加完美的象形贝壳，但在必要的时候，贝壳本身才是最重要的，无论它们以何种形态存在。
Forget Me Not: Your commitment to quality is impressive, but the shells needn't be perfect to perform as needed. Do not waste time unnecessarily.

勿忘我：你明白了么？小格蕾丝。
Forget Me Not: Do you understand, Apostle Grace?

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

勿忘我：我想你已经充分吸收了上一次失败的教训。
Forget Me Not: I trust you've learned from the last failure.

淑女格蕾丝：是的。
Ms. Grace: Yes.

勿忘我：很好，我们已经布设好了传送术阵，当你们的船抵达坐标后，立刻发动咒语……术阵时间有限，不要浪费时间。
Forget Me Not: Excellent. A teleportation array has been set up for you. But it will last only a short while. You must begin the ritual as soon as your ship reaches the target location.

勿忘我：重塑期待你的回归。
Forget Me Not: Manus Vindictae awaits your return.

淑女格蕾丝：谨遵祂的指引，勿忘我先生。
Ms. Grace: Yes, Mr. Forget Me Not. I will always follow THEIR guidance.

通讯器毫无征兆地失去了信号，徒留无休止的空洞回声。
The communication ends, leaving only the echo of the final words spoken through it.

苍白的手腕轻轻抬起，摩挲着一颗颗纹路驳杂的象形贝壳。
Grace raises a pale hand and gently caresses the intricate patterns on the Spirit Shells.

沉默笼罩了这片不大的空间。
Silence fills the room.

LEE-16 意大利之歌 / Barcarolle

十四行诗：*Ed è sübito sera——！
Sonetto: *Ed è sübito sera——！

十四行诗：不行……船舱的内壁似乎做了加固处理，我的神秘术根本无法打破它。
Sonetto: It's no use. The cabin's wall is heavily reinforced. My arcane skills can barely scratch it.

星锑：那个可恶的船长……难怪她没有收缴我们的武器！
Regulus: I guess that's why they didn't even bother taking our stuff.

星锑：乌尔里希组长，难道你没有随身携带什么神奇的、能帮助我们离开这儿的小发明吗？
Regulus: Ulrich, you've got to have some miraculous trinkets up your sleeve to bust us out, right?

星锑：你可是科算中心的骄傲啊！
Regulus: You're the pride of Laplace, after all!

乌尔里希：科算中心可不是什么暴力机构，星锑。
Ulrich: Laplace is not a circus, and I am no magician.

乌尔里希：但我确实携带了一些可能有效的工具。
Ulrich: But I may have something that can help.

乌尔里希：305.7千克爆炸当量的反应堆与纸莎草毛虫溶剂。
Ulrich: I have a small amount of TNT and some Papyrpillar Solvents.

乌尔里希：前者产生的冲击波大概会在炸开舱门之前先给我们的身子开几个洞。
Ulrich: The former can blast the door open; however, it will likely blast us to smithereens along with it.

乌尔里希：当然，后者就要安全得多了，我们需要做的只是将它们抹在墙上，然后在这儿静坐两天。
Ulrich: The latter is much safer, of course. All we need to do is apply it to the walls and then wait for a couple of days.

星锑：那我们是彻底完蛋了吗？
Regulus: We're abso-frigging-lutely screwed, aren't we?

乌尔里希：当然不是。
Ulrich: Don't be glum, Ms. Regulus. We aren't beat yet.

乌尔里希将那些显然难堪大用的工具们随手搁在一旁。
Ulrich sets aside the obviously useless tools.

眼下，它有了更重要的发现。
He has made a much more important discovery.

乌尔里希：司辰，看看这个吧。
Ulrich: Take a look at this, Timekeeper.

乌尔里希：我的数据箱记录了“自由海风号”从悉尼港出发以来的移动轨迹。
Ulrich: I've been recording the "Free Breeze's" heading since it left Sydney.

乌尔里希：遗憾的是，在启航一段时间后，我们的信号就遭到了屏蔽。
Ulrich: Though, unfortunately, something has been jamming our signal.

乌尔里希：坐标轨迹显示，“自由海风号”并没有像传单所宣传的那样回归意大利。
Ulrich: Yet, we can still extrapolate from my earlier readings that this ship is not heading to its advertised destination.

维尔汀：重塑的目的地难道是……
Vertin: It's heading steadily ...

维尔汀：——南方。
Vertin: Southward.

乌尔里希：很有可能。
Ulrich: It appears so.

维尔汀的思绪显然比磁流体的震动更加剧烈。
Her thoughts churn more violently than the ferrofluid's vibrations.

维尔汀：“暴雨”的预言、太阳的消失、重塑之手的面具试炼、“自由海风号”的加速……
Vertin: The forecast of the "Storm," the sudden eclipse, the mask trials, and the speed at which the "Free Breeze" is now heading.

维尔汀：如果重塑之手计划筛选出更优秀的信徒，他们理应为愿意戴上面具的人们留出更充分的准备时间。
Vertin: If all they wanted was to recruit more followers, they would allow for more time to convince the others.

维尔汀：如果“暴雨”即将到来，格蕾丝便不应该冒着巨大的风险授意“自由海风号”加速。
Vertin: However, if the "Storm" is indeed coming, then why would we be racing forward through these reefs?

维尔汀：重塑之手的行动并非为了筛选，反而更像是……
Vertin: Their actions don't seem to be aimed at recruiting nor at passing through the "Storm." Rather, they seem to be aimed at ...

乌尔里希&维尔汀：一种恐吓。
Ulrich & Vertin: Intimidation.

监牢里的空气似乎短暂地停滞了。
The air in the cell seems to momentarily stagnate.

乌尔里希：另一种可能是，“暴雨”本身便是一场巨大的骗局。
Ulrich: This would add weight to the possibility that the "Storm" they're promising is only a trick to inspire more fear.

乌尔里希：但很抱歉，身为科研工作者，我必须考虑“暴雨”发生的可能，哪怕微乎其微。
Ulrich: That said, we must consider the chance of the "Storm" occurring, no matter how slim it may seem.

乌尔里希郑重地站直了身子，它并未因为任何一种假设而动摇。
Ulrich stands tall, unwavering in the face of conjecture.

乌尔里希：在真正的答案出现以前，我们能坚信的，唯有手中的仪器与眼前的读数。
Ulrich: Until the truth is ultimately revealed, all we can rely on are the instruments in our hands and the readings before our eyes.

维尔汀：我赞成你的想法，乌尔里希组长。
Vertin: Then we're agreed, Mr. Ulrich.

维尔汀：不论“暴雨”来临与否，我们都需要做更全面的准备。
Vertin: Whether the "Storm" is coming or not, we need to be well-prepared.

乌尔里希：很高兴我们能达成一致。
Ulrich: I'm glad we're on the same page.

维尔汀：我们携带了不少平衡伞，箱子也能够作为临时的避难所。
Vertin: We've brought quite a few Equilibrium Umbrellas with us, and my suitcase can also serve as a temporary shelter.

维尔汀：它能够让神秘学家们免于回溯，但……箱子无法覆盖普通的人类。
Vertin: However, that will do nothing for the humans aboard.

乌尔里希：传闻居然是真的——？！
Ulrich: Your suitcase? Then the rumors are true!

乌尔里希：难怪一向保守的基金会也愿意让你独立组建一支小队。
Ulrich: No wonder the stick-in-the-mud Foundation greenlit you to build your own team.

乌尔里希久久地凝视着维尔汀手中的箱子。
Ulrich stares intently at the suitcase held in her hands.

乌尔里希：真希望有一天我能参与它的研究！
Ulrich: Ah, I would give anything to analyze it one day!

维尔汀：会有那么一天的。
Vertin: I'm certain that day will come, eventually.

Vertin: Sonetto, how many Equilibrium Umbrellas have we brought exactly?

Sonetto: Ermm. Exactly 73.

一个足以覆盖所有箱中同僚的数字。
A sufficient number to cover all the comrades in the suitcase.

但遗憾的是，它远远无法企及“自由海风号”上的近千名人类船员。
Unfortunately, it's far from enough to account for the nearly thousand people aboard the "Free Breeze."

Vertin: Mr. Ulrich, you're not speaking of your "Artificial Storm" experiment, are you? We have neither the time nor personnel to assist you with it.

维尔汀：希望你能慎重考虑。
Vertin: And I implore you to consider the potential risks, especially in attempting it alone and under these conditions.

组长仍兴致勃勃地介绍着，丝毫没有在意对方的担忧。
Ulrich eagerly continues his explanation, heedless of his companion's concerns.

乌尔里希：多亏了那些石油脑袋，我从他们的面具里搞到了不少非对称核素R，已经足够完成余下材料的稳定性实验了。
Ulrich: Irrespective of your concerns, thanks to those oily heads and their quirky masks, I've acquired more than enough asymmetrical nuclide R to perform the immutability experiments.

维尔汀：可你似乎从未提及过实验的副作用，乌尔里希组长。
Vertin: But have you considered the side effects, Mr. Ulrich?

磁流体的运转停滞了一瞬。
The ferrofluid halts for a moment.

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：好吧好吧，“人工暴雨”实验确实存在一丁点儿无可避免的副作用。
Ulrich: It's true. There is the risk of unavoidable side effects the experiments pose.

乌尔里希：我承认，在实验室里，我们能有充分的时间找到更合适的实验人员。
Ulrich: And I admit that, if I were in the lab, we would use much more time and caution.

乌尔里希：但在这儿，能感染时代病的只剩下我自己。
Ulrich: But on this ship, I am the only one capable of withstanding the effects of the Storm Syndrome.

看似平淡的语气却依然引来了新一轮的抗议。
Despite his seemingly calm tone, a new round of protestation is volleyed his way.

星锑：什么——？！
Regulus: Hold on, hang about!

星锑：慎重啊组长，你可是我们这儿唯一懂电子设备的人了！

星锑：修好信号接收器可就全指望你了——！
Regulus: We're counting on you to fix the signal!

忧心忡忡的组员用力摇晃组长的脑袋。
She grabs Ulrich by the tank and frantically shakes it, sending the ferrofluid swirling inside.

乌尔里希：你在诅咒我吗？星锑研究员。
Ulrich: Mind the negativity, Regulus. I may be a scientist, but I'd rather not have the bad omens.

乌尔里希：时代病症状的表现并不稳定，可能是三个月，十五天，当然也可能只是几十秒……我的运气一向不错。
Ulrich: It does take time to recover from the Storm Syndrome. Indeed, it could be as long as three months, or a few weeks. But hey, it may well be just a matter of seconds. "Fortune favors the bold," you know.

星锑：那可是几十次实验啊——！
Regulus: But if I've learned anything at Laplace, it's that we'll need to do dozens of tests!

维尔汀：这太冒进了，乌尔里希组长。
Vertin: I agree with Regulus. Your plan is too reckless, Mr. Ulrich.

维尔汀：我们的当务之急是离开这里。
Vertin: Our priority should be to find a way to escape this ship safely.

她望向窗外，舱门口空无一人。
She looks through the cell door window. There's no one outside.

Sonetto: What about Ms. Barcarola? Do you think she'll stand with us?

维尔汀：我相信她。

Helmsman Esam: What brought our brightest little star? Oh, look at you, out of breath and all covered in dust. What happened?

舵手老查理：别着急，大伙儿都在这儿呢～
Helmsman Charlie: Easy, easy, Barcarola. We're here to help!

热情的问候将狼狈的乐手包裹其中，一股温热的液体涌上眼眶。
The warmth of their greetings causes tears to well up in her eyes.

舵手乔瓦尼：发生什么事了吗？芭卡洛儿小姐。尽管按照规矩，咱们只能守在这个小舱室里，但这儿的老伙计都很乐意帮你的忙。
Helmsman Giovanni: That's right, Miss. Why don't you tell us what happened? The captain told us to stay put, but we'll do whatever we can to help you.

芭卡洛儿：我……
Barcarola: I ... We ...

芭卡洛儿：我们的“自由海风号”……再也不会回家了……
Barcarola: The "Free Breeze" will never go home again.

舵手乔瓦尼：什……么？
Helmsman Giovanni: Uh, what?

芭卡洛儿：格蕾丝船长说，这个时代即将毁灭……只有戴上面具的人才能够通过筛选，跟随她踏上新时代的土地。
Barcarola: Captain Grace said this era is coming to an end, and only those who put on a Manus Vindictae mask and pass its trial can reach the new era with her.

舵手老查理：你把老查理越说越糊涂啦！……咱们的终点站难道不是热那亚吗？
Helmsman Charlie: Sorry, what? You just turned your old friend Charlie's brain into a knot. Where are we going then?

芭卡洛儿：不，不是的。我们会去到一个谁也不知道的地方，也许是十年前，或者是一百年前……
Barcarola: There's no telling where or even when we'll end up. Could be someplace ten years ago, or even a hundred years.

舵手伊萨姆：就像时空穿梭？
Helmsman Esam: You mean we're traveling through time?

芭卡洛儿：……我、我不知道。
Barcarola: I-I don't know.

舵手乔瓦尼：芭卡洛儿小姐，您说的这些实在是太离奇了，我乔瓦尼跑过那么多地方，也从没听说过这样的事。
Helmsman Giovanni: I've got to admit, Miss. This all sounds a bit too wild to be believed.

舵手乔瓦尼：可你是从不会欺骗我们的——
Helmsman Giovanni: But as sure as a compass points north—

粗糙的手掌轻轻拍了拍少女仍在发颤的肩头。
He gently pats her on the shoulder with a large, rough hand.

舵手乔瓦尼：我愿意相信你说的这一切。
Helmsman Giovanni: I will trust you mean every word you say.

芭卡洛儿：……谢谢你，乔瓦尼先生。
Barcarola: Thank you, Giovanni.

舵手伊萨姆：按照你的意思，咱们再也没法回去了？鹿特丹、哥本哈根、比雷埃夫斯……哪儿都不行？
Helmsman Esam: So, you're saying if we don't do something, then none of us will ever see home again?

沉默昭示了答案。
Her silence is answer enough.

水手们互相望了望，甚至不需要言语，他们迅速做出了唯一的决定。
The sailors exchange a glance, needing no words to make their decision.

舵手Ⅳ：芭卡洛儿小姐，我们站在你这一头！
Helmsman IV: It's decided then. We'll fight by your side, Ms. Barcarola!

舵手Ⅳ：毕竟咱们这儿的伙计，可没谁乐意去一个谁也没听过的鬼地方！
Helmsman IV: Because none of us wants to find ourselves in a random land back when the dinosaurs roamed!

舵手老查理：没错，我还打算干完这一趟就安安稳稳地退休呢～
Helmsman Charlie: You've got that right! I won't let them ruin my retirement!

舵手乔瓦尼：在海上漂泊再久的水手，也总得有回家的一天——
Helmsman Giovanni: We'll sail ourselves home if we've got to!

舵手乔瓦尼：我可不打算在外头待一辈子。
Helmsman Giovanni: One thing's for certain: I don't want to be stuck here for the rest of my life!

舵手伊萨姆：别说这些客气话了，芭卡洛儿小姐。我们能帮上什么忙吗？
Helmsman Esam: Alright, gentlemen, enough with the words. It's time to take action. Ms. Barcarola, is there anything we can do?

芭卡洛儿：当然！
Barcarola: Yes, of course!

LEE-17 不和谐音 / Dissonance

星锑：天呐，外面什么人都没有了，那些努库泰澳的小子们该不会把我们彻底忘了吧？！
Regulus: Hey, the Nukutai nutjobs outside are gone! Don't tell me they've abandoned ship and left us here to starve!

星锑：快开门，我要求更换行刑方式！我拒绝海葬，我要与你们对抗到底——
Regulus: Come back here, you yellow-bellied cowards! This pirate is not going to Davy Jones's locker without a fight!

愤怒的海盗朝着舷窗外大声疾呼。
Having satisfied her anger by yelling through the porthole, she turns to the others.

星锑：十四行诗，我们的毛毛虫溶剂渗透到哪一步了？
Regulus: Sonetto, are those solvents working at all? Tell me they are!

十四行诗：我确认过了……目前它们已经将舱门的外表皮都腐蚀完毕了。
Sonetto: It appears the outer layer of the door has already dissolved substantially.

乌尔里希：很好，纸莎草毛虫溶剂的效果比我想象中的更加高效。
Ulrich: Excellent. The Papyrpillar Solvents are more effective than I anticipated.

乌尔里希：按照目前的腐蚀程度估算，距离溶解整面舱门大概只需13个自然时！
Ulrich: At this rate, the door should be fully dissolved in approximately 13 hours!

星锑：……真是个了不起的好消息。
Regulus: Oh wow, that fast! Really, Fish Tank? I'll be waiting with bated breath!

焦躁的星锑恼怒地摇晃一旁的玻璃缸。
She furiously shakes his glass tank.

星锑：乌尔里希组长，你为什么不在科算中心普及你的玻璃缸脑袋——！
Regulus: Hey, why don't you just whip us up a few helmets like yours?

星锑：这样我们就能用上你那“轰——”的一下就能搞定一切的爆炸反应堆了！
Regulus: That way, you can just blast the door open with the TNT, and we'll be sound as a pound. Well, our heads at least.

乌尔里希：你误会了，星锑研究员。它的材质只是最普通的二氧化硅，以及7.092%碳酸钙镁与3.27%的氧化铝……并不具备任何防爆破与减震效果。
Ulrich: My helmet is made of regular silica, 7.092% calcium magnesium carbonate, and 3.27% aluminum oxide. I'm afraid it's no more explosion-proof than your regular old skull.

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

海盗颓然靠在舱门上，失去了最后一点儿抗争的力气。
Regulus slumps against the door as the last vestiges of resistance leave her body.

恍惚间，某种似有若无的嘈杂呼喊声传入了监牢。
A faint shout comes from the other side of the door.

维尔汀：星锑，我建议你离那扇舱门远一点儿。
Vertin: Regulus, I'd stay away from the door if I were you.

星锑：哈？
Regulus: Huh?!

芭卡洛儿：……她们在这儿！
Barcarola: They're here!

舵手伊萨姆：抱紧备用锚，伙计们！
Helmsman Esam: Hold onto this anchor like your life depends on it!

舵手老查理：数三、二、一，咱们一起撞开它——！
Helmsman Charlie: We ram the door open on the count of three!

门外的声音有如天籁。
The helmsmen's voices are like music to their ears.

舵手众：三——
Helmsmen: Three!

相似的倒计时。
A countdown begins.

舵手众：二——
Helmsmen: Two!

几乎震撼灵魂的撞击声。
A nearly soul-stirring impact.

舵手众：一！
Helmsmen: One!

牢不可破的舱门在一声声热切的呼喊中轰然倒塌。
With their final count, the supposedly unbreakable door collapses.

熟悉的脸庞又一次出现在眼前。
The cheering of familiar faces echoes through the room.

星锑发誓，这是她有生以来听过的最美妙的一段噪音。
Regulus swears it's the most beautiful noise she's ever heard.

星锑：芭卡洛儿，我就知道你一定会来拯救我的，你一定不希望见到一颗冉冉升起的电台新星在此刻坠落！
Regulus: Right on! I knew you'd come through for us, Barcarola! A rising star through hell or high water!

维尔汀：谢谢你，芭卡洛儿小姐。
Vertin: You have our thanks, Ms. Barcarola.

芭卡洛儿：我……我只是想拯救更多的人。
Barcarola: I just want to save as many people as possible, for the pride of the "Free Breeze"!

身为“自由海风号”的一员，我决不能让她蒙羞！

维尔汀：我们也一样。
Vertin: We aim to do the same thing.

沉默许久的组长也站起身来。
After a pause, Ulrich steps forward.

乌尔里希：司辰，我申请去寻找这艘船的广播室。
Ulrich: Timekeeper, I need to get to the radio room.

乌尔里希：那儿很可能是唯一一处能够收发无线电信号的地方。
Ulrich: It's likely to be the only place on the ship that we'll be able to get through their jamming.

维尔汀与磁流体郑重地对视。
She turns to Ulrich with a solemn look on her face.

乌尔里希：我会带回好消息的，我向你承诺。
Ulrich: I'll bring good news. I promise.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀：我明白了，我会派遣星锑协助你的行动。
Vertin: I see. Regulus, you should go with him.

乌尔里希：不不不，找广播室完全用不上这么多人——
Ulrich: No, no, no, I don't need additional manpower for such an easy—

维尔汀：我们不能牺牲任何人，乌尔里希组长。
Vertin: I insist. We can't afford to lose anyone, Mr. Ulrich.

一台小巧的仪器被放在了黑色皮质手套上。
She places a compact device in his leather-gloved hand.

乌尔里希：这是……
Ulrich: This is ...

维尔汀：“前行者”Ⅰ号卫星定位系统，来自你们科算中心的最新技术。
Vertin: The Pioneers Mk I positioning system, the latest in technology from Laplace.

乌尔里希：可我记得它还没有进入量产阶段，仅有几台原型机可用。
Ulrich: But if I recall correctly, it's never been mass-produced. Only a few prototypes were made available.

维尔汀：如果不慎落入海中，或是陷入某种不可控的危险，至少有人能够通过它来确认你的坐标。
Vertin: And this is one of them. If anything happens, someone can use it to track you down if you're in serious trouble, like if you've fallen into the sea.

乌尔里希：这是份宝贵的援助，司辰。

Vertin: Good luck, Mr. Ulrich.

Regulus: Ha, he won't need it, because no one knows radio systems better than this captain!

维尔汀点了点头，目送拉普拉斯的二人没入黑暗中。

维尔汀：其余人和我一起返回大厅，我们需要率先控制住那些被面具侵蚀的平民。
Vertin: The rest of us need to return to the lobby and get the masked guests under control.

维尔汀：十四行诗，我们还有多少昏睡幻剂？
Vertin: Sonetto, do we have sufficient sedatogens left?

十四行诗：请放心，司辰，我们还有充足的储备！
Sonetto: Yes, Timekeeper. We still have plenty!

维尔汀走上前来，面对着热心肠的水手们。
She turns to the helmsmen.

维尔汀：各位，我还需要你们的协助。
Vertin: Gentlemen, I'll need your assistance, too.

舵手伊萨姆：当然，女士。芭卡洛儿小姐把一切事儿都告诉咱们了，这不仅是为了帮你，也是为了帮助咱们自己！
Helmsman Esam: Of course, ma'am. Ms. Barcarola already told us everything. Sounds like helping you means we're helping ourselves!

Barcarola: Esam, do you know where we can find the spare keys to the passenger cabins?

Barcarola: We have another friend to free.

船体的另一边，两个鬼祟的身影一前一后地在黑暗中摸索着。
Elsewhere on the ship, two stealthy figures navigate through the darkness.

星锑：组长，你确定我们的方向没错吗？
Regulus: Are you sure this is the right way?

乌尔里希：你在怀疑我的专业性吗？
Ulrich: Are you doubting my capabilities?

Regulus: Not exactly.

广播室内空无一人。
The broadcasting room is empty.

星锑：这儿居然连一个重塑的守卫也没有？

乌尔里希：那一点儿也不重要。
Ulrich: We'll concern ourselves with that later.

Ulrich: Let's get to work, Regulus!

罔顾一旁四处转悠的星锑，乌尔里希迅速将自己的“思维电流”导向了广播台。
Ignoring Regulus's wandering about, Ulrich quickly channels his "thought current" into the broadcasting console.

“广播台”：……

"VHF Radio": ...

星锑：——难怪重塑对这儿不管不顾！
Regulus: No wonder there's been no sight nor sound of those oily freaks!

乌尔里希似乎对眼前的一切早有预料，它收回了“思维电流”，对眼前的困境置若罔闻。
Ulrich seems unsurprised. Retracting his "thought current," he disregards the apparent predicament.

一件件古怪的材料被摆到了桌上。

乌尔里希：这难道不是一个完美的“人工暴雨”反应场吗？

乌尔里希：这正是我需要你的原因，星锑研究员。
Ulrich: Which is why it's lucky you were sent along with me, Regulus. If anything happens to me, you'll have to be the one to report the experiments' results!

实验以外的人员协调工作可都压在你身上了！

它拍了拍对方的肩膀。
He gives her a hearty pat on the shoulder.

乌尔里希：无论“暴雨”是否到来，我们的研究都会向前迈出一大步。
Ulrich: Whether the "Storm" comes or not, we'll have made an undeniable leap of progress.

乌尔里希：就算我不幸患上了某种糟糕的时代病。

乌尔里希：这儿至少能多出一把平衡伞来。

雷厉风行的组长没有顾及一动不动的组员。
He pays no mind to his immobile teammate.

它正严谨地为手头上的材料排序。

星锑：乌尔里希。

星锑：我拒绝你的提议！
Regulus: I refuse to be a part of this!

LEE-18 二十七岁俱乐部 / The 27 Club

拥挤的监控室里，一人一玻璃缸面面相觑。
In the cramped broadcasting room, the little lion and the lightbulb are at a face-off.

乌尔里希：你说什么？
Ulrich: What did you say?

未曾预料过的宣言令玻璃缸里的磁流体也停止了旋转。
Her unexpected declaration has caused the ferrofluid to come to a halt.

星锑：我说，我拒绝承担“人工暴雨”实验的善后工作。
Regulus: You heard me, you daft lightbulb! I will not be your undertaker!

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：星锑研究员，你只是还没有意识到这项实验的意义！
Ulrich: Regulus, you still haven't grasped the significance of this project, have you?!

乌尔里希：我们搞清楚了“暴雨”的基础结构，甚至还模拟出“人工暴雨”，尽管还有不少完善空间，但这可是实打实地把理论研究推进到了应用层面！
Ulrich: We've figured out the principles of the "Storm" and even developed the means to create its simulacra! Yes, there's still much room for improvement, but we've already made a huge leap!

乌尔里希：而现在，我们终于能够把它运用在“暴雨”本身的研究上。
Ulrich: And now, we finally have the opportunity to put our theories into application!

乌尔里希：稳定性材料绝不是一场空谈，“星锑”天文望远镜的实证就赤裸裸地摆在每一个人的面前！
Ulrich: Finding an immutable material is essential to our survival! The "Regulus Satellite" proved it to all of us!

乌尔里希：好好想一想，星锑。
Ulrich: Just think about it, Regulus.

乌尔里希：我们已经站在后“暴雨”时代的分界线上了！
Ulrich: We are standing right on the cusp of the post-"Storm" era!

顽固分子低垂着脑袋，似乎对组长的训示置若罔闻。
Regulus hangs her head.

星锑：乌尔里希组长……
Regulus: Fish Tank.

星锑：你从一开始就打算独自实验吗？
Regulus: You planned this all along, didn't you?

乌尔里希：……
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：难道你在担心实验经费的事吗？
Ulrich: Don't tell me you're worried about the funds and credit for the experiment?

乌尔里希：别担心，你同样在项目人员名单中，在实验中造成的一切材料或是个人财产的损耗，拉普拉斯都会为你全额报销！
Ulrich: Laplace will cover all your potential losses and expenses incurred should anything go wrong.

乌尔里希：不论成功与否，对“人工暴雨”实验的协助都能够让你得到一个更高的评级，它当然也会让你得到一笔梦寐以求的报酬。
Ulrich: And whether this project succeeds or not, your assistance has been indispensable. Surely enough to earn you a fat bonus and a high rating for your salary review, and I will certainly not be hogging all the credit.

乌尔里希还想再说些什么，却突然对上一副更加认真的脸。
Ulrich stops upon seeing an even more resolute expression come across Regulus's face.

星锑：打住，打住！
Regulus: Whoa, no, keep it in the tank!

星锑：乌尔里希组长，你是不是搞错了什么？
Regulus: You've got me all wrong, Magnet Head.

乌尔里希：啊……？
Ulrich: Huh?

两个茫然的脑袋怔怔对望。
The two exchanged stunned looks.

星锑：我和你一样，同样是科算中心的一员，同样隶属于“暴雨”专项研究小组。
Regulus: I'm a member of Laplace now, same as you. A researcher, not just an observer.

星锑：同样是“暴雨”的亲历者。
Regulus: I, too, witnessed the "Storm."

乌尔里希从未见过如此郑重的星锑。
Ulrich has never seen Regulus so earnest.

星锑：我也应该真正地参与“人工暴雨”的实验，不是为你处理后事——
Regulus: So, ergo, therefore, Q.E.D., I'll participate in your "Artificial Storm" experiment, not as your note taker.

星锑：而是作为一位实验者。
Regulus: But as your fellow experimenter!

乌尔里希：……你总能给我惊喜，星锑研究员。
Ulrich: I never expected this from you, Regulus.

磁流体无奈地拍了拍脑袋。
He knocks on his glass tank, perplexed.

星锑：我的形象有这么糟糕吗？
Regulus: Don't tell me my reports were really that bad.

星锑：既然我提前预支了工资，我就一定会履行研究员的职责！
Regulus: Never mind, really, don't tell me. Fact of the matter is, I got an advance on my wages, so I fully intend to do my duty as a researcher!

星锑：更何况——
Regulus: Besides ...

星锑：热心肠的摇滚海盗绝对不会将任何一个同伴独自扔在危险之中。
Regulus: No rockin' pirate with a spine would ever leave their shipmates stranded in danger.

结实的手按在星锑的肩上。
Ulrich squeezes Regulus's shoulder.

乌尔里希：我敬佩你的勇气。
Ulrich: I admire your courage, truly.

乌尔里希：但在“人工暴雨”的实验上，你应该相信你的组长能搞定这一切！
Ulrich: However, when it comes to these experiments, you must leave it to me!

星锑：……
Regulus: ...

乌尔里希：这是命令，星锑。
Ulrich: That is an order, Regulus.

玻璃缸的意志显然比顽石更加坚决。
His resolve is unyielding.

它推开门，示意星锑离开这间临时实验室。
He opens the door, signaling Regulus to leave his "lab."

乌尔里希：你负责通过舷窗观测我的实验状态，并记录相关实验数据。
Ulrich: I need you to observe my status through the porthole and record our experimental data. You're the only one that can do it.

星锑：好吧。
Regulus: Alright, Magnet Head, have it your way.

临别的目光扫过实验箱里的一份份材料。
Her eyes linger on the experimental materials in the case.

铂金通灵板、幼龙舌管、火蛾脂粉、许多张一模一样的复制唱片……
Platinum Ouija boards, young dragon tongue tubes, fire moth powder, and numerous duplicated records ...

星锑：乌尔里希组长，你听摇滚吗？
Regulus: Say Ulrich, do you like rock?

乌尔里希：你在说什么乱七八糟的？现在可不是分享音乐的时候！
Ulrich: Now is hardly the time to chat about music, don't you think?

乌尔里希：我希望这是你最后一个莫名其妙的问题了——
Ulrich: I hope you won't be pestering me with more of these inane questions.

乌尔里希：比起摇滚乐，棕色噪音更能让我的磁流体得到充分的舒展与锻炼。
Ulrich: And to answer you, I prefer Brown noise. Its frequencies produce a soothing rhythm in my ferrofluid.

星锑：这正是我不能把它交给你的原因。
Regulus: See? That's exactly why I can't leave it to you.

乌尔里希：什……么？
Ulrich: Errr. What?

逻辑跳跃的话语差点儿令组长宕机。
This logical leap nearly causes Ulrich's circuits to crash.

星锑：如果我对眼前的翻印行为置之不理……
Regulus: I turned a blind eye to your blatant acts of piracy ...

星锑：如果我容许了盗版唱片对于音乐的亵渎……
Regulus: And brushed off your blasphemies against rock.

星锑：倘若我放弃了眼下如此具有摇滚精神的冒险……
Regulus: But, if I miss out on an adventure like this,

星锑：——我将永远失去加入27岁俱乐部的机会！
Regulus: I'll forever lose the right to join the 27 Club!

乌尔里希：摇滚……俱乐部……？
Ulrich: The 27 Club?

星锑：最适合摇滚巨星离世的年龄便是27岁，其次就是现在！
Regulus: All the best rock stars die at 27, or in a blaze of glory!

星锑：这是我的唱片，我必须为它负责。
Regulus: This is my record, my responsibility.

星锑：也许我们会倒下。
Regulus: We might fall or even vanish.

星锑：会变成谁也认不出的古怪模样。
Regulus: Maybe we'll get turned into cubes or paint or whatever!

星锑：但……
Regulus: But at the end of the day ...

星锑：摇滚永远不死！
Regulus: Rock never dies!

乌尔里希：……

乌尔里希：…………
Ulrich: ...

乌尔里希：！
Ulrich: !

乌尔里希：这正是人类所独有的辉光。
Ulrich: Whether you're a rock legend or not, you shine with the radiance of humanity.

乌尔里希：向你的实验精神与摇滚精神致敬！
Ulrich: Regulus, I salute both your experimental spirit and your rock 'n' roll spirit!

乌尔里希：我宣布——
Ulrich: There's only one thing left to do.

乌尔里希：实验项目：“人工暴雨”下的稳定性材料试验
Ulrich: Project: Experiments on Material Immutability via "Artificial Storm"

乌尔里希：实验场地：“自由海风号”广播室临时实验室
Ulrich: Locale: Radio Room of the "Free Breeze" Cruise Ship

乌尔里希：实验人员：乌尔里希，星锑
Ulrich: Experimenters: Ulrich and Regulus

乌尔里希：实验开始。
Ulrich: Our experiment will now commence.

LEE-19 我们称作乡愁之物 / The Pain of Missing Home

舵手伊萨姆：嘿，维尔汀小姐，客人们似乎都集中在这儿——！
Helmsman Esam: Ms. Vertin, it seems all the passengers are gathered in the lobby.

越狱后的一行人终于抵达了一片狼藉的游轮大厅。
The group has finally arrived at the cruise ship lobby. The place is a mess.

十四行诗：司辰，越来越多人被重塑的面具影响了……！
Sonetto: We've lost too much time. A lot of people have put on masks while we were locked up.

维尔汀：先将那些尚有意识的客人们保护起来！
Vertin: We'll need to round up the ones that are still conscious!

舵手老查理：没问题！
Helmsman Charlie: Sure!

临时召集的救援队迅速行动起来，他们翻越此起彼伏的谩骂与争吵，努力分开争抢面具的人群。
The hastily assembled rescue team leaps into action, breaking up rising quarrels and separating the crowd members fighting over masks.

客人Ⅰ：**的[那不勒斯脏话]！——又来了几个抢名额的人！！
Guest I: Damn, more contenders! Like we don't have enough people wrestling for a mask!

客人Ⅱ：混账，把你脑袋上的面具给我——！
Guest II: Give me that mask, asshole!

客人Ⅱ：我要加入重塑之手！我要参加试炼！
Guest II: I'm joining Manus Vindictae! I will take the trial!

客人们相互推搡，行船礼仪被远远抛在了脑后。
Clearly, any semblance of onboard etiquette has been long abandoned.

船员Ⅰ：不行，琼斯先生，您的身体缺乏锻炼，别浪费宝贵的试炼机会！
Crew Member I: Sir, I believe you may be too weak to endure the trial! You should leave this valuable opportunity to someone who will be more useful to Captain Grace!

——这个面具应该留给更有可能博得格蕾丝船长信任的人！

十四行诗：请放下面具，它们不能解决任何问题！
Sonetto: Please put the masks down, everyone! This isn't the way to survive!

客人Ⅲ：小姑娘，放开它，那是我的——！
Guest III: Give it to me! That mask belongs to me!

客人Ⅲ：格蕾丝女士曾对我微笑！她一定是希望我与她一起登上救生艇！
Guest III: Ms. Grace smiled at me once! She must like me! She'll want me to join her!

船员Ⅱ：我……我不想被“暴雨”回溯……
Crew Member II: I just don't want to be killed by this "Storm" thing.

船员Ⅱ：呜呜……我也想要活下去……
Crew Member II: *sob* I don't want to die.

舵手们一拥而上，将昏睡幻剂灌入几乎癫狂的乘客口中。
The helmsmen dip and dive through the crowd as they administer sedatogens to the almost delirious passengers.

舵手伊萨姆：伙计们，快醒醒！
Helmsman Esam: Get back to your senses, people!

舵手伊萨姆：我要是你们，早就把这些怪面具扔到海里去了——！
Helmsman Esam: If I were you, I'd have thrown these creepy masks into the sea the moment I saw them!

同样狼狈的努库泰澳余众也发现了不远处的救援行动。
The Nukutai survivors watch the nearby rescue operation from afar.

多亏了格蕾丝的善心，他们的处境似乎远比其他人“光明”得多。
Thanks to Grace's kindness, their situation appears far "brighter" than the other guests.

但并非人人都如此笃信。
But not all of them share their newfound faith.

托阿：求你了……塞洛尼，戴上重塑面具吧……这只是个简单的仪式……
Toa: Selone, you must put on the mask, please. For our people. It's not scary, I promise.

托阿：难道你情愿被那些外族人抓住吗？！
Toa: Would you rather be captured by those outsiders?!

塞洛尼：快离开这儿吧，托阿。
Selone: Go to the captain's room, Toa.

塞洛尼：你通过了重塑的筛选，快到船长室去吧，那儿的努库泰澳朋友更需要你。
Selone: You passed your trial. I'm sure the captain and our people there need you more than I do.

塞洛尼：我必须留在这儿……我得照顾基蒂欧纳、小皮塔，还有那些状态糟糕的朋友们……
Selone: I must stay here to look after Kitiona, little Pita, and our friends who still seem to be lost.

托阿：塞洛尼——你为什么不愿尝试戴上面具呢？！
Toa: What is wrong with you, Selone? All you need to do is put on the mask!

塞洛尼甩开对方的手，几乎跌坐在地。
Selone breaks free of Toa's grip, nearly falling to the floor as she does so.

塞洛尼：抱歉，托阿。我想……图图石子的犹豫是对的。
Selone: I'm sorry, Toa. I think Fatutu was right to have second thoughts.

塞洛尼：有多少人和你一起戴上了面具，可他们又有多少人活了下来呢？
Selone: Look at all the people who have put on the mask. Now, tell me how many of them have survived?

顺着塞洛尼的泪光望去，无数的试炼失败者躺倒在地。
Following Selone's tear-filled gaze, countless failures of the trial lie sprawled on the floor.

努库泰澳人，澳大利亚人，意大利人……
Nukutai, Australians, Italians ...

水手，商人，游客……
Sailors, merchants, tourists ...

托阿：我还是不明白，还有什么事比回到故乡更重要呢——？！
Toa: And what, you're afraid? Is this really more important than bringing our people home?!

窗外的暴雨仍在急迫地拍打舷窗。
The storm outside continues to batter the ship.

大厅内却变得更安静了。
The lobby, however, grows increasingly silent.

塞洛尼：重塑的面具的确令你变愚钝了，托阿。若是以前的你，又怎么会提出这样浅显的疑问呢？
Selone: You have changed. The Toa I knew would never have dared to ask me such a foolish question.

塞洛尼：你听见他们的哀嚎声了么？
Selone: Haven't you heard their cries?

托阿：想想未来，塞洛尼，想想那个美好的世界！我们能拥有一座新的岛，能重新过上安稳的日子，我们能——
Toa: You need to think of the future, Selone, the new, beautiful homeland we're going to recover! We could live peacefully once more. We could—

托阿激动地挥手，晶莹的泪珠与粘稠的黑液一同淌在地上。
His tears mix with the viscous black liquid of the mask as they drip onto the floor.

塞洛尼：对不起，托阿……对不起。
Selone: Please stop, Toa. I'm sorry.

托阿：……
Toa: ...

塞洛尼：我只是不希望自己的“象形贝壳”也变得那样的粗糙，那样的……扭曲与狰狞。
Selone: When I see how tainted and twisted your Spirit Shell has become, I can't. I won't.

塞洛尼终究还是失去了站立的力量，她的声音几乎微弱得听不见了。
Selone crumples to the floor, her voice barely a whisper.

救援队的行动终于推进到了这儿。
Sonetto spots them among the crowd.

十四行诗：……是塞洛尼小姐！
Sonetto: I recognize her. That's Ms. Selone!

十四行诗：司辰，那边也有人需要救援！
Sonetto: Timekeeper, I think they need assistance!

灰白色的身影急匆匆地奔向努库泰澳人的方向。
She rushes toward the Nukutai survivors.

维尔汀：小心，十四行诗！
Vertin: Sonetto, watch out!

努库泰澳信徒Ⅰ：ㄎ——！……ㄒ……世界……！
Nukutai Believer I: *roar* To ... a new world!

堪堪躲开攻击的十四行诗惊讶地抬起头来。
Narrowly dodging the attack, Sonetto looks up in surprise.

努库泰澳信徒Ⅱ：……ㄗ……ㄙ……
Nukutai Believer II: ... *roar* ... *roar*

冰冷的古铜面具下，粘稠的墨色液体从努库泰澳人的瞳孔与口中缓缓淌下。
Beneath their cold bronze masks, viscous black fluid seeps from the Nukutai believers' eyes and mouths.

他们的肢体扭成古怪的姿势，低声喃喃自语，似乎遭受着无尽的痛苦。
Their limbs have twisted into grotesque shapes, and they mutter to themselves, as though tormented by an unending pain.

维尔汀：十四行诗，准备更多的昏睡幻剂。
Vertin: Sonetto, get ready to use those sedatogens.

狂热的潮水消退了些，痛苦的人们终于进入了梦乡。
Their frenzy subsides as the suffering individuals drift into slumber.

迷失的信徒：ㄙ——！！我……
Delirious Believer: *roar* I ...

十四行诗：抱歉，先生们。
Sonetto: Pardon me for this, please.

科算中心的最新喷剂源源不断地洒向周围。
She sprays a dose of sedatogen over them.

迷失的信徒：家……回ㄐ——！！
Delirious Believer: Home ... home ...

十四行诗：——！
Sonetto: ...!

但遗憾的是，昏睡幻剂对那些被面具影响甚深的迷茫信徒显然收效甚微。
Unfortunately, the sedatogen seems to have little effect on those under the control of the masks.

托阿：你在做什么！
Toa: What're you doing to my people?!

托阿：不许伤害我们的同胞！
Toa: I won't let you hurt them!

托阿警惕地看着眼前的灰白色身影，将那些无意识向前抓挠的重塑信众护在身后。
Toa stands vigilantly before Sonetto, shielding the unconscious Manus believers.

芭卡洛儿：维尔汀小姐、十四行诗小姐，我们回来了！
Barcarola: Ms. Vertin, Ms. Sonetto, we're back!

托阿：……？
Toa: ...?

一个熟悉的轮廓迅速扑了上来。
Fatutu comes rushing over.

图图石子：塞洛尼……托阿……你们没事吧？
Fatutu: Selone, Toa, are you alright?

托阿：图图石子……
Toa: Tutu?

意料之外的相逢似乎并不令人高兴。
Their encounter brings little joy.

托阿摸了摸脸颊上的面具，不自觉地向后退缩了几步。
Toa, instinctively touching the mask clasped to his face, takes a few steps back.

塞洛尼：真高兴你没什么大碍，图图石子。可我们的朋友们……
Selone: I'm so glad to see you unharmed, Fatutu. But our friends ...

图图石子：我都知道的，塞洛尼。芭卡洛儿小姐救下了我，她把一切都告诉了我。
Fatutu: I know what happened, Selone. Barcarola told me everything when she got me out.

图图石子：我想我明白了……我们不应该戴上重塑的面具，更不应该答应他们的复仇计划……
Fatutu: I've made up my mind now. We can't wear their masks, Selone. We never should have agreed to their so-called revenge plan.

迷茫中的信徒似乎捕捉到了关键的字眼，他们像是又被注射了一剂强心针。
The Manus believers seem to latch onto her words, reacting as though they are a shot of adrenaline.

迷失的信徒：复仇……杀ㄙ ——！！
Delirious Believer: Revenge ...! *roar*

图图石子：——！
Fatutu: ...!

狰狞的爪痕撕裂了另一副更结实的臂膀，儿时的同伴又一次挡在了图图石子的身前。
Toa leaps forward, the ragged claws tearing through his arm as he shields his childhood friend once again.

托阿：……
Toa: ...

塞洛尼：托阿——！
Selone: Toa!

芭卡洛儿：图图石子……大家……
Barcarola: No! No! Why is this happening?

鲜血在眼前溅起，洁白的大厅映出一片鲜红。
Blood splatters before her eyes, painting the lobby wall crimson.

迷失之人的复仇欲望却因此愈发高涨。
The believer's appetite for vengeance has only grown stronger.

迷失的信徒：重塑……ㄙ ！
Delirious Believer: Retribution ...! *roar*

十四行诗：糟糕，他们看上去更加疯狂了。司辰，我申请加大昏睡幻剂的剂量！
Sonetto: They seem to be more frantic than ever before! Timekeeper, I suggest increasing the dosage of sedatogens!

维尔汀：不，重塑面具已经扎根在了大脑的深层，单纯的外部刺激无法唤醒他们的意识。
Vertin: The mask's influence has wormed its way deep into their brains. I'm afraid sedatogens won't be able to awaken their consciousness any longer.

维尔汀：他们需要更直白的呼唤。
Vertin: They need something that reaches into their soul.

重塑信徒们涌上前来，誓要撕碎眼前的一切。
The Manus believers are determined to destroy everything in their path.

芭卡洛儿：……！
Barcarola: ...!

人群被推搡着后退，可怜的乐手同样深陷其中。
As they surge forward, the crowd is pushed back. Barcarola is caught in the center of the chaos.

芭卡洛儿：我……我能做些什么呢？
Barcarola: Isn't there something I can do?

哀嚎声、哭声、窗外的雨声几乎挤破了她的耳膜，连琴弓都跌落在地。
The wails, the cries, and the pounding rain outside nearly overwhelm her. Amidst the chaos, her bow slips out of her hand.

“啪——”
*thwack*

清脆的声响令她有些恍惚。
She jumps at the sound.

？？？：别摆弄你的小匣子了，芭卡洛儿——回到课上来！
???: Stop playing with that atrocious toy of yours and pay attention to the class, Barcarola!

？？？：音乐是无关种族与身份的另一门语言。
???: Music is a language that moves us on to a deeper level than any other, transcending both culture, place, and time.

？？？：它四海皆准，它直抵心灵。
???: Whoever you are, and wherever you go, it will always stir the depths of your soul!

芭卡洛儿：……
Barcarola: ...

无须回想，无须思索。
No need to remember. No need to think.

熟悉而简洁的音色从繁复的匣子里流淌而出。
Familiar, simple tones flow from her Crackling Box.

某种难以言喻的、轻柔的声音拂过了图图石子。
A soft, indescribable melody washes over Fatutu.

耳畔的歌儿如此陌生，如此亲切，它究竟来自哪儿呢？
This song is both strange yet intimate. Where is it from?

是乐手口中的克雷莫纳，无意闯入的舵手合唱团，还是岛上经年累月的篝火大会？
Is it from the Cremona that Barcarola talked about? The helmsmen's spontaneous sing-song? Or from Meli's traditional bonfire festival?

图图石子：它们没有什么不同……对吧？
Fatutu: We're not so different deep down, are we?

惊讶的客人：嗯……？
Surprised Guest: Huh? What's that sound? Violins, piano, cellos, double bass, and flutes!

是小提琴的声音，还有钢琴、低音提琴……长笛？

疑惑的客人：可……她不是一直都说自己不喜欢这些太过寻常的乐器吗？
Confused Guest: But violins? She hates violins!

恍惚的客人：我、我想回家……呜呜……
Dismayed Guest: I-I want to go home! *sob*

迷失的信徒：ㄛ……ㄒ……
Delirious Believer: *roar* ... *roar*

迷失的信徒：ㄥㄡ……努库泰澳……
Delirious Believer: *roar* Nukutaeao ...

曾经的伙伴们高举双手，无助地抓挠着。
Her people raise their hands helplessly, clawing at the air.

泪水淌湿了视野，思绪却越发清晰。
Tears blur her vision, but her thoughts only grow clearer.

不住打颤的手郑重地捧起了那枚口琴。
Though her hands are trembling, she gently lifts the harmonica to her lips.

踩着温和的节拍，微微发颤的唇齿轻轻吹响了口琴。
Her quivering lips blow a gentle rhythm into the harmonica.

新的音色加入其中。
A new melody joins the ensemble.

乐手与来自岛上的女孩对望了一眼，没有指挥棒，也无需语言，音乐朝着古老而欢快的河道奔流。
The islander and the musician exchange a glance, and, with no baton nor words, music flows between them like an ancient, joyful river.

斑驳的粘稠液体近乎凝固，它不再从那些呢喃着的无助面具下涌出。
The black liquid stills, no longer seeping from the masks of the helpless.

不知名的歌谣流淌着，轻柔地合上迷失信徒们的双眼。
The melody echoes through the lobby, gently closing the eyes of the tormented believers.

托阿：……
Toa: ...

那双高高举起的手终于放了下来，像是步入了一个沉沉的梦。
Toa's raised hands finally fall, as though succumbing to a deep sleep.

图图石子：……朋友们，一切都结束了。
Fatutu: It's over now, dear friends.

结束表演的游轮乐手局促地捏紧自己的衣角。
Barcarola nervously wrings her hands.

芭卡洛儿：对不起，我没想到这首歌会让努库泰澳人陷入这样的境地……我只是想……
Barcarola: I'm sorry, Fatutu. I didn't expect my song to put your people in this state. I only wanted to help.

图图石子：谢谢你，芭卡洛儿小姐，你是我见过最伟大的演奏家。
Fatutu: You did. You're the greatest musician I've ever seen.

芭卡洛儿：他们……去世了么？
Barcarola: But, your friends, they've—

图图石子：不，他们只是回家了。
Fatutu: They've gone home.

芭卡洛儿：可……
Barcarola: But ...

眼前轻微发抖的肩膀令芭卡洛儿有些陌生。
The lightly trembling shoulders before her suddenly feel unfamiliar.

像那样柔弱、稚嫩的肩膀，从一开始，就是这般勇敢而坚决吗？
Had those fragile, tender shoulders always been so brave and resolute?

图图石子：你瞧，他们身上的象形贝壳是多么光洁、多么圆润——
Fatutu: Look at the shining, pristine Spirit Shells around their necks. That is a sign. It tells us that their souls are at peace.

这是一种美好的象征，芭卡洛儿小姐。它自豪地向我们宣告……

图图石子：我们的朋友已经度过了充实而坦然的，圆满的一生。
Fatutu: That our friends lived a full and honest life.

擦干眼泪，图图石子轻轻拾起那些漂亮的“象形贝壳”。贝壳上仍保留着温润的触感，在她的手中微微发烫。
Wiping her tears, Fatutu gets to her feet and starts to gently collect her lost people's Spirit Shells. She can still feel their warmth in her palm.

卡穆塔：图图石子——！
Kamuta: Fatutu!

贝壳的余温尚未消退，一个冷酷的身影大踏步奔进了这里。
Before the warmth of the Spirit Shells can fade, Kamuta strides into the lobby, his demeanor cold.

LEE-20 向别处 / To Elsewhere, To Home

卡穆塔：……你知道自己在做些什么吗？
Kamuta: What are you doing?!

卡穆塔：你竟然投靠了我们的仇人，你还记得自己重建家园的使命吗？！
Kamuta: How could you side with our enemies? Against your own people, against the ones who would rebuild our home?!

不可置信的严厉语气在她的耳畔炸响。
Incredulous severity colors his tone.

卡穆塔：我对你很失望，图图石子。
Kamuta: You've brought shame on our people. You've disappointed me.

卡穆塔：跟我走，我们现在就去请求格蕾丝女士为你洗礼——你不能再胡闹了！
Kamuta: Stop all this now, and come with me. We will beg Ms. Grace to cleanse your soul!

如往常无数次伸出的手一般，他等待着一次熟悉的回握。
Like the countless times before, he waits for her to grasp his outstretched hand.

“啪——”
*thwack*

卡穆塔：……？！
Kamuta: ?!

一次出乎意料的反叛。
An unexpected act of defiance.

图图石子：加入重塑之手是一个完全错误的决定，卡穆塔。
Fatutu: Joining Manus Vindictae was a mistake, Kamuta.

图图石子：重塑的面具已经把我们害得够惨了，无数的努库泰澳同胞们因此被仇恨蒙蔽，因此牺牲，因此永远地离开了我们……
Fatutu: Their masks blinded our people, they tricked us with their lies and empty promises, but look! So many precious lives lost for nothing.

卡穆塔：这是为了重建努库泰澳，图图石子！
Kamuta: It wasn't for nothing. They died for the resurrection of Nukutaeao!

卡穆塔：难道你不希望在一片没有人类、没有纷争与污染的土壤上，重新建起我们的新家园吗？
Kamuta: Isn't it your dream, too? To rebuild our home in a land free of humans and their wickedness?!

图图石子轻轻地摇了摇头。
Fatutu shakes her head.

图图石子：不，不是这样的，卡穆塔。
Fatutu: No. Not anymore, Kamuta.

她环顾周围的努库泰澳人，迷茫与痛苦写满了每一张脸。
She looks around at her people, their faces marked with pain and confusion.

图图石子：为了抵达那样美好的新世界，我们已经失去了太多宝贵的东西。
Fatutu: We may have lost our islands, but what we've done here lost us something far more precious.

卡穆塔：……
Kamuta: ...

图图石子：让我们为之骄傲的，从来都不是那些外人羡慕的新奇珍宝，也不是格蕾丝女士口中美好的新时代……
Fatutu: There's nothing in this so-called "new era" that Ms. Grace promised us that is worth becoming monsters and corrupting our Spirit Shells.

图图石子：是来自努库泰澳的每一个人！
Fatutu: Our pride must be in ourselves and who we are.

图图石子：所有的人都能通过我们的贝壳、我们的口音、我们说的每一句话、做的每一件事认出我们……
Fatutu: The shells around our necks, the words we speak to one another, the way we treat others with kindness, not hatred. That is what defines us.

图图石子：他们会说，我见过努库泰澳人，是的，他们胸口的贝壳整齐又漂亮，他们擅长给每一位客人的脑袋编上花环。他们热情，善良，脸上永远都挂着笑容……
Fatutu: We are more than just how the outsiders can use us, more than our Sea Mother's Eye. We are the wisdom of our elders, and the traditions we keep sacred.

图图石子：他们会想起大家编织的“罗盘灼灼”，会记得一位小客人曾在船舱里和他们一起驱赶巨齿飞鳐，会想起来自努库泰澳的歌声……
Fatutu: And if our islands all sink beneath the waves, we will remember them in our craft and in our stories, we will remember the story of the brave Nukutai girl fighting off the Serres, we will remember them in the songs of Nukutaeao!

图图石子：无论我们去到哪儿，在哪个岛上漂流……努库泰澳都在我们脚下。
Fatutu: No matter whether it's an island or a ship we stand on, as long as we're together, Nukutaeao—our home—lies beneath our feet!

卡穆塔：…………
Kamuta: ...

图图石子：你早就说过的，卡穆塔——
Fatutu: Didn't you say you would always have faith in me, Kamuta?

图图石子：你认为我能够肩负起带领族人的使命……你相信我……
Fatutu: You believed I could lead our people to a better future.

图图石子：现在，我也相信我自己。
Fatutu: Now, I believe in myself, too.

她抬起头来，胸前的贝壳随着剧烈的呼吸起伏着。
She raises her head, the shells on her chest heaving with every breath.

它们一同震颤着，像是无数努库泰澳人发自灵魂的共鸣。
They tremble in unison, resonating with the collective energy of the Nukutai.

卡穆塔：呵呵……
Kamuta: Heh heh.

卡穆塔：你做的很好，图图石子。
Kamuta: You'll be a better leader than I ever was, Fatutu.

预想中的责备并未到来，错愕的目光紧紧盯住了自己的哥哥。
The expected reprimand never comes. She stares in shock at her brother,

嘴角仍未消退的欣慰笑容，颤抖着伸出、试图抚摸对方额头的手，以及……
at his lips curled into a faint smile, at his trembling hand still extended out to her, and ...

从眼眶与耳廓中，不断渗出的黑色血迹。
at the black blood seeping from his eyes and ears.

图图石子：卡穆塔，你怎么了……？
Fatutu: What's happening to you?!

“哐——”
*crash*

眼前的高大身影直直地倒了下去。
The towering figure before her falls to the ground.

卡穆塔：我很好……图图石子……
Kamuta: I'm fine, Tutu. I'll be alright.

卡穆塔：我很高兴你能说出那样的话……你是对的……妹妹……
Kamuta: You're right, dear sister. The words you spoke have opened my eyes.

断断续续的话语从发黑的嘴唇中艰难地挤出来。
Pained words are forced through his blackened lips.

图图石子：哥哥——？！
Fatutu: Brother!

少女的惊呼声将人群都吸引了过来。
As she cries out, heads turn toward her.

那副扎眼的面具仍然紧紧攀附在他的脸上，漆黑的液体几乎覆盖了整副面庞。
The mask remains tightly affixed to Kamuta's face, its black liquid nearly covering it entirely.

维尔汀：糟了，是重塑面具的反噬！
Vertin: It's the mask's punishment!

图图石子：我……我不明白……
Fatutu: I-I don't understand!

维尔汀：重塑之手通过面具筛选出忠诚的门徒，通过考验者能够不受神智束缚，保留自我意识与部分记忆。
Vertin: Manus Vindictae use their masks to sift out their most loyal followers. Those who pass the trial can retain their personality and memories.

维尔汀：但……
Vertin: However ...

维尔汀：意志动摇的背叛者将遭到重塑面具的反噬，被无边无际的神秘学汪洋所捕获……
Vertin: If they should show any signs of faltering in their faith, the mask will punish them. Their consciousness will be devoured by the fathomless depths of arcanum.

维尔汀：永远地沦为一具在痛苦中沉沦的……行尸走肉。
Vertin: Until they become nothing but a walking corpse, caught in eternal agony.

刺耳的掌声突兀响起。
A slow clap breaks the silence.

淑女格蕾丝：呵呵，维尔汀小姐对我们的了解实在令人讶异。
Ms. Grace: Well, well, I am stunned by the breadth of your knowledge of our operations, Ms. Vertin.

淑女格蕾丝：但我必须提醒您，随意暴露他人的秘密可算不上什么淑女的品格，维尔汀小姐。
Ms. Grace: But I must remind you: gossip like that is terribly bad manners.

淑女格蕾丝：托您的福，女士……那些可怜的客人们牙关都开始打颤了。
Ms. Grace: Is it any wonder why our guests look so terrified?

淑女格蕾丝：难道他们比起死亡，更害怕我们吗？
Ms. Grace: Though it does pique my curiosity. I wonder, even with all you said, do they fear us more than they fear death?

居高临下的目光在船舱的客人们之间好奇地打着转，最后落在了曾经的同僚身上。
Her commanding gaze hovers over the ship's passengers before finally landing on her former follower.

淑女格蕾丝：真遗憾，卡穆塔先生……
Ms. Grace: What a pity, Mr. Kamuta.

淑女格蕾丝：我本来以为我们能成为更长久的朋友呢～
Ms. Grace: I had high hopes for you. It seems our friendship has come to an untimely end.

毫无波澜的话语轻飘飘地落在每一个人的耳中，人群在惶恐中缓缓向后退去。
Her words are cold and emotionless, instilling a new fear in the crowd.

维尔汀：现在所有人都知道了面具的真相，你们再也无法欺骗任何人了。
Vertin: The people here know the truth about your masks. There's no sense trying to deceive them any longer!

淑女格蕾丝：……是吗？
Ms. Grace: Oh, is that so?

优雅的步伐缓缓逼近。
Grace slowly advances, her steps poised.

十四行诗：司辰，请站在我身后！
Sonetto: Timekeeper, stay behind me!

一抹扎眼的灰白色挡在了格蕾丝的视线前。
Sonetto imposes herself between the two, poised to fight.

淑女格蕾丝：噢，我瞧见了什么——！
Ms. Grace: Oh, what do we have here?

淑女格蕾丝：这儿有一只多么可爱、多么天真的忠诚小狗儿啊～
Ms. Grace: How adorable, the ever-loyal deputy leaps into action! *chuckle*

淑女格蕾丝：好狗狗，我保证，要不是时间紧迫，我肯定愿意多陪你玩一会儿扔项圈小游戏……
Ms. Grace: But we're on a tight schedule, and I don't have time to play games.

淑女格蕾丝：嗯，没错……就是你胸口那枚～
Ms. Grace: There's no power in your shiny little badge here.

她的目光掠过那枚明亮而刺眼的勋章。
She glances at the Foundation emblem on her chest.

淑女格蕾丝：重塑之手将永远铭记你的贡献，卡穆塔先生。
Ms. Grace: Mr. Kamuta, Manus Vindictae will forever remember your contribution.

淑女格蕾丝：……永别了。
Ms. Grace: Farewell.

维尔汀：图图石子——小心！
Vertin: Fatutu, watch out!

淑女格蕾丝：*Slæstu í djúpan dvala.
Ms. Grace: *Slæstu í djúpan dvala.

图图石子：不！——哥哥！
Fatutu: Brother! No!

四周传来的术法波动轻飘飘地溶解在无名者的周围。
The arcane fluctuations gently dissipate around Grace.

芭卡洛儿：格蕾丝船长……
Barcarola: Captain Grace!

淑女格蕾丝：你在难过么？芭卡洛儿小姐。
Ms. Grace: What is it now, Ms. Barcarola?

淑女格蕾丝：但我必须遗憾地通知你，你被解雇了。
Ms. Grace: I'm sure you've already guessed this, but you've been relieved of your duties here.

维尔汀：格蕾丝，重塑的目的，从来都不是拉拢努库泰澳人，对么？！
Vertin: Gaining the support of the Nukutai was never your purpose, am I right?

图图石子：格蕾丝女士，把我的朋友们还给我！
Fatutu: Ms. Grace, give me back my friends!

对女孩的呐喊声置若罔闻，格蕾丝的眉头轻轻皱起。
Grace ignores Fatutu's shouts and slightly furrows her brow.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

淑女格蕾丝：维尔汀，你聪明得令人生厌。
Ms. Grace: Oh, Vertin. I could almost delight in your cleverness, if it wasn't so damnably frustrating.

她打了个响指。
She snaps her fingers.

“哐——”
*clink*

一枚磨损的、造型极不规整的象形贝壳滚落到她的脚边。格蕾丝捧起它来，像是迎着一位终于相逢的好友。
A worn, oddly shaped Spirit Shell rolls to Grace's feet. She picks it up, as if greeting a long-lost friend.

淑女格蕾丝：多遗憾呀，可怜的朋友……
Ms. Grace: A pity.

淑女格蕾丝：你再也回不去了。
Ms. Grace: But there's no turning back now.

四周终于安静了下来，连窗外的风声都清晰可闻。
The room falls silent once more. There is no sound but the howling of the wind outside.

一股嘈杂的电流声突兀地在大厅的广播中响起。
A burst of static echoes from the lobby's speakers.

乌尔里希：喂、喂——！
Ulrich: Hello! Hello?!

乌尔里希：有人能听见吗？
Ulrich: Can't anyone hear me?

乌尔里希：这里是科算中心“暴雨”专项研究小组，我是乌尔里希。
Ulrich: This is Ulrich from Laplace's "Storm" Research Group.

受惊的游客：——！
Startled Guest: Oh, dear!

嘈杂的无线电广播令神经衰弱的客人为之一震。
The radio broadcast jolts the already frazzled guests.

耳鸣的游客：喂——！
Tinnitus-Stricken Guest: Whoa!

耳鸣的客人抬起头来，广播仍在滋滋地播放着什么。
The tinnitus-stricken guest looks up, the broadcast still hissing incomprehensibly.

乌尔里希：……各位……
Ulrich: Everyone!

乌尔里希：我们确认了……材料……
Ulrich: We've found a material that ...

乌尔里希：……问题……
Ulrich: Our "Storm" problem is ...

四周短暂地安静了一瞬。
The room falls briefly silent.

随后，雷鸣般的、绵延不绝的欢呼与掌声覆满了他的耳膜。
Then, it breaks into thunderous cheers and applause.

耳鸣的游客：……什么？
Tinnitus-Stricken Guest: What?

LEE-21 最后一次告别 / Final Farewell

突如其来的惊喜宣言向四周迅速扩散。
The joy of this declaration has reached the hearts of the crowd.

有人将信将疑，有人欢呼。但无一例外的，更多的面具被抛到了一边。
Amid the cheers, more and more masks are cast aside.

淑女格蕾丝：真令人意外，你们总能给我源源不断的惊喜。
Ms. Grace: You never cease to amaze me, do you?

维尔汀：重塑之手，你们的阴谋已经失败了。
Vertin: Manus Vindictae have failed.

淑女格蕾丝：当然，维尔汀小姐。
Ms. Grace: It would appear that way to you, wouldn't it, Ms. Vertin?

淑女格蕾丝：……我该怎么恭喜你呢？
Ms. Grace: How shall I congratulate you?

在似有若无的感慨声中，一位传讯门徒从格蕾丝的身后显现了出来。
A Manus messenger emerges behind Grace.

传讯门徒：ㄍㄟㄙㄉㄣㄖˊㄡㄣㄠㄚㄜㄉㄗㄅˋ
Manus Messenger: Ma'am, we've arrived at the target location.

<格蕾丝大人，我们抵达了对应的坐标。>

传讯门徒：一 ㄩㄞㄠㄗㄌㄢ一ˊㄎㄚㄨㄥㄨㄓˋ
Manus Messenger: We've gathered all the remaining shells and are ready to activate the teleportation ritual at any time.

<其余的材料也已经整理完毕，随时可以发动传送术阵。>

淑女格蕾丝：……相逢的时刻总是如此短暂。
Ms. Grace: Well, well. Time does fly, as they say. Be seeing you and sooner than you think!

格蕾丝最后一次打开了怀表，而后随手将它掷到地上。
Grace opens her pocket watch one last time before casually tossing it aside.

淑女格蕾丝：当然，我还为你们准备了最后一份临别的礼物。
Ms. Grace: But before I go, consider this a parting gift from your captain, for old time's sake.

“轰——”
*boom*

一阵巨响从船舱的底部传来。
An explosion booms from the ship's depths.

她转过身来，朝着倾倒的众人款款鞠躬。
Grace gives an elegant bow.

淑女格蕾丝：再见了，朋友们，我由衷地感激你们——
Ms. Grace: Goodbye, my dear guests. From the bottom of my heart—

淑女格蕾丝：为这一段难忘的美好旅程。
Ms. Grace: Thank you all for this unforgettable journey.

舵手伊萨姆：——！
Helmsman Esam: ...!

“轰隆——”
*rumble*

舵手老查理：是动力室的方位！
Helmsman Charlie: That came from the engine room!

舵手老查理：那儿是……那些怪模怪样的铁皮水手负责管理的地方！
Helmsman Charlie: Those tin-headed bastards, they must have done something to it.

舵手伊萨姆：去甲板上看看，老查理！
Helmsman Esam: Go see what you can from the deck, Charlie!

老练的舵手们匆匆登上了甲板。
The seasoned helmsmen hurriedly make their way to the deck.

舵手老查理：糟了——！
Helmsman Charlie: Damn it all! They've blown a hole straight through the starboard hull!

“自由海风号”的右侧被炸了个大洞！

舵手们焦急地来回踱步，游轮乐手终于意识到了一个更严峻的问题。
While the helmsmen pace anxiously, Barcarola suddenly realizes the gravity of the situation.

芭卡洛儿：伊萨姆先生……您的意思是“自由海风号”就要沉没了吗？！
Barcarola: Gentlemen, you can't possibly be saying that the "Free Breeze" is going to sink?!

船舱的震动并未停下，反而愈发剧烈，像是战场中接连不断的火药爆炸与爆破声，又像是海神波塞冬排山倒海般的怒吼。
The ship's tremors again. It's as if they're on a battlefield.

舵手伊萨姆：该死的，咱们的救生艇也放在那附近！
Helmsman Esam: What's worse, that explosion came from over by the lifeboats!

舵手伊萨姆：重塑之手铁了心要干掉我们所有人！
Helmsman Esam: These bastards are hellbent on making sure we all end up at the bottom of the sea!

撕裂的海浪、金属钢板的嗡鸣与周遭人们的哭泣声一同从支离破碎的舷窗碎片间灌进了船舱。
The sound of tearing waves, humming steel plates, and crying guests pours into the cabin through shattered portholes.

漆黑一片的海洋中，目力所及之处，只有一片狂舞的墨色。
The pitch-black sea stretches as far as the eye can see, its surface alive with turbulent, inky swirls.

人们的心又一次随着船舱的倾角晃荡了起来。
There is another wave of panic as the ship tilts once again.

客人Ⅰ：救救我们，你们是“自由海风号”的负责人，你们承诺过的！
Guest I: Help us, Ms. Barcarola! You promised to keep us safe!

客人Ⅱ：还有你，女士！
Guest II: And you, Miss!

客人Ⅱ：你说过你们来自什么基金会，你们会保护好所有人的！
Guest II: Aren't you from the Foundation or whatever?! You said you'd protect us!

恐慌的客人们试图抓住每一根救命稻草。
The guests are desperately clinging to any chance of salvation.

维尔汀：请各位排好队，我的箱子能够暂时容纳一部分人员。
Vertin: Please line up, everyone. My suitcase should be able to temporarily shelter some passengers.

维尔汀：芭卡洛儿小姐，你知道船上的客人数目吗？
Vertin: Ms. Barcarola, do you know how many passengers are aboard?

经验丰富的乐手显然对“自由海风号”的数据了如指掌。
The musician clearly knows every detail about the "Free Breeze."

芭卡洛儿：1600余人，但现在可能有一半人都受伤了，他们没法迅速行动……
Barcarola: About 1600 in total. But I think many of them will be injured. I don't know how well they can move.

维尔汀：仅仅依靠我的箱子，来不及转移这么多人员……
Vertin: My suitcase alone won't be able to transfer that many people in time.

一旁握着通讯器的第一助手突然惊呼起来。
Suddenly, the communicator clutched in Sonetto's hand makes a sharp sound.

通讯器：“滴滴——滴滴——”
Communicator: Beep beep! Beep beep!

十四行诗：信号恢复了，司辰！
Sonetto: The signal's back, Timekeeper!

维尔汀：看来之前果然是重塑在捣乱……
Vertin: Just as we suspected, they were jamming our signal.

维尔汀：可是，他们是怎么知道我们的信号频段的呢？
Vertin: But how did they know our internal frequency?

冗杂的信息被甩出大脑，眼下有更紧要的事需要解决。
She quickly brushes this question aside. There are more urgent matters to attend to.

维尔汀：圣洛夫基金会，这里是维尔汀，收到请回答。
Vertin: This is Vertin. Please come in.

维尔汀：我们正位于“自由海风号”，坐标南纬55°35′，西经65°01′。
Vertin: We're currently aboard the cruise ship "Free Breeze," at coordinates 55.35°S, 65.01°W.

维尔汀：重塑之手炸毁了“自由海风号”的动力室，目前“自由海风号”正在下沉。
Vertin: The engine has been destroyed by Manus Vindictae, and the ship is taking on water fast.

维尔汀：船上乘客约有千余人。
Vertin: There are more than 1600 passengers aboard. But we won't be able to evacuate every passenger through my suitcase alone before the ship goes under.

仅仅依靠手提箱，我们无法在船只沉没之前疏散所有乘客……

维尔汀：重复，我们需要足够数量的救生艇援助。
Vertin: We're in need of immediate rescue.

通讯器：收到，我们将就近调遣相关救援人员。救援工作需要时间，在此之前，请各位积极自救，尽可能降低人员伤亡。
Communicator: Understood. We will dispatch rescue resources and personnel from the nearest branch as soon as possible. Before their arrival, please do everything possible to minimize casualties.

十四行诗：芭卡洛儿小姐，请告诉我广播室的位置，我还需要去援救另外两名同伴。
Sonetto: Ms. Barcarola, could you point me towards the radio room? I believe our friends may be in need of help.

芭卡洛儿：当然。
Barcarola: Of course.

橘发姑娘小跑着离开了。
Sonetto jogs away in the pointed direction.

船板的吱嘎声愈发剧烈，栏杆和索具在风中摆荡，发出一阵阵痛苦的呻吟。它窜入舷窗与冻得通红的耳中，把所有人的五官拧成可怖的一团。
The creaking of the ship's planks grows louder, and its railings and rigging groan painfully. Their sound carries on the freezing wind, and whips at the ears of the crowd.

冷冽的风令芭卡洛儿打了个激灵，她突然想起了什么。
Shivering from the cold, Barcarola remembers something.

芭卡洛儿：格蕾丝……她接管“自由海风号”的时间并不久，肯定不知道后备救生艇的位置，重塑没法毁掉它们！
Barcarola: Wait. Ms. Grace wasn't the captain for long. It's possible she didn't know about the ship's backup lifeboats. They might still be intact.

舵手伊萨姆：了不起，芭卡洛儿——！
Helmsman Esam: Good thinking, Ms. Barcarola!

舵手老查理：我就知道没人比你更了解这艘船！
Helmsman Charlie: You're a natural-born captain!

芭卡洛儿：——大家跟我来！
Barcarola: Everyone, follow me!

LEE-22 我不曾遗憾 / Without Regret

空旷的房间隐秘而晦暗，好似孕育着某种可怖的魂灵。
The room is cloaked in oppressive shadow, as if harboring a menacing spirit.

绅士靠近了略显狼狈的姑娘。
A gentleman emerges from the darkness.

勿忘我：你很好地完成了任务，使徒小姐。
Forget Me Not: You did well, Apostle.

他打量着形态各异的象形贝壳，努库泰澳人毕生的情感积淀在他的手中轻轻碰撞。
He examines the Spirit Shells, the lifelong emotions of the Nukutai lightly clinking in his hands.

勿忘我：很优异的材料。
Forget Me Not: These are splendid.

勿忘我：仪式倾泻的能量将得到一个最好的去处。
Forget Me Not: They will ensure the overflow of ritual energy will be properly contained.

勿忘我：坦白说，我一直很担心你能否行使自己的使命。
Forget Me Not: To be frank, I had my doubts about your capabilities.

勿忘我：你还太年轻，还没能积攒足够的经验，甚至不曾弄脏过自己的手。
Forget Me Not: You're still wet behind the ears, and you haven't yet gotten enough blood on those hands of yours.

扶着门框的使徒向钢琴前的身影款款鞠躬。
The apostle bows. Her pale hand is clinging to the doorframe.

淑女格蕾丝：为祂的……归来，献出一切。
Ms. Grace: I am willing to do anything for THEIR return.

勿忘我露出一个鼓励的微笑。
Forget Me Not offers her an encouraging smile.

勿忘我：但这一次，你做的很好。
Forget Me Not: Still, you surpassed my expectations.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

门框支撑着轻微摇晃的手，发出丝丝噪响。
Her hand is trembling.

勿忘我：你看上去很疲惫，小格蕾丝。
Forget Me Not: You look tired.

勿忘我：船上的颠簸日子肯定不太好受……放松些，你已经回家了。
Forget Me Not: Life at sea must have taken its toll on you. Relax now. You're home.

淑女格蕾丝：好的。
Ms. Grace: As you wish.

格蕾丝深吸一口气，将发颤的手指藏在身后。
She takes a deep breath and hides her trembling fingers behind her back.

勿忘我：在未来的计划里，你很重要。
Forget Me Not: You will play an important role in our upcoming plans.

勿忘我：好好休息吧。
Forget Me Not: Rest well, Apostle.

淑女格蕾丝：……是。
Ms. Grace: I will.

对方饶有兴趣地盯着格蕾丝，后者关门的手滞住了。
Grace's hand freezes as she goes to close the door. Her hesitation is evident.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

淑女格蕾丝：向您致意，勿忘我先生。
Ms. Grace: Thank you, Mr. Forget Me Not.

勿忘我：呵呵。
Forget Me Not: Heh heh.

门缓缓地闭合，勿忘我的轮廓逐渐模糊，他的笑容隐没在阴影里。
As she shuts the door, Forget Me Not's outline blurs, and his smile vanishes into the shadows.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

努力维持镇定的脚步朝着仅有的一阵微光缓步走去。
Steadying herself, Grace slowly moves toward the faint glimmer of light.

淑女格蕾丝：……
Ms. Grace: ...

风声跌跌撞撞地扑过走廊，令苍白的姑娘打了个寒颤。
The wind whipping through the corridor causes her to shiver.

淑女格蕾丝：——！
Ms. Grace: ...!

格蕾丝将脊背抵住门口，在一阵冰冷的触感中滑落在地。
She presses her back against the door and slides to the ground.

淑女格蕾丝：咳、咳咳……！
Ms. Grace: *cough*

她颤抖着爬进了一个最近的棺椁。
Trembling, she crawls into the nearest coffin.

本该为下一件收藏品准备的展柜。
A display case meant for the next specimen.

淑女格蕾丝：…………
Ms. Grace: ...

淑女格蕾丝：♪……
Ms. Grace: ♪ ...

淑女格蕾丝：♪……♫……
Ms. Grace: ♪ ... ♫ ...

芭卡洛儿：这儿的照明设施并不好，请大家牵紧彼此的手，跟着音乐的方向。
Barcarola: It's hard to see here. Please hold onto each other and follow the sound of my music.

感激的客人：芭卡洛儿小姐，您真了不起……您没有丢下我们，否则我们现在只能在船上等死了……
Grateful Guest: Thank you so much, Ms. Barcarola! If it weren't for you, we never would've survived!

感激的客人：我敬佩您的勇气。
Grateful Guest: You're so courageous!

忐忑的客人：可、那些救生筏的数量真的足够吗？
Antsy Guest: But what if there aren't enough lifeboats for everyone?

忐忑的客人：……如果我们之中一定会有人牺牲呢？
Antsy Guest: Will we have to leave anyone behind?

颤抖的疑问被海风吹散了。
The guest's shivering questions are scattered by the sea breeze.

人们打着冷颤，步履蹒跚地循着音乐缓缓前进。
They shudder and stumble as they follow the music.

四周黯淡无光，翻腾的云不再喧闹，鸥鸟与海浪的声音也隐没在人潮的呜咽里。
The sky is dark, but the churning clouds are no longer noisy. The cries of gulls and the crashing of waves merge with the weeping of the crowd.

脚步声在走廊与楼梯间穿行了许久，人们的表情扑朔迷离。
They make their way through corridors and staircases for what seems like an eternity, their faces steeped in shadow.

忐忑的客人：我不想就这样死去……我还有很多事没有完成……
Antsy Guest: I don't want to die like this. There are still so many things I want to do!

恍惚的客人：呜呜呜……哪怕“暴雨”真的改变了一切，我也希望能回到家乡看看……
Dismayed Guest: *sob* I want to go home. Even if the "Storm" changes everything, I just want to go ...

图图石子：请大家放心，努库泰澳人愿意让出救生艇的名额。
Fatutu: We have talked about it, and the Nukutai are willing to give up their spots if there aren't enough boats for everyone.

图图石子：……“自由海风号”发生的一切，对不起。
Fatutu: We want to make amends for what happened earlier.

芭卡洛儿：不——埃迪特先生，图图石子小姐。
Barcarola: Fatutu, this wasn't your people's fault.

芭卡洛儿：“自由海风号”不会放弃任何一位乘客，我决不会辱没她的名号。
Barcarola: The "Free Breeze" will not abandon any of its passengers.

芭卡洛儿：……
Barcarola: ...

她将背后的啪唧匣子举过了头顶，雪白的面庞涨得通红。
She raises her Crackling Box high, her face flushing red.

芭卡洛儿：这是“自由海风号”游轮乐手的保证。
Barcarola: You have my word as the official musical director, and I suppose, the acting captain.

图图石子：芭卡洛儿小姐，你在做什么——啪唧盒子不是你最引以为傲的……
Fatutu: Barcarola, what have you done to your Crackling Box?

芭卡洛儿：“*分解咔咔咒——！ ”
Barcarola: *Sinfonia gioiosa, dividetevi con grazia!

惊讶的客人：您居然抛下了这柄绞弦琴……芭卡洛儿小姐，我可是记着您当时花了多少工夫才找到它的……
Surprised Guest: Oh, Ms. Barcarola, not your zanfona! I remember you telling us how hard you worked to find it.

怀念的客人：天呐——离开加利西亚以后，我有多久没见着它了……
Reminiscing Guest: I haven't seen one of those since my time in Galicia.

感动的客人：它、它们变成了救生船……芭卡洛儿女士，您是我见过最伟大的游轮乐手……不、最伟大的音乐家！
Emotional Guest: You've turned them into boats! Ms. Barcarola, you're not just a great musician, you're a kind soul, too!

感动的客人：您拯救了更多的人……
Emotional Guest: You saved us!

LEE-23 海中升起的她 / Finding Home on the Waves

海水打湿了发梢，流苏边的花呢裙子在一阵接一阵翻涌的海潮中起伏，像是一片格外斑斓的浪花。
Seawater soaks the tips of her hair, the hem of her tweed skirt ripples among the waves.

这柄曾深藏在啪唧匣子里的小提琴与湿透的姑娘相互依偎，琴颈、琴身、尾杆相互嵌合……来自过去的小舟稳稳地托起了她。
The violin once hidden within the Crackling Box nestles against her, its neck, body, and tailpiece interlocking ... a small boat from the past buoying her steadily.

女孩终于惊觉了一件可怕的、被自己忽略已久的事实。
Barcarola realizes a terrifying truth, one she has long ignored.

芭卡洛儿：他们早就告诉过我的……
Barcarola: It's just like what Papà and Mamma said ...

？？？：“要为淘气的女儿制造一柄最特别的小提琴，
???: "Our cheeky little pumpkin's violin should have a rich and bright tone

它得有丰富深邃的音色，声音不能尖锐，当然也不能空洞或是不平衡。”
—not too sharp or unbalanced—just like her."

？？？：“我们得向比利先生要来云杉或者枫木，
???: "Let's ask Mr. Belli for some top-notch spruce or maple wood

嗯，克雷莫纳人最骄傲的那些好木头，它们的年轮紧密而均匀，让琴声能够更好地传导、共振……”
—the best that Cremona can offer!"

？？？：“琴颈与琴身的连接、漆面的处理……这些都不能落下……”
???: "We'll need some glue for the neck joint and plenty of varnish."

？？？：“这是克雷莫纳的小提琴，是我们的骄傲，到哪儿都能被认出来。”
???: "Of course. This is a Cremona violin we're talking about."

？？？：“最最重要的是，这是给芭卡洛儿的小提琴……”
???: "Most important of all, it will be a violin for our little Barcarola."

那些逐渐失真的模糊话语如在耳边，如在昨日。
The voices sound so close, as if they were spoken just yesterday.

芭卡洛儿：……我从没离开过那儿，是么？
Barcarola: As much as I try to deny it, I suppose my heart is still there with them.

一阵轻柔的风刮过了她，又像是一缕萦绕在心尖儿上的烟。
A gentle breeze blows as she finally recognizes that little wisp of smoke lingering in her heart.

怀中的小提琴被搂得更紧了，甚至在手腕与脚踝上勒出了一道道红印。
She clutches the violin even tighter.

芭卡洛儿：爸爸……妈妈……克雷莫纳……
Barcarola: Papà, Mamma, and Cremona.

一个氤氲着水汽与暖风的厚实怀抱无声无息地包裹了她。
A solid embrace, infused with the scent of rain and warmth, silently envelops her.

雨终于停了。
The rain has finally stopped.

船只与木质乐器半沉在水中，海平面渗出微弱的金色光芒。
The horizon shimmers faintly with a golden light once more.

维尔汀：……我们成功了。
Vertin: We did it.

乌尔里希：恭喜你，司辰。
Ulrich: Congratulations, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：那我是不是也应该恭喜你，乌尔里希组长？
Vertin: I should be the one congratulating you. Don't you think, Mr. "Fish Tank"?

玻璃缸中的液体努力凝成了一个V字。
The ferrofluid in the glass tank struggles to form a V.

维尔汀：所以这一切真的如此巧合……
Vertin: It's an odd twist of fate, isn't it?

乌尔里希：是的，我已经向科算中心汇报了这一结论，对“暴雨”的研究终于能够步入新的阶段了。
Ulrich: Indeed. I've just reported our findings to Laplace. With this, our research on the "Storm" can finally advance to a new stage.

乌尔里希：它甚至让我对摇滚乐有所改观了——！
Ulrich: I've even managed to develop a taste for rock 'n' roll.

乌尔里希：♪～♫～～
Ulrich: ♪ ... ♫ ...

十四行诗：说起“暴雨”……
Sonetto: Speaking of the "Storm" ...

十四行诗抬头望天，一抹微光映在她的脸上。
Sonetto looks up at the sky, the reflection of the light on the water glimmering on her face.

漫无边际的徜徉似乎迎来了尽头。
This unfortunate cruise has finally come to an end.

星锑：哇啊——天亮了！
Regulus: Hey, here comes the sun! Woo-hoo!

十四行诗：“暴雨”并没有到来……司辰，您是对的……
Sonetto: I never doubted you, Timekeeper. There was no "Storm," not this time anyway.

维尔汀：谢谢你一直以来的信任，十四行诗。
Vertin: Thank you for your continued trust, Sonetto.

海浪声似乎变得渺远，某些更清晰而炽热的声响飘进了耳朵。
The sound of the waves seems to fade away as it's replaced by a new melody.

星锑：太酷了，我决不能错过这样一场海上派对！
Regulus: Smashing! This is sure to be the most fabulous boat party ever held! I wouldn't miss it for the world!

熟悉的、陌生的、来自无数故乡的歌儿在这片海上亲切地交织着。
Familiar and foreign songs from countless lands intertwine as voices carry gently over the sea.

海盗扑腾着海水，朝着歌声的方向奋力划去。
Regulus paddles fiercely toward the music.

歌唱的人们：<啊，梦中家乡，那儿野牛流浪，羚羊与小鹿儿尽情嬉戏>
Singing Crowd: Oh, give me a home where the buffalo roam, where the deer and the antelope play.

歌唱的人们：<啊，抛下烦恼，抛下难过悲伤，乌云呀早散在天外远方>
Singing Crowd: Where seldom is heard a discouraging word, and the skies are not cloudy all day.

歌唱的人们：<我们围坐在树荫中 享欢乐时光美而长>
Singing Crowd: There we have spent many an hour, sitting in a joyful circle.

歌唱的人们：<歌儿嘹亮 它久久回响 在橡树梢上>
Singing Crowd: And we sang, the songs resounding in the oak grove.

歌唱的人们：<～顽皮月儿闪烁，遮起它双眸～>
Singing Crowd: By moonlight, little can be seen.

歌唱的人们：<～人们找寻羽毛，人们找寻火～>
Singing Crowd: They looked for the pen, they looked for the fire.

歌唱的人们：<如此陈旧的忧郁，归于灵魂，它们飘然而至，在这静谧的清晨～♫>
Singing Crowd: Melancholy of the past visits my soul this tranquil morn.

歌唱的人们：<我在门前目送，她飞回家中～♫>
Singing Crowd: When I go out to see her, she flies back to her home.

熟悉的歌谣从恍惚的姑娘口中脱口而出。
A familiar ballad leaves Barcarola's lips.

芭卡洛儿：<月落海面上 银星多明亮>
Barcarola: Silver stars shine upon the sea.

芭卡洛儿：<浪花儿徜徉 轻拂我脸庞>
Barcarola: Feel the gentle waves and warm breeze.

芭卡洛儿：<请随风儿来 同乘小船上>
Barcarola: Sail with me beneath the stars.

芭卡洛儿：<桑塔露琪亚 桑塔露琪亚>
Barcarola: Santa Lucia, Santa Lucia.

星锑：唱得不错，芭卡洛儿～
Regulus: You have a truly heavenly voice, Barcarola!

星锑：话说，这到底是哪儿的曲子……我怎么从来没听过？
Regulus: I've never heard that song before. Where's it from?

图图石子：它一定和芭卡洛儿小姐一样，也来自克雷莫纳！
Fatutu: Oh, I know! It must be from Cremona!

芭卡洛儿：才、才不是！
Barcarola: N-No! It's a Neapolitan song. It has nothing to do with Cremona!

这是那不勒斯的曲子，和克雷莫纳没有半点儿关系——！

十四行诗：……是基金会的直升机！
Sonetto: That's a Foundation helicopter!

维尔汀：那座岛是……
Vertin: That island ...
